indrapramatirucyate  BndP pṛthoḥ sutāyāṃ saṃbhūtaḥ putrastasyābhavadvasuḥ upamanyuḥ sutastasya yasyeme hyaupamanyavaḥ  BndP mitrāvaruṇayoścaiva kuṇḍineyāḥ pariśrutāḥ ekārṣeyāstathā cānye vasiṣṭhā nāma viśrutāḥ  BndP ete pakṣā vasiṣṭhānāṃ smṛtā hyekādaśaiva tu ityete brahmaṇaḥ putrā mānasā aṣṭa viśrutāḥ  BndP bhrātaraḥ sumahābhāgā yeṣāṃ vaṃśāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ trīṃllokāndhārayantīmāndevarṣigaṇasaṃkulān  BndP teṣāṃ putrāśca pautrāśca śataśo tha sahasraśaḥ vyāptā yestu trayo lokāḥ sūryasyeva gabhastibhiḥ  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīya upoddhātapāde ṛṣivaṃśavarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭamo dhyāyaḥ  ṛṣaya ūcuḥkathaṃ dvivārāvutpannā bhavānī prāksatī tu yā āsīddākṣāyaṇī pūrvamumā kathamajāyata  BndP menāyāṃ pitṛkanyāyāṃ janayañchailarāṭ svayam ke vai te pitaro nāma yeṣāṃ menā tu mānasī  BndP mainākaścaiva dohitro dauhitrī ca tathā hyumā ekaparṇā tathā caiva tathā caivaikapāṭalā  BndP gaṅgā cāpi saricchreṣṭhā sarvāsāṃ pūrvajā tathā sarvametatvayoddiṣṭaṃ nirdeśaṃ tasya no vada  BndP śrotumicchāmi bhadraṃ te śrāddhasya ca vidhiṃ param putrāśca ke smṛtāsteṣāṃ kathaṃ ca pitarastu te  BndP kathaṃ vā te samutpannāḥ kiṃnā mānaḥ kimātmakāḥ svarge vai pitaro hyete devānāmapi devatāḥ  BndP evaṃ veditumicchāmi pitṝṇāṃ sargamuttamamā yathā ca dattamasmābhiḥ sārddhaṃ prīṇāti vai pitṝn  BndP yadarthaṃ te na dṛśyante tatra kiṃ kāraṇaṃ smṛtam svarge tu ke ca varttante pitaro narake va ke  BndP abhisaṃbhāṣya pitaraṃ pituśca pitaraṃ tathā pratitāmahaṃ tathā caiva triṣu piṇḍeṣu nāmataḥ  BndP nāmnā dattāni śrāddhāni kathaṃ gacchanti vai pitṝn kathaṃ ca śaktāste dātuṃ narakasthāḥ phalaṃ punaḥ  BndP ke ca te pitaro nāma kānyajāmo vayaṃ punaḥ devā api pitṝn svarge yajantīti hi naḥ śrutam  BndP etadicchāmi vai śrotuṃ vistareṇa bahuśrutam spaṣṭābhidhāna mapi vai tadbhavānvaktumarhasi  BndP sūta uvācaatra vo kīrtayiṣyāmi yathāprajñaṃ yathāśrutam manvantareṣu jāyante pitaro devasūnavaḥ  BndP atītānāgatāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ kaniṣṭhāḥ kramaśastu vai devaiḥ sārddhaṃ purātītāḥ pitaro nyentareṣu vai  BndP vartante sāṃprataṃ ce tu tānvai pakṣyāmi niścayāt śrāddhakriyāṃ manuścaiṣāṃ śrāddhadevaḥ pravarttayet  BndP devānsṛjata brahmā māṃ yakṣyantīti ca prabhuḥ tamutsṛjya tadātmānamayajaṃste phalārthinaḥ  BndP te śaptā brahmaṇā mūḍhā naṣṭasaṃjñā bhaviṣyatha tasmātkiñcinna jānīta tato lokeṣu muhyata  BndP te bhūyaḥ praṇatāḥ sarve yācanti sma pitāmaham anugrahāya lokānāṃ punastānabravītprabhuḥ  BndP prāyaścittaṃ caradhvaṃ vai vyabhicāro hi vaḥ kṛtaḥ putrānsvānparipṛcchadhvaṃ tato jñānamavāpsyatha  BndP tatasta svasutāṃścaiva prayaścittaji ghṛkṣavaḥ pīvarī nāma viśrutā  BndP yoginī yogapatnī ca yogamātā tathaiva ca bhavitā dvāparaṃ prāpya aṣṭāviṃśatimeva tu  BndP śrīmānvyāso mahāyogī yogastasmindvijottamāḥ vyāsādaraṇyāṃ saṃbhūto vidhūma iva vai  BndP kanyāṃ kīrtimatīṃ caiva yoginīṃ yogamātaram brahmadattasya cananī mahiṣī tvaṇuhasya sā  BndP ādityakiraṇopetamapunarmārgamāsthitaḥ sarvavyāpī vinirmukto bhaviṣyati mahāmuniḥ  BndP traya ete sarvakāmasamṛddheṣu dvijāstānbhāvayantyuta eteṣāṃ mānasī kanyā yogotpattiritiśrutā  BndP dattā sanatkumāreṇa śukrasya mahiṣī tu yā ekaśṛṅgeti vikhyātā bhṛgūṇāṃ kīrtivarddhinī  BndP marīci garbhāste kanyā yaśodā nāma viśrutā matā yā jananī devī khaṭvāṅgasya mahātmanaḥ  BndP yajñe yasya purā gītā gāthāgītairmaharṣibhiḥ agnerjanma tadā dṛṣṭvā śāṇḍilyasya mahātmanaḥ  BndP yajamānaṃ dilīpaṃ ye hairaṇyagarbhasya sutāḥ śūdrāstāṃ bhāvayantyuta  BndP mānasā nāma te lokā vartante yatra te divi eteṣāṃ mānasī kanyā narmadā saritāṃ varā  BndP sā bhāvayati bhūtāni dakṣiṇāpathagāminī jananī gandhānsūtrapraṇayanaṃ tathā  BndP kāśeḥ punarbhavaiḥ kāryamaśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet kāśāḥ punarbhavā ye ca barhiṇo hyupabarhiṇaḥ  BndP ityete pitaro devā devāśca pitaraḥ punaḥ puṣpagandhavibhūṣāṇāmeṣa mantra udāhṛtaḥ  BndP āhṛtya dakṣiṇāgniṃ tu homārthaṃ vai prayatnataḥ anyārthe laukikaṃ vāpi juhuyātkarmasiddhaye  BndP antarvidhāya samidhastato dīpto vidhīyate samāhitena manasā praṇīyāgniṃ samantataḥ  BndP agnaye kavyavāhāya svadhā aṅgirase namaḥ somāya vai pitṛmate svadhā aṅgirase punaḥ  BndP yamāya vaivasvataye svadhānama iti dhruvam ityete homamantrāstu trayāṇāmanupūrvaśaḥ  BndP dakṣiṇenāgnaye nityaṃ somāyottaratastathā etayorantare nityaṃ juhuyādvai vivasvate  BndP upahāraḥ svadhākārastathaivollekhanaṃ ca yat homajapye namaskāraḥ prokṣaṇaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ  BndP bahuhavyendhane cāgnau susamiddhe tathaiva ca añjanābyañjanaṃ caiva piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ tathā  BndP aśvamedhaphalaṃ caitatsamiddhe yatkṛtaṃ dvijaiḥ kriyā sarvā yathoddiṣṭāḥ prayatnena samācaret  BndP bahuhavyendhane cāgnau susamiddhe viśeṣataḥ vidhūme lelihāne ca hotavyaṃ karmasiddhaye  BndP aprabuddhe samiddhe vā juhuyādyo hutāśane yajamāno bhave dandhaḥ so mutreti hi naḥ śrutam  BndP alpendhano vā rūkṣo gnirvasphuliṅgaśca sarvaśaḥ jvālādhūmāpasavyaśca sa tu vahnirasiddhaye  BndP durgandhaścaiva nīlaśca kṛṣṇaścaiva viśeṣataḥ bhūmiṃ vagāhate yatra tatra vidyātparābhavat  BndP arciṣmān piṇḍitaśikhaḥ sarppikāñjanasannibhaḥ snigdhaḥ pradakṣiṇaścaiva vahniḥ syātkāryasiddhaye  BndP naranārīgaṇebhyaśca pūjāṃ prāpnoti śāśvatīm akṣayaṃ pūjitāstena bhavanti pitaro gnayaḥ  BndP bilvoduṃbarapatrāṇi phalāni samidhastathā śrāddhe mahāpavitrāṇi medhyāni ca viśeṣataḥ  BndP pavitraṃ ca dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ śuddhaye janmakarmaṇām pātreṣu phalamuddiṣṭaṃ yanmayā śrāddhakarmaṇi  BndP tadeva kṛtsnaṃ vijñeyaṃ samitsu ca yathākramam kṛtvā samāhitaṃ cittamāgneyaṃ vai karomyaham  BndP anujñātaḥ kuruṣveti tathaiva dvijasattamaiḥ ghṛtamādāya pātre ca juhuyāddhavyavāhane  BndP palāśaplakṣanyagrodhaplakṣāśvatthavikaṅkatāḥ uduṃbarastathābilvaścandano yajñiyāśca ye  BndP saralo devadāruśca śālaśca kadirastathā samidarthe praśastāḥ syurete vṛkṣā viśeṣataḥ  BndP grāmyāḥ kaṇṭakinaścaiva yājñiyā ye ca kecana pūjitāḥ samidarthaṃ te pitṝṇāṃ vacanaṃ yathā  BndP samidbhiḥ ṣaṭphaleyābhirjuhuyādyo hutāśanam phalaṃ yatkarmaṇastasya tanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu  BndP akṣayaṃ sarvakāmīyamaśvamedhaphalaṃ hi tat śleṣmāntako naktamālaḥ kapitthaḥ śālmalistathā  BndP nīpo vibhītakaścaiva śrāddhakarmaṇi garhitāḥ cirabilvastathā kolastidukaḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi  BndP balvajaḥ kovidāraśca varjanīyāḥ samantataḥ śakunānāṃ nivāsāṃśca varjayeta mahīruhān  BndP anyāṃścaivaṃvidhānsarvānnayajñīyāṃśca varjayet svadheti caiva mantrāṇāṃ pitṝṇāṃ vacanaṃ yathā svāheti caiva devānāṃ yajñakarmaṇyudāhṛtam  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīyeupoddhātapāde śrāddhakalpe samidvarṇana nāmaikādaśo dhyāyaḥ  sūta uvācadevāścapitaraścaiva anyonyaṃ niyatāḥ smṛtāḥ ātharvaṇastveṣa vidhirityuvāca bṛhaspatiḥ  BndP pūjayeta pitṝnpūrvaṃ devāṃśca tadanantaram devā api pitṝnpūrvamarccayanti hi yatnataḥ  BndP dakṣasya duhitā nāmnā viśvā nāmeti viśrutā viśvākhyāstu sutāstasyāṃ dharmato jajñire daśa  BndP prakhyātā striṣu lokeṣu sarvalokanamaskṛtāḥ samastāste mahātmānaścerurugraṃ mahattapaḥ  BndP himavacchikhare ramye devarṣigaṇasevite śuddhena mansā prītā ūcustānpitarastadā  BndP varaṃ vṛṇīdhvaṃ prītāḥ sma kaṃ kāmaṃ kakhāmahe evamukte tu pitṛbhistadā trailokyabhāvanaḥ  BndP brahmovāca mahātejāstapasā taistu toṣitaḥ prīto smi tapasānena kaṃ kāmaṃ karavāṇi vaḥ  BndP evamuktāstadā viśve brahmaṇā viśvakarmaṇā ūcuste sahitāḥ sarve brahmāṇāṃ lokabhāvanam  BndP śrāddhe smākaṃ bhavedaṃśo hyeṣa naḥ kāṅkṣito varaḥ pratyuvāca tato brahmā tānvai tridaśapūjitaḥ  BndP bhaviṣyatyevamevaṃ tu kāṅkṣito vo varastu yaḥ pitṛbhiśca tathetyuktamevametanna saṃśayaḥ  BndP sahasmābhistu bhoktavyaṃ yatkiṃ ciddṛśyate tviha asmākaṃ kalpite śrāddhe yuṣmānaprāśanaṃ hi vai  BndP bhaviṣyati manuṣyeṣu satyame tadbruvāmahe mālyairgandhaistathānnena yuṣmānagre rccayiṣyati  agre dattvā tu yuṣmākamasmākaṃ dāsyate tataḥ visarjanamathāsmākaṃ pūrvaṃ paścāttu daivatam  BndP rakṣaṇaṃ caiva śrāddhasya ātithyasya vidhidvayam bhūtānāṃ devatānāṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ caiva karmaṇi  BndP evaṃ kṛte samyagetatsarvameva bhaviṣyati evaṃ dattvā varaṃ teṣāṃ brahmā pitṛgaṇaiḥ saha  BndP kṣamānugrahakṛddevaḥ saṃcakāra yathoditam vede pañca mahāyajñā narāṇāṃ samudāhṛtāḥ  BndP etānpañca mahāyajñānnirvapetsatataṃ naraḥ yatra sthāsyanti dātārastatsthānaṃ vai nibodhata  BndP nirbhayaṃ virajaskaṃ ca niḥśokaṃ nirvyathaklamam brāhmaṃ sthānamavāpnoti sarvalokapuraskṛtam  BndP śūdreṇāpi ca karttavyāḥ pañcaite mantravarjitāḥ ato nyathā tu yo bhuṅkte sa ṛṇaṃ nityamaśnute  BndP ṛṇaṃ bhuṅkte sa pāpātmā yaḥ pacedātmakāraṇāt tasmānnirvartayetpañca mahāyajñānsadā budhaḥ  BndP udakpūrve baliṃ kuryādudakānte tathaiva ca baliṃ suvihitaṃ kuryā duccairuccataraṃ kṣipet  BndP paraśṛṅgaṃ gavāṃ mūtraṃ baliṃ sūtraṃ samutkṣipet tannivedyo bhavetpiṇḍaḥ pitṝṇāṃ yastu jīvati  BndP iṣṭenānnena bhakṣyaiśca bhojayecca yathāvidhi nivedyaṃ kecidicchanti jīvantyapi hi yatnataḥ  BndP devadevā mahātmāno hyete pitara ityuta icchanti kecidācāryaḥ paścātpiṇḍanivedanam  BndP pūjanaṃ caiva vipraṇāṃ pūrvameveha nityaśaḥ taddhidharmārthakuśalo netyuvāca bṛhasmatiḥ  BndP pūrvaṃ nivedayetpiṇḍānpaścādviprāṃśca bhojayet yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ pitaro yoga saṃbhavāḥ  BndP somamāpyāyayantyete pitaro yogasaṃsthitāḥ tasmāddadyācchuciḥ piṇḍānyogebhyastatparāyaṇaḥ  BndP pitṝṇāṃ hi bhavedetatsākṣādiva hutaṃ haviḥ brahmaṇānāṃ sahasrasya yogasthaṃ grāsayedyadi  BndP yajamānaṃ ca bhoktṝṃś ca naurivāmbhasi tārayet asatāṃ pragraho yatra satāṃ caiva vimānatā  BndP daṇḍo daivakṛtastatra sadyaḥ patati dāruṇaḥ itvā mama sadharmāṇaṃ bāliśaṃ yastu bhojayet  BndP ādikarma samutsṛjya dātā tatra vinaśyati piṇḍamagnau sadā dadyadbhogārthī prathamaṃ naraḥ  BndP dadyātprajārthī yatnena madhyamaṃ mantrapūrvakam uttamāṃ kāntimanvicchangoṣu nityaṃ prayacchati  BndP prajñāṃ caiva yaśaḥ kīrttimapsu vai saṃprayacchati prārthayandīrghāmāyuśca vāyasebhyaḥ prayacchati  BndP sokumāryamathānvicchankukkuṭebhyaḥ prayacchati evametatsamuddiṣṭaṃ piṇḍanirvapaṇe phalam  BndP ākāśe gamayedvāpi apsu vā dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ pitṝṇāṃ sthānamākāśaṃ dakṣiṇā caiva digbhevet  BndP eke viprāḥ punaḥ prāhuḥ piṇḍoddharaṇamagrataḥ anujñātastu tairvipraiḥ kāmasuddhriyatāmit  BndP puṣpāṇāṃ ca phalānāṃ ca bhakṣyāṇāmannatastathā agramuddhṛtya sarveṣāṃ juhuyāddhavyavāhane  BndP bhaṅyamannaṃ tathā peyaṃ mūlāni ca phalāni ca hutvāgnau ca tataḥ piṇḍānnirvapeddakṣiṇā mukhaḥ  BndP vaivasvatāya somāya hutvā piṇḍānnivedya ca udakānnayanaṃ kṛtvā paścādviprāṃśca bhojayet  BndP anupūrvaṃ tato viprānbhakṣyairannaiśca śaktitaḥ snigdhairuṣṇaiḥ sugandhaiśca tarpayettānrasairapi  BndP ekāgraḥ paryupāsīnaḥ prayataḥ prāñjaliḥ sthitaḥ tatparaḥ śraddadhānaśca kāmānāpnoti mānavaḥ  BndP akṣudratvaṃ kṛtajñatvaṃ dākṣiṇyaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ vacaḥ tapo yajñāṃśca dānaṃ ca prayacchanti pitāmahāḥ  BndP ataḥ paraṃ vidhiṃ saumyaṃ bhuktavatsu dvijātiṣu ānupūrvyeṇa vihitaṃ tanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu  BndP prokṣya bhūmimathoddhṛtya pūrvaṃ pitṛparāyaṇaḥ tato nnivikiraṃ kuryādvidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā  BndP svadhā vācya tato viprān vidhivadbhūritakṣiṇān annaśeṣamanujñāpya satkṛtya dvijasattamān  BndP prāñjaliḥ prayataścaiva anugamya visarjayet  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīyeupoddhātapāde śrāddhakalpe dvādaśo dhyāyaḥ  bṛhaspatiruvācasakṛdabhyarcitāḥ prītā bhavanti pitaro vyayāḥ yogātmāno mahātmāno vipāpmāno mahaujasaḥ  BndP pretya ca svargalokāya kāmaiśca bahulaṃ bhuvi yeṣu vāpyanugṛhṇanti mokṣaprāptiḥ krameṇa tu  BndP tāni vakṣyāmyahaṃ saumya sarāṃsi saritastathā tīrthāni caiva puṇyāni deśāṃśchailāṃstathāśramān  BndP puṇyo hi triṣu lokeṣu sadaivāmarakaṇṭakaḥ parvatapravaraḥ puṇyaḥ siddhayāraṇasevitaḥ  BndP yatra varṣasahasrāṇi prayutānyarbudāni ca tapaḥ suduścaraṃ tepe bhagavānaṅgirāḥ purā  BndP yatra mṛtyorgatirnnāsti tathaivāsurarakṣasām na bhayaṃ naiva cālakṣmīryāvadbhūmirddhariṣyati  BndP tapasā tejasā tasya bhrajate sa nagottamaḥ śṛṅge mālyavato nityaṃ vahniḥ saṃvarttako yathā  BndP mṛdavastu sugandhāśca hemābhāḥ priyadarśanāḥ śāntāḥkuśā iti khyātāḥ paridakṣiṇanarmadām  BndP dṛṣṭavānsvargasopānaṃ bhagavānaṅgirāḥ purā agnihotre mahātejāḥ prastārārthaṃ kuśottamān  BndP teṣu darbheṣu yaḥ piṇḍānmarakaṇṭaṭakaparvate dadyātsakṛdapi prājñastasya vakṣyāmi yatphalam  BndP tadbhavatyakṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāṃ prītivardhanam antarddhānaṃ ca gacchanti kṣetramāsādya tatsadā  BndP tatra jvālāsaraḥ puṇyaṃ dṛśyate cāpi parvasu saśalyānāṃ ca sattvānāṃ viśalyakaraṇī nadī  BndP prāgdakṣiṇāyatāvarttā vāpī sā sunagottame kaliṅgadeśapaścārddhe śṛṅge mālyavato vibhoḥ  BndP siddhikṣetramṛṣiśreṣṭhā yaduktaṃ paramaṃ bhuvi saṃmataṃ devadaityānāṃ ślokaṃ cāpyuśanā jagau  BndP dhanyāste puruṣā loke ye prāpyāmarakaṇṭakam pitṝnsaṃtarpayiṣyantiśrāddhe pitṛparāyaṇāḥ  BndP alpena tapasā siddhiṃ gamiṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ sakṛdevārcitāstatra svargamāmarakaṇṭake  BndP mahendraḥparvataḥ puṇyo ramyaḥ śakraniṣevitaḥ tatrāruhya bhavetpūtaḥ śrāddhaṃ caiva mahāphalam  BndP vailāṭaśikhare yuktvā divyaṃ cakṣuḥ pravartate adhṛṣyaścaiva bhūtānāṃ devavaccarate mahīm  BndP saptagodāvare caiva gokarṇe ca tapovane aśvamedhaphalaṃ snātvā tatra dattvā bhavettataḥ  BndP dhūtapāpasthalaṃ prāpya pūtaḥ snātvā bhavennaraḥ rudrastatra tapastepe devadevo maheśvaraḥ  BndP gokarṇe nihitaṃ devair nāstikānāṃ nidarśanam abrāhmaṇasya sāvitrīṃ paṭhatastu praṇaśyati  BndP devarṣibhavane śṛṅge siddhacāraṇasevite āruhyataṃ niya mavāṃstato yāti triviṣṭapam  BndP divyaiścandanavṛkṣaiśca pādapairupaśobhitam āpaścandanasaṃyuktāḥ spandeti satataṃ tataḥ  BndP nadī pravartate tābhyastāmraparṇīti nāmataḥ yā candanamahākhaṇḍāddakṣiṇaṃ yāti sāgaram  BndP nadyāstasyāśca tāmrāyāstūhyamānā mahodadhau śaṅkhā bhavanti śuktyaśca jāyate yāsu mauktikam  BndP udakānayanaṃ kṛtvā śaṅkhamauktikasaṃyutam ādhibhirvyādhibhiścaiva muktā yāntyamarāvatīm  BndP candanebhyaḥ prasūtānāṃ śaṅkhānāṃ mauktikasya vā pāpakarttṝnapi pitṝṃstārayanti yathāśruti  BndP candratīrthe kumāryāṃ ca kāverīprabhave kṣaye śrīparvatasya tīrtheṣu vaikṛte ca tathā girau  BndP ekasthā yatra dṛśyante vṛkṣāhyauśīraparvate palāśāḥ khadirā bilvāḥ plakṣāśvatthavikaṅkatāḥ  BndP evaṃ dvimaṇḍalāviddhaṃ vijñeyaṃ dvijasattamāḥ asmiṃstyaktvā janoṃgāti kṣipraṃ yātyamarāvatīm  BndP śrīparvatasya tīrthe tu vaikṛte ca tathā girau karmāṇi tu prayuktā ni siddhyanti prabhavāpyaye  BndP duṣprayuktā hi pitṛṣu suprayogā bhavantyuta pitṝṇāṃ duhitā puṇyā narmadā saritāṃ varā  BndP yatra śrāddhāni dattāṃni hyakṣayāṇi bhavantyuta māṭharasya vane puṇye siddhacāraṇasevite  BndP antarddhānena gacchanti yuktvā tasminmahā girau vindhye caiva girau puṇye dharmādharmanidarśanīm  BndP dhārāṃ pāpā na paśyanti dhārāṃ paśyanti sādhavaḥ tatra taddṛśyate pāpaṃ keṣāṃ citpāpakarmaṇām  BndP kailāse yā mataṅgasya vāpī pāpaniṣūdanī snātvā tasyā divaṃ yānti kāmacārā vihaṅgamāḥ  BndP śaurpārake tathā tīrthe parvate pālamañjare pāṇḍukūpe samudrānte piṇḍārakataṭe tathā  BndP vimale ca vipāpe ca saṃkalpaṃ prāpya cākṣayam śrīvṛkṣe citrakūṭe ca jaṃbūmārge ca nityaśaḥ  BndP asitasya girau puṇye yogācāryasya dhīmataḥ tatrāpi śrāddhamānantyamasitāyāṃ ca nityaśaḥ  BndP puṣkareṣvakṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ tapaścaiva mahāphalamā mahodadhau prabhāse ca tadvadeva vinirdiśet  BndP devikāyāṃ vṛṣo nāma kūpaḥ siddhaniṣevitaḥ samutpatanti tasyāpo gavāṃ śabdena nityaśaḥ  BndP yogeśvaraiḥ sadā juṣṭaḥ sarvapāpabahiṣkṛtaḥ dadyācchrāddhaṃ tu yastasmiṃstasya vakṣyāmi yatphalam  BndP akṣayaṃ sarvakāmīyaṃ śrāddhaṃ prīṇāti vai pitṝn jātavedaḥ śilā tatra sākṣādagneḥ sanātanāt  BndP śrāddhāni cāgnikāryaṃ ca tatra kuryātsadā kṣayam yastvagniṃ praviśettatra nākapṛṣṭhe sa modate  BndP agniśāntaḥ punarjātastatra dattaṃ tato kṣayam daśāśvamedhike tīrthe tīrthe pañcāśvamedhike  BndP yathoddiṣṭaphalaṃ teṣāṃ kratūnāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ khyātaṃ hayaśiro nāma tīrthaṃ sadyo varapradam  BndP śrāddhaṃ tatra sadākṣayyaṃ dātā svarge ca modate śrāddhaṃ suṃdanisuṃde ca deyaṃ pāpaniṣū danam  BndP śrāddhaṃ tatrākṣayaṃ proktaṃ japahomatapāṃsi ca jatuṅge śubhe tīrthe tarpayetsatataṃ pitṝn  BndP dṛśyate parvasu cchāyā yatra nityaṃ divaukasām pṛthivyāmakṣayaṃ dattaṃ virajā yatra pādapaḥ  BndP yogeśvaraiḥ sadā juṣṭaḥ sarvapāpabahiṣkṛtaḥ dadyācchrāddhaṃ tu yastasmiṃstasya vakṣyāmi yatphalam  BndP arcitāstena vai sākṣādbhavanti pitaraḥ sadā asmiṃlloke vaśī ca syātpretya svarge mahī yate  BndP prāyaśo madravā puṇyā śivo nāma hradastathā tatra vyāsasaraḥ puṇyaṃ divyo brahmahradastathā  BndP ūrjjantaḥ parvataḥ puṇyo yatra yogeśvarālayaḥ atraiva cāśramaḥ puṇyo vasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ  BndP ṛgyajuḥ sāmaśirasaḥ kapotāḥ puṣpasāhvayāḥ ākhyāna pañcamā vedāḥ sṛṣṭā hyete svayaṃbhuvā  BndP gatvaitānmucyate pāpaddvijo vahniṃ samāśrayan śrāddhaṃ cānantyameteṣu japahomatapāṃsi ca  BndP puṇḍarīke mahātīrthe puṇḍarīkasamaṃ phalam brahmatīrthe mahāprājña sarvayajñasamaṃ phalam  BndP siṃdhusāgarasaṃbhede tathā pañcanade kṣayam virajāyāṃ tathā puṇyaṃ madravāyāṃ ca parvate  BndP deyaṃ saptanade śrāddhaṃ mānase vā viśeṣataḥ mahākūṭe hyanante ca girau trikakude tathā  BndP saṃdhyāyāṃ ca mahānadyāṃ dṛśyate mahādadbhutam aśraddadhānaṃ nābhyeti sā cābhyeti dhṛtavratam  BndP saṃśrayitvaikamekena sāyāhnaṃ prati nityaśaḥ tasmindeyaṃ sadā śrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāmakṣayārthinām  BndP kṛtātmā vākṛtātmā ca yatra vijñāyate naraḥ svargamārgapradaṃ nāma tīrthaṃ sadyo varapradam  BndP cīrāṇyutsṛjya yasmiṃstu divaṃ saptarṣayo gātāḥ adyāpi tāni dṛśyante cīrāṇyaṃbhogatāni tu  BndP snātvā svargamavāpnoti tasmiṃstīrthettame naraḥ khyātamāyatanaṃ tatra nandinaḥ siddhasevitam  BndP nandīśvarasya sā mūrttirnirācārairnadṛśyate dṛśyante kāñcanā yupāstvarciṣo bhāskarodaye  BndP kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ tāṃstu gacchantyānanditā divam sarvataśca kurukṣetraṃ sutīrthaṃ tu viśeṣataḥ  BndP puṇyaṃ sanatkumārasya yogeśasya mahātmanaḥ kīrtyate ca tilāndattvā pitṛbhyovai sadākṣayam  BndP uktamevākṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ dharmarājaniṣevitam śrāddhaṃ dattamamāvāsyāṃ vidhinā ca yathākramam  BndP puṃsaḥ sannihitāyāṃ tu kurūkṣetre viśeṣataḥ arcayitvā pitṝṃstatra sa putrastvanṛṇo bhavet  BndP sarasvatyāṃ vinaśane plakṣapraśravaṇe tathā vyāsatīrthe dṛṣadvatyāṃ triplakṣe ca viśeṣataḥ  BndP deyamoṅkārapavane śrāddhamakṣayamicchatā śakrāvatāre gaṅgāyāṃ maināke ca nagottame  BndP yamunāprabhave caiva sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate atyuṣṇāścātiśītāśca āpastasminnidarśanam  BndP yamasya bhaginī puṣyā mārttaṇḍaduhitā śubhā tatrākṣayaṃ sadā śrāddhaṃ pitṛbhiḥ pūrvakīrttitam  BndP brahmatuṇḍahrade snātvā saddayo bhavati brāhmaṇaḥ tasmiṃstu śrāddhamānantyaṃ japahomatapāṃsi ca  BndP sthāṇubhūto carattatra vasiṣṭo vai mahātapāḥ adyāpi tatra dṛśyante pādapā maṇibarhaṇāḥ  BndP tulā tu dṛśyate tatra dharmāndharmanidharśinī yathā vai tolitaṃ vipraistīrthānāṃ phalamuttamam  BndP pitṝṇāṃ duhitā yogā gandhakālīti viśrutā caturtho brahmaṇastvaṃśaḥ parāśarakulodbhavaḥ  BndP vyasiṣyati caturddhā vai vedaṃ dhīmānmahāmuniḥ mahāyogaṃ mahātmānaṃ yā vyāsaṃ janayiṣyati  BndP acchodakaṃ nāmasarastatrācchodāsamudbhavaḥ matsyayonau punarjātā niyogātkāraṇena tu  BndP tasyāstvādyāśrame puṇye puṇyakṛdbhirniṣevite dattaṃ sakṛdapi śrāddhamakṣayaṃ samudāhṛtam  BndP nadyāṃ yogasamādhānaṃ dattaṃ yugapadudbhavet kuberatuṅge pāpaghnaṃ vyāsatīrthetathaiva ca  BndP puṇyāyāṃ brahmaṇo vedyāṃ śrāddhamānantyamiṣyate siddhaistu sevitā nityaṃ dṛśyate tu kṛtātmabhiḥ  BndP anivartanaṃ tu nandāyāṃ vedyāḥ prāguttaradiśi siddhikṣetraṃ surairjuṣṭaṃ yatprāpya na nivarttate  BndP mahālaye padaṃ nyastaṃ mahādevena dhīmatā bhūtānāmanukaṃpārthaṃ nāstikānāṃ nidarśanam  BndP viraje tvakṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ pūrvameva mahālaye nandāyāṃ viraje caiva tathaiva ca mahālaye  BndP ātmānaṃ tārayantīha daśapūrvāndaśāparān kākahrade jātismaryaṃ suvarṇamamitaujasam  BndP kaumāraṃ ca saraḥ puṇyaṃ nāgabhogābhirakṣitam kumāratīrthe snātvā tu tridivaṃ yāti mānavaḥ  BndP devālaye tapastasvā ekapādena duścaram nirāhāro yugaṃ divyamumātuṅgo sthito jvalan  BndP umātuṅge bhṛgostuṅge brahmatuṅge mahālaye tatra śrāddhāni deyāni nityamakṣayamicchatā  BndP akṣayaṃ tu sadā śrāddhaṃ śālagrāme samantataḥ duṣkṛtaṃ dṛśyate tatra pratyakṣamakṛtātmanām  BndP pratyadeśo hyaśiṣṭānāṃ śiṣṭānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ tatra devahradaḥ puṇyo brahmaṇo nāgarāṭ śuciḥ  BndP piṇḍaṃ gṛhṇati hi satāṃ na gṛhṇātyasatāṃ sadā atipradīptairbhujagairbhoktumannaṃ na śakyate  BndP pratyakṣaṃ dṛśyate dharmastīrthayornatayordvayoḥ kāravatyāṃ ca śāṇḍilyāṃ guhāyāṃ vāmanasya ca  BndP gatvā caitāni pūtaḥsyācchradaddhamakṣayameva ca japo homastapo dhyānaṃ yatkiñcitsukṛtaṃ bhavet  BndP brahmacaryaṃ ca yau dhatte gurubhaktiṃ śataṃ samāḥ evamādyāssaricchreṣṭhā yatsnānādaghamokṣaṇam kumāradhārā tatraiva dṛṣṭā pāpaṃ praṇaśyati  BndP dhyānāsanaṃ tu tatraiva vyāsasyādyāpi dṛśyate śailaḥ kāntipurābhyāśe prāgudīcyāṃ diśi sthitaḥ  BndP puṇya puṣkariṇī tatra kirātagaṇarakṣitā yasyāṃ snātvā sakṛdvipraḥ kāmānāpnoti śāśvatān  BndP adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ devavaccarate mahīm  BndP kāśyapasya mahātīrthaṃ kālasarpiriti śrutam tatra śrāddhāni deyāni nityamakṣayamicchatā  BndP devadāruvane vāpi dhārāyāstu nidarśanam nirdhūtāni tu pāpāni dṛśyante sukṛtātmanām  BndP bhāgīrathyāṃ prayāge tu nityamakṣayamucyate kālañjare daśārṇāyāṃ naimiṣe kurujāṅgale  BndP vārāṇasyāṃ nagaryāṃ ca deyaṃ śrāddhaṃ prayatnataḥ tatra yogeśvaro nityaṃ tasyāṃ dattamathākṣayam  BndP gatvā caitāni pūrtaḥ syācchrāddhamakṣayyameva ca jabo homastathā dhyānaṃ yatkiñcitsukṛtaṃ bhavet  BndP lauhitye vaitaraṇyāṃ casvargavedyāṃ tathaiva ca sā tu devī samudrānte dṛśyate caiva nāmabhiḥ  BndP gayāyāṃ dharmavṛṣṭhe tu sarasi brahmaṇastathā gayāṃ gṛdhravaṭe caiva śrāddhaṃ dattaṃ mahāphalam  BndP himaṃ ca patate tatra samantātpañcayo janam bharatasyāśrame puṇye raṇyaṃ puṇyatamaṃ smṛtam  BndP mataṅgasya vanaṃ tatra dṛśyate sarvamānuṣaiḥ sthāpitaṃ dharmasarvasvaṃ lokasyāsya nidarśanam  BndP yaddaṇḍakavanaṃ puṇyaṃ puṇyakṛdbhirniṣevitam yasminprāhurviśalyeti tīrthaṃ sadyo nidarśanam  BndP tulāmānaistathā cāpi śāstraiśca vividhaistathā unmaccanti tathā lagna ye vai pāpakṛto janāḥ  BndP tṛtīyāyāṃ tathā pāde nirādhāyāṃ tu maṇḍale mahāhrade ca kauśikyāṃ dattaṃ śrāddhaṃ mahāphalam  BndP muṇḍapṛṣṭe padaṃ nyastaṃ mahādevena dhīmatā bahudevayugāṃstaptvā tapastīvraṃ sudaścaram  BndP alpenāpyatra kālena naro dharmaparāyaṇaḥ pāpmānamutsṛjatyāśu jīrṇāṃ tvacamivoragaḥ  BndP siddhānāṃ prītijananaṃ papānāṃ ca bhayaṅkaram lelihānairmahāghorai rakṣyate sumahoragaiḥ  BndP nāmnā kanakanandīti tīrthaṃ jagati viśrutam udīcyāṃ muṇḍapṛṣṭasya brahmarṣigaṇasevitam  BndP tatra snātvā divaṃyānti svaśarīreṇa mānavāḥ dattaṃ vāpi sadā śrāddhamakṣayyaṃ samudāhṛtam  BndP ṛṇaistribhistataḥ snātvā niṣkrīṇāti narastanum mānase sarasi snātvā śrāddhaṃnirvarttayettataḥ  BndP tīre tu sarasastasya devasyā yatanaṃ mahat āruhya tu japaṃstatra siddho yāti divaṃ tataḥ  BndP uttaraṃ mānasaṃ gatvāsiddhiṃ prāpnotyanuttamām snātvā tasminsaraśreṣṭhe dṛśyate mahādadbhutam  BndP divaścyutā mahābhāgā hyantarikṣe virājate gaṅgā tripathagā devī viṣṇupādāccyutā satī  BndP ākāśe dṛśyate tatra toraṇaṃ sūryasannibham jāṃbūnadamayaṃ puṇyaṃ svagadvāramivāyatam  BndP tataḥ pravarttate bhūyaḥ sarvasāgaramaṇḍikā pāvanī sarvabhūtānāṃ dharmajñānāṃ viśeṣataḥ  BndP candrabhāgā ca siddhuśca śubhe mānasasaṃbhave sāgaraṃ paścimaṃ yāto divyaḥ siṃdhunado varaḥ  BndP parvato himavānnāma nānādhātuvibhūṣitaḥ āyato vai sahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ bahuni tu  BndP siddhacāraṇasaṃkīrṇā devarṣigaṇasevitā tatra puṣkariṇī ramyā suṣumṇā nāma nāmataḥ  BndP daśavarṣasahasrāṇi tasyāṃ snātastu jīvati śrāddhaṃ bhavati cānantaṃ tatra dattaṃ mahodayam  BndP tārayecca sadā śrāddhe daśapūrvāndaśāparān sarvatra himavānpuṇyo gaṅgā puṇyā samantataḥ  BndP samudragāḥ samudrāśca sarve puṇyāḥ samantataḥ evamādiṣu cānyeṣu śrāddhaṃ nirvartayedbudhaḥ  BndP puto bhavati vai snātvā hutvā dattvā tathaiva ca śelasānuṣu śṛṅgeṣu kandareṣu guhāsu ca  BndP upahvaranitaṃbeṣu tathā prasravaṇeṣu ca pulineṣvāpagānāṃ ca tathaiva prabhaveṣu ca  BndP mahodadhau gavāṃ goṣṭe saṃgameṣu vaneṣu ca susaṃmṛṣṭopalipteṣu tdṛdyeṣu surabhiṣvatha  BndP gomayenopalipteṣu vivikteṣu gṛheṣu ca kuryācchrāddhamathaiteṣu nityameva yathāvidhi  BndP prāgdakṣiṇāṃ diśaṃ gatvā sarvakāmacikīrṣayā evameteṣu sarveṣu śrāddhaṃ kuryādatandritaḥ  BndP eteṣveva tu medhāvī brāhmīṃ siddhimavāpnuyāt traivarṇavihitaiḥ sthāne dharme varṇāśrame rataiḥ  BndP kaupasthānaṃ ca saṃtyāgātprāpyate pitṛpūjanam tīrthānyanusaranvīraḥ śraddadhānaḥ samāhitaḥ  BndP kṛtapāpo pi śudhyeta kiṃ punaḥ śubhakarmakṛt tiryagyoniṃ na gacchecca kudeśe ca na jāyate  BndP svargī bhavati vipro vai mokṣopāyaṃ ca vindati aśraddadhānaḥ pāpāyurnāstiko cchinnasaṃśayaḥ  BndP hetuniṣṭhaśca pañcaite na tīrthe phalabhāginaḥ gurutīrthe parā siddhistīrthānāṃ paramaṃ padam  BndP dhyānaṃ tīrthaṃ paraṃ tasmādbrahmatīrthaṃ sanātanam upavāsātparaṃ dhyānamindriyāṇāṃ nivarttanam  BndP upavāsanibaddhairhi prāṇaireva punaḥ punaḥ prāṇāpānau vaśe kṛtvā vaśagānīndiyāṇi ca  BndP buddhiṃ manasi saṃyamya sarveṣāṃ tu nivarttanam pratyāhāraṃ kṛtaṃ viddhi mokṣopāyamasaṃśayam  BndP indriyāṇāṃ mano ghoraṃ buddhyādīnāṃ vivarttanam anā hāro kṣayaṃ yāti vidyādanaśanaṃ tapaḥ  BndP nigrahe buddhimansoranyabuddhirna jāyate kṣīṇeṣu sarvadoṣeṣu kṣīṇeṣvevendriyeṣu ca  BndP parinirvāti śuddhātmā yathā vahniranidhanaḥ kāraṇebhyo guṇebhyaśca vyaktāvyaktācca kutsnaśaḥ  BndP niyojayati kṣetrajñaṃ tebhyoyogena yogavit tasya nāsti gatiḥ sthānaṃ vyaktāvyakte ca sarvaśaḥ na sannāsanna sadasannaiva kiñcidavasthitaḥ  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīya upoddhātapāde śrāddhakalpe puṇyadeśānukīrttanaṃ nāma trayodaśo dhyāyaḥ  bṛhaspatiruvācaataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvadānaphalāni ca śrāddhakarmaṇi medhyāni varjanīyāni yāni ca  BndP himaprapatane kuryādā haredvā himaṃ tataḥ agnihotramupāyuṣyaṃ pavitraṃ paramaṃ hitam  BndP naktaṃ tu varjayecchrāddhaṃ rāhoranyatra darśanāt sarvasvenāpi karttavyaṅkṣipraṃ vai rāhudarśane  BndP uparāge na kuryādyaḥ paṅke gauriva sīdati kurvāṇastattaretpāpaṃ satī nauriva sāgare  BndP vaiśvadevaṃ ca saumyaṃ ca khaḍgamāṃsaṃ paraṃ haviḥ viṣāṇavarjaṃ khaḍgasya mātsaryānnāśayāmahe  BndP tvāṣṭrā vai yajamānena deveśena mahātmanā pibañchacīpatiḥ somaṃ pṛthivyāṃ madhyagaḥ purā  BndP śyāmākāstatra utpannāḥ pitrarthamaparajitāḥ vipruṣastasya nāsābhyāmāsaktābhyāṃ tathekṣavaḥ  BndP śreṣmalāḥ śītalāḥ snigdhā madhurāśca tathekṣavaḥ śyāmākairikṣubhiścaiva pitṝṇāṃ sarvakāmikam  BndP kuryādāgrayaṇaṃ yastu sa śīghraṃ siddhimāpnuyāt śyāmākāstu dvināmāno vihitā yajanesmṛte  BndP yasmāttedevasṛṣṭāstu tasmātte cākṣayāḥ smṛtāḥ prasātikāḥ priyaṅguśca mudgāśca haritāstathā  BndP etānyapi samānāni śyāmākānāṃ guṇaistu taiḥ kṛṣṇamāṣāstilāścaiva śreṣṭhāstu yavaśālayaḥ  BndP mahāyavāśca niṣpāvāstathaiva ca madhūlikāḥ kṛṣṇāścaivānnalohāśca garhyāḥ syuḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi  BndP rājamāṣāstathānye vai varjanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ masūrāścaiva puṇyāśca kusuṃbhaṃ śrīniketanam  BndP varṣāsvatiyavā nityaṃ tathā vṛṣakavāsakau bilvāmalakamṛdvīkāpanasāmrātadāḍimāḥ  BndP tavaśolaṃyatākṣaudrakharjūrāmralāni ca khaśerukovidāryaśca tālakandaṃ tathā visam  BndP tamālaṃ śatakandaṃ ca madvasūcāntakāndikī kāleyaṃ kālaśākaṃ ca bhūripūrṇā suvarcalā  BndP māṃsākṣaṃ duviśākaṃ ca bubucetā kurastathā kaphālakaṃ kaṇā drākṣā lakucaṃ cocameva ca  BndP alābuṃ grīvakaṃ vīraṃ karkandhūmadhusāhvayam vaikaṅkataṃ nālikeraśṛṅgaja pakarūṣakam  BndP pippalī maricaṃ caiva paṭholaṃ bṛhatīphalam sugandhamāṃsapīvanti kaṣāyāḥ sarva eva ca  BndP evamādīni cānyāni varāṇi madhurāṇi ca nāgaraṃ cātra vai deyaṃ dīrghamūlakamava ca  BndP vaṃśaḥ karīraḥ surasaḥ sarjakaṃ bhūstṛṇāni ca varjanīyāni vakṣyāmi śrāddhakarmaṇi nityaśaḥ  BndP laśunaṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva tathā vai palvalodakam karaṃbhādyāni cānyāni hīnāni rasagandhataḥ  BndP śrāddhakarmaṇi varjyāni kāraṇaṃ cātra vakṣyate purā devāsure yuddhe nirjitasya baleḥ suraiḥ  BndP śaraistu vikṣatādaṅgātpatitā raktabindavaḥ tata etāni jātāni laśunādīni sarvaśaḥ  BndP tathaiva raktaniryāsā lavaṇānyauṣaraṇi ca śraddhakarmaṇi varjyāni yāśca nāryo rajasvalāḥ  BndP durgandhaṃ phenilaṃ caiva tathā vai palvalodakam labhedyatra na gaustṛptiṃ naktaṃ yaccaiva guhyate  BndP āvikaṃ mārgamauṣṭraṃ ca sarvamekaśaphaṃ ca yat māhiṣaṃ cāmaraṃ caiva payo varjyaṃ vijānatā  BndP ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi varjyāndeśānprayatnataḥ na draṣṭavyaṃ ca yaiḥ śrāddhaṃ śaucāśaucaṃ ca kṛtsnaśaḥ  BndP vanyamūlaphalairbhakṣyaiḥ śrāddhaṃ kuryāttu śraddhayā rājaniṣṭhāmavāpnoti svargamakṣayameva ca  BndP aniṣṭaśabdāṃ saṃkīrṇāṃ jantupyāptāmathāvilām pūtigandhāṃ tathā bhūmiṃ varjayecchrāddhakarmaṇi  BndP nadyaḥ sāgaraparyantā dvāraṃ dakṣiṇapūrvataḥ triśaṅkorvarjayeddeśaṃ sarvaṃ dvādaśa yojanam  BndP uttareṇa mahānadyā dakṣiṇena ca vaikaṭam deśāstriśaṅkavo nāma varjyā vai śrāddhakarmaṇi  BndP kāraskarāḥ kaliṅgaśca sidhoruttarameva ca pranaṣṭāśramadharmāśca varjyā deśāḥ prayatnataḥ  BndP nagnādayo na paśyeyuḥ śrāddhakarma vyavasthitam gacchantyetaistu dṛṣṭāni na pitṝṃśca pitāmahāṃna  BndP śaṃyuruvācanagnādīnbhagavansamyagācakṣva paripṛcchataḥ bṛhaspatiruvācasarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ trayīsaṃvaraṇaṃ smṛtam  BndP tāṃ ye tyajanti saṃmohātte vai nagnādayo janāḥ pralīyate vṛṣo yasminnirālaṃbaśca yo bṛṣe  BndP vṛṣaṃ yastu parityajya mokṣamanyatra mārgati vṛṣo vedāśramastasminyo vai samyaṅna paśyati  BndP brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyo vṛṣalaḥ sa na saṃśayaḥ purā devāsure yuddhe nirjitairasuraistathā  BndP pāśaṇḍā vai kṛtāstāta teṣāṃ sṛṣṭiḥ prajāyate vṛddhaśrāvakinirgranthāḥ śākyā jīvakakārpaṭāḥ  BndP ye dharmaṃ nānuvarttante te vai nagnādayo janāḥ vṛthā jaṭī vṛthā muṇḍī vṛthā nagnaśca yo dvijaḥ  BndP vṛthā vratī vṛthā jāpī te vai nagnādayo janāḥ kuladharmātigāḥ śaśvadvṛthā vṛttikalatrakāḥ  BndP kṛtakarmadiśastvete kupathāḥ parikīrttitāḥ etairhi dattaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ vai śrāddhaṃ gacchati dānavān  BndP brahmaghnaśca kṛtaghnaśca nāstiko gurutalpagaḥ dasyuścaiva nṛśaṃsaśca darṇane tānvisarjayet  BndP patitāḥ krūrakarmāṇaḥ sarvāṃstānparivarjayet devatānāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca vivāde pravadanti ye  BndP devāṃśca brāhmaṇāṃścaiva āmnāyaṃ yastu nindati asurānyātudhānāṃśca dṛṣṭamebhirvrajatyuta  BndP brāhmaṃ kṛtayugaṃ proktaṃ tretā tu kṣatrriyaṃ yugam vaiśyaṃ dvāparamityāhuḥ śūdraṃ kaliyugaṃ smṛtam  BndP kṛte pūjyanta pitarastretāyāṃ tu surāstathā yuddhāni dvāpare nityaṃ pākhaṇḍāśca kalau yuge  BndP apamānāpaviddhaśca kukkuṭo grāmasūkaraḥ śvā caiva hanti śrāddhāni darśanādeva sarvaśaḥ  BndP śvasūkaropa saṃsṛṣṭaṃ dīrgharogibhireva ca patitairmalinaiścaiva na draṣṭavyaṃ kathañcana  BndP annaṃ paśyeyurete yattannārhaṃ havyakavyayoḥ utsraṣṭavyāḥ pradhā nārthaiḥ saṃskārastvāpado bhavet  BndP haviṣāṃ saṃhatānāṃ ca pūrvameva vivarjayet sṛṣṭaṃ yuktābhiradbhiśca prokṣaṇaṃ ca vidhīyate  BndP siddhārthakaiḥ kṛṣṇatilaiḥ kāryaṃ vāpyapavāraṇam gurusūryāgnivāsrāṇāṃ darśanaṃ vāpi yatnataḥ  BndP āsanārūḍhamannādyaṃ pādopahatameva ca amedhyairjaṅgamairdṛṣṭaṃ śuṣkaṃ paryuṣitaṃ ca yat  BndP  BndP pādau prakṣālya hastau ca antarjānu tvapaḥ spṛśet prasannastriḥ pibedvāri prayataḥ susamāhitaḥ  BndP dvireva mārjanaṃ kuryātsakṛdabhyukṣaṇaṃ tataḥ khāni mūrddhānamātmānaṃ hastau pādau tathaiva BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīya upoddhātapāde śrāddhakalpe śaucavidhirnāma caturdaśo dhyoyaḥ  ṛṣaya ūcuḥaho dhanyastvayā sūta śrāddhakalpaḥ prakīrtitaḥ śrutā naḥ BndP akliṣṭa mavraṇaṃ yuktaṃ kṛśavṛttimayācakam ekāntaśīlaṃ dhīmantaṃ sadā śrāddheṣu bhojayet  BndP no dadāmi tamityevaṃ brūyādyo vai durātmavān api jātiśataṃ gatvā na sa mucyeta kilbiṣāt  BndP BndP vaktā vedaphalādbhraśyeddātā dānaphalāttathā bhṛtako dhyāpayedyastu bhṛtakādhyāpitastu yaḥ  BndP nārhatastāvapi śrāddhe brahmāṇaḥ krayavikrayī krayaśca vikrayaścaivājīvitārthe vigarhitau  BndP sthitā nityaṃ jñānino dhyāninastathā devabhaktā mahātmānaḥ punīyurdarśanādapi  BndP śikhibhyo dhāturaktebhyastridaṇḍebhyaḥ pradāpayet sarvaṃ yogeśvarairvyāptaṃ trailokyaṃ hi nirantaram  BndP tasmātpaśyanti te sarvaṃ yatkiñcijjagatīgatam vyaktāvyaktaṃ vaśe kṛtvā sarvasyāpi ca yatparam  BndP satyāsatyaṃ ca yaddṛṣṭaṃ sada sacca mahātmabhiḥ sarvajñānāni sṛṣṭāni mokṣādīnimahātmabhiḥ  BndP tasmātteṣāṃ sadā bhaktaḥ phalaṃ prāpnoti vottamam  BndP ṛcaśca yo veda sa veda vedānyajūṃṣi yo veda yajñam sāmāni yo veda sa veda brahma yo mānasaṃ veda sa veda sarvam  BndP iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīya upoddhātapāde śrāddhakalpe brāhmaṇaparīkṣā nāma pañcadaśo dhyāyaḥ  bṛhaspatiruvācaataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dānāni ca phalāni ca tāraṇaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ svargamārgasukhāvaham  BndP loke śreṣṭhatam sarvamātmanaścaiva yatpriyam sarvaṃ pitṝṇāṃ dātavyaṃ teṣāmevājñayārthinā  BndP jāṃbūnadamayaṃ divyaṃ vimānaṃ sūryasannibham divyāpsarobhiḥ saṃpūrṇamannado brahmadānasya tatphalam  BndP plutaṃ vipreṣu yo dadyācchrāddhakāle kamaḍalum madhukṣīrājyadadhibhirdātāramupatiṣṭhate  BndP cakrāviddhaṃ ca yo dadyācchrāddhakāle kamaṇḍalum dhenuṃ salabhate divyāṃ prayutānyarbudāni ca  BndP sumahadvyomagaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvakāmasamanvitam candrasūryanibhaṃ divyaṃ vimānaṃ labhate kṣayam  BndP apsarobhiḥ parivṛtaṃ kāmagaṃ sumanojavam vasetsa tu vimānāgre stūyamānaḥ samantataḥ  BndP divyaiḥpuṣpaiścitaścāhurdānānāṃ paramaṃ budhāḥ suślakṣmāni suvarṇāni śrāddhe pātrāṇi dāpayet  BndP rasāstamupatiṣṭhanti bhakṣyaṃ saubhāgyameva ca tilānikṣūṃstathā śrāddhe dvijebhyaḥ saṃprayacchati  BndP mitrāṇi labhate loke strīṣu saubhāgyameva ca yaḥ pātraṃ taijasaṃ dadyānmanojña śrāddhabhojanaiḥ  BndP pātraṃ bhavati kāmānā rūpasya ca dhanasya ca rājataṃ kāñcanaṃ vāpi yo BndP vastrābhāve kriyā nāsti yadānatapāṃsi ca tasmādvastrāṇi deyāni śrāddhakāle tu nityaśaḥ  BndP tāni sarvāṇyavāpnoti śrāddhe dattvā tu mānavaḥ nityaśrāddhe tu yo dadyātprayatastatparāyaṇaḥ  BndP sarvakāmānavāpnoti rājyaṃ svage tathava ca sarvakāmasamṛddhasya yajñasya phalamaśnute  BndP bhakṣyajātaṃ tu sukṛtaṃ svastikādyaṃ saśarkaram kṛsara madhusarpiśca payaḥ pāyasameva ca  BndP snigdhaprāyāśca yo dadyādagniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet dadhigavyamasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ bhakṣyānnānāvidhāṃstathā  BndP dattvā na śocate śrāddhe varṣāsu ca maghāsu ca ghṛtena bhojayedviprānghṛtaṃ bhūmau samutsṛjot  BndP chāyāyāṃ hastinaścaiva dattvā śrāddhena śocate odanaṃ pāyasaṃ sarpirmadhumūlaphalāni ca  BndP bhakṣyāṃśca vividhāndattvā paratreha ca modate śarkarākṣīrasaṃyuktāḥ pṛthukā nityamakṣayāḥ  BndP syāttu navasasyāniyo dadyācchrāddhe satkṛtya yatnataḥ sarvabhogānavāpnoti pūjyate ca divaṃ gataḥ  BndP bhakṣyabhojyāni peyāni coṣyaleṅyavarāṇi ca bhojanāgrāsanaṃ dattvā atithibhyaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ  BndP BndP kṣetrabhāgī bhavetputrī śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā punarvasau puṣṭikāmaḥ punastiṣye śrāddhaṃ kurvīta mānavaḥ  BndP āśleṣāsu pitṝnarcanvīrānputrānavāpnuyāt jātīnāṃ bhavati śreṣṭho maghāsu śrāddhamācaran  BndP BndP na brāhmaṇaṃ parikṣeta sadā deyaṃ hi mānavaiḥ daivekarmaṇi pitrye ca śrūyate vai parīkṣaṇam  BndP sarvavedavratasnātāḥ paṅktīnāṃ pāvanā dvijāḥ ye ca bhāṣāvidaḥ kecidye ca vyākaraṇe ratāḥ  BndP adhīyate purāṇaṃ vai dharmaśāstramathāpi ca triṇāciketaḥ pañcāgniḥ sa sauparṇaḥ ṣaḍaṅgavit  BndP brahmadevasutaścaiva cchandogo jyeṣṭhasāmagaḥ puṇyeṣu yaśca tīrtheṣu kṛtasnānaḥ kṛtavrataḥ  BndP makheṣu ye ca sarveṣu bhavantyavabhṛthāplutāḥ ye ca satyavratā nityaṃ svadharmaniratāśca ye  BndP akrodhanā lobhaparāstāñchrāddheṣu nimantrayet etebhyo dattamakṣayyamete vai paṅktipāvanāḥ  BndP śrāddhīyā brahmaṇā ye tu yogavratasuniṣṭhitāḥ trayo pi pūjitāstena brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ  BndP pitṛbhiḥ saha lokāśca yo hyetānpūjayennaraḥ pavitrāṇāṃ pavitraṃ ca maṅgalānāṃ ca maṅgalam  BndP prathamaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ yogadharmo nigadyate apāṅkteyānpravakṣyami gadato me nibodhata  BndP kitavo madyapo yaśca paśupālo nirākṛtaḥ grāmapreṣyo vārdhuṣiko hyāpaṇo vaṇijastathā  BndP agāra dāhī garado vṛṣalo grāmayājakaḥ kāṇḍapṛṣṭho tha kuṇḍāśī madhupaḥ somavikrayī  BndP samudrāntarito bhṛtyaḥ piśunaḥ kūṭasākṣikaḥ pitrā vivadamānaśca yasya copapatirgṛhe  BndP abhiśastastathā stenaḥ śilpaṃ yaścopajīvati stavakaḥ sūpakāraśca yaśca mitrāṇi nindati  BndP kāṇaśca khañjakaścaiva nāstiko vedavarjitaḥ unmatto pyatha ṣaṇḍhaśca bhrūṇahā gurutalpagaḥ  BndP bhiṣagjīvī prāśanikaḥ parastrīṃ yaśca sevate vikrīṇāti ca yo brahmavratāni niyamāṃstathā  BndP naṣṭaṃ syānnāstike dattaṃ vrataghne cāpavarjitam yaccavāṇijake dattaṃ neha nāmutra saṃbhavet  BndP nikṣepahārake caiva kṛtaghne vidavarjite tathā pāṇavike vai ca kāruke dharmavarjite  BndP krīṇāti yo hyapaṇyāni vikrīṇāti praśaṃsati anyatrāsya samādhānaṃ na vaṇikūchrāddhamarhati  BndP bhasmanīva hutaṃ havyaṃ dattaṃ paunarbhave dvijaḥ ṣaṣṭiṃ kāṇaḥ śataṃ ṣaṇḍhaḥ śvitrī pañcaśatānyapi  BndP pāparogī sahasraṃ vai dāturnāśayate phalam bhraśyeddhi sa phalāttasmātpradātā yastu bāliśaḥ  BndP yadviṣṭitaśirā bhuṅkte yadbhuṅkte dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ sopānatkaśca yadbhuṅkte yacca dattamasatkṛtam  BndP sarvaṃ tadasuredrāya brahmā bhāgamakalpayat śvā caiva brahmahā caiva nāvekṣeta kathañcana  BndP tasmātparivṛtairdadyāttilaiścānnaṃ vikīrya ca rākṣasānāṃ tilāḥ proktāḥ śunāṃ parivṛtāstathā  BndP darśanātsūkaro hanti pakṣavātena kukkuṭaḥ rajasvalāyāḥ sparśena kruddhoyaśca prayacchati  BndP nadītīreṣu ramyeṣu saritsu ca sarassu ca vivikteṣu ca prīyante datteneha pitāmahāḥ  BndP nāsavyaṃpātayejjānu na yukto vācamīrayet tasmātparivṛteneha vidhivaddarbhapāṇinā  BndP pitrorārādhanaṃ kāryamevaṃ prīṇayate pitṝn anumānya dvijānpūrvamargauṃ kuryādyathāvidhi  BndP pitṝṇāṃ nirvapedbhūmau sūrye vā darbhasaṃstare śuklapakṣe ca pūrvāṅṇe śrāddhaṃ kuryādyathāvidhi  BndP kṛṣṇapakṣe paraṅṇe tu rauhiṇaṃ vai na laṅghayet evamete mahātmāno mahāyogā mahaujasaḥ  BndP sadā vai pitaraḥ pūjyāḥ saṃ prāptau deśakālayoḥ pitṛbhaktyaiva tu naro yogaṃ prāpnoti durllabham  BndP dhyānena mokṣaṃ gaccheddhi hitvā karma śubhāśubham yajñahetostaduddhṛtya mohayitvā jagattathā  BndP guhāyāṃ nihitaṃ brahma kaśyapena mahātmanā amṛtaṃ guhyamuddhṛtya yoge yogavidāṃ varāḥ  BndP proktaḥ sanatkumāreṇa mahāto brahmaṇaḥ padam devānāṃ paramaṃ guhyamṛṣīṇāṃ ca parāyaṇam  BndP pitṛbhaktyā prayatnena prāpya te tanmanīṣibhiḥ pitṛbhaktaḥ samāsena pitṛpūrvaparaśca yaḥ  BndP ayatnātprāpnuyādeva sarvametanna saṃśayaḥ  BndP bṛhaspatiruvācayasmaiśrāddhāni deyāni yacca dattaṃ mahatphalam yeṣu cāpyakṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ tīrtheṣu ca guhāsu ca  BndP yeṣu svargamavāpnoti tatte proktaṃ sasaṃgraham śrutvemaṃ śrāddhakalpaṃ ca na kuryādyastu mānavaḥ  BndP sa majjennarake ghore nāstikastamasāvṛte parivādo na karttavyo yogināṃ tu viśeṣataḥ  BndP parivādātkrimirbhūtvā tatraiva parivarttate yogānparivadedyastu dhyānino mokṣakāṅkṣiṇaḥ  BndP sa gacchennarakaṃ ghoraṃ śrotāpyasya na saṃśayaḥ āvṛtaṃ tamasaḥ sarvaṃ narakaṃ ghoradarśanam yogīśvaraparīvādānna svargaṃ yāti mānavaḥ  BndP yogeśvarāṇāmā krośaṃ śṛṇuyādyo yatātmanām sahi kālaṃ ciraṃ majjennarake nātra saṃśayaḥ kuṃbhīpākeṣu pacyante jihvācchede punaḥ punaḥ  BndP samudre ca yathā loṣaṭastadbatsīdanti te narāḥ manasā karmaṇā vācā dveṣaṃ yogeṣu varjayet protyānantaṃ phalaṃ bhuṅkta iha vāpi na saṃśayaḥ  BndP na pārago vindati paramātmanastrilokamadhye carati svakarmamiḥ ṛco yajuḥ sāma tadaṅgapārage vikārametaṃ hyanavāpya sīdati  BndP vikārapāraṃ prakṛteśca pāragastrayīguṇānā triguṇasya pāragaḥ yaḥ syāccaturviśatitattvapāragaḥ sa pārago nādhyayanasya pāragaḥ  BndP kṛtsnaṃ yathāvatsamupaiti tatparastathaiva bhūyaḥ pralayatvamātmanaḥ pratyāharedyogapathaṃ na yo dvijo na sarvapāra kramapāragocaraḥ  BndP vedasya veditavyaṃ ca vedyaṃ vindati yogavit taṃ vai vedavidaḥ prāhustamāhurvedapāragam  BndP vedaṃ ca veditavyaṃ ca viditvā vai yathāsthitaḥ evaṃ vedavidaḥ prāhuranyaṃ vai vedapāragam  BndP yajñānvedāṃstathā kāmāṃstapāṃsi vividhāni ca prāpnotyāyuḥ prajāścaiva pitṛbhakto na saśayaḥ  BndP śraddhayā śrāddhakalpaṃ tu yastvimaṃ niyataḥ paṭhet sarvāṇyetāni vāpnoti tīrthadānaphalāni ca  BndP sa paṅktipāvanaścaiva dvijānāmagrabhugbhavet āśrāvya ca dvijānso tha sarvakāmānavāpnuyāt  BndP yaścaitacchṛṇuyānnityama nyāṃśca śrāvayeddvijaḥ anasūyurjitakrodho lobhamohavivarjitaḥ  BndP tīrthādīnāṃ phalaṃ prāpya dānādīnāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ mokṣopāyaṃ labhecchreṣṭhaṃ svargopāyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ iha cāpi parā puṣṭhistasmātkurvīta nityaśaḥ  BndP imaṃ vidhiṃ yo hi paṭhedatandritaḥ samāhitaḥ saṃsadi parvasaṃdhiṣu apatyabhāgī ca pareṇa tejasā divaukasāṃ sa vrajate salokatām  BndP yena proktastvayaṃ kalpo namastasmai svayaṃbhuve mahāyogeśvarebhyaśca sadā ca praṇato smyaham  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīya upoddhātapādeśrāddhakalpe brahmaṇaparīkṣā nāma ekonaviṃśo dhyāyaḥ  bṛhaspatiruvācaityete pitaro devā devānāmapi devatāḥ saptasvete sthitā nityaṃ sthāneṣu pitaro vyayāḥ  BndP prajāpatisutā hyete sarveṣāṃ tu mahātmanām ādyo gaṇastu yogānāmanuyogavivarddhanaḥ  BndP dvitīyo devatānāṃ tu tṛtīyo dānavādinām śeṣāstu varṇiṃnāṃ jñeyā iti sarve prakīrttitāḥ  BndP devāschaitānyajante vai sarvajñāneṣvavasthitān āśramaśca yajantyenāṃścatvārastu yathākramam  BndP sarve varṇā yajantyenāṃścatvārastu yathāgamam tathā saṃkarajātyaśca mlecchāścāpi yajanti vai  BndP pitṛṃstu yo yajedbhaktyā pitaraḥ prīṇayanti te pitaraḥ puṣṭikāmasya prajākāmasya vā punaḥ  BndP puṣṭiṃ prajāṃ tu svargaṃ ca prayacchanti pitāmahāḥ devakāryādapi tathā pitṛkāryaṃ viśiṣyate  BndP devatānāṃ hi pitaraḥ pūrvamāpyāyanaṃ smṛtāḥ na hi yogagatiḥ sūkṣmā pitṝṇāṃ jñāyate naraiḥ  BndP tapasā hi prasiddhena kiṃ punarmāṃsacakṣuṣā sarveṣāṃ rājataṃ pātramatha vā rajatānvitam  BndP pāvanaṃ hyuttamaṃ proktaṃ devānāṃ pitṛbhiḥ saha yeṣāṃ dāsyanti piṇḍāṃstrīnbāndhavā nāmagotrataḥ  BndP bhūmau kuśottarāyāṃ ca apasavyavidhānataḥ sarvatra varttamānāste piṇḍāḥ prīṇanti vai pitṝn  BndP yadāhāro bhavejjanturāhāraḥ so sya jāyate yathā goṣṭhe pranaṣṭāṃ vai vatso vindati mātaram  BndP tathā taṃ nayate mantro janturyatrāvatiṣṭhati nāmagotraṃ ca mantraṃ ca dattamannaṃ nayanti tam  BndP api yoniśataṃ prāptāṃstṛptistānanugacchati evameṣā sthitā sattā brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ  BndP pitṝṇamādisargetu lokānāmakṣayārthinām ityete pitaraścaiva lokā duhitarastathā  BndP dauhitrā yajamānaśca proktāścaiva mayānagha kīrttitāḥ pitaraste vai tava putra yathākramam  BndP śaṃyuruvācaaho divyastvayā tāta pitṛsargastu kīrtitaḥ lokā duhitaraścaiva dohitrāśca śrutāstathā  BndP dānāni saha śaucena kīrttitāni phalāni ca akṣayyatvaṃ dvijāṃścaiva sarvametadudāhṛtam adyaprabhṛti karttāsmi sarvametadyathātatham  BndP bṛhaspatiruvācaityetadaṅgirāḥ pūrvamṛṣīṇāmuktavānprabhuḥ pṛṣṭaśca saṃśayānsarvānṛṣīnāha nṛsaṃsadi  BndP satre tu vitate pūrvaṃ tathā varṣasahasrake yasminsadaspatisnāto brahmā sīddevatāprabhuḥ  BndP gatāni tatra varṣāṇāṃ pañcāśacca śatāni vai ślokāścātra purā gītā ṛṣibhirbrahmavādibhiḥ  BndP dīkṣitasya purā satre brahmamaḥ paramātmanaḥ tatraiva dattamannāgraṃ pitṝṇāmakṣayarthinām lokānāṃ ca hitārthāya brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā  BndP sūta uvācaevaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ pūrvaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ putreṇa dhīmatā provāca pitṛsargaṃ tu yaścaiva samudāhṛta  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīya upoddhātapādeśrāddhakalpo nāma viṃśatitamo dhyāyaḥ  samāptaścāyaṃ śrāddhakalpaḥ vasiṣṭha uvācaitthaṃ pravarttamānasya jamadagnermahātmanaḥ varṣāṇi katicidrājanvyatīyuramitaujasaḥ  BndP rāmo pi nṛpaśārdūla sarvadharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ vedavedāṅgatattvajñaḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ  BndP pitroścakāra śuśrūṣāṃ vinītātmā mahāmatiḥ prītiṃ ca nijaceṣṭābhiranvahaṃ paryavarttayat  BndP itthaṃ pravarttamānasya varṣāṇi katicinnṛpa pitroḥ śuśrūṣayānaiṣīdrāmo matimatāṃ varaḥ  BndP sa kadācinmahātejāḥ pitāmaha guhaṃ prati gantuṃ vyavasito rājandaivena ca niyojitaḥ  BndP nipīḍya śirasā pitroścaraṇau bhṛgupuṅgavaḥ uvāca prāñjalirbhūtavā sapraśrayamidaṃ vacaḥ  BndP kañcidarthamahaṃ tāta mātaraṃ tvāṃ ca sāmpratam vijñāpayitumicchāmi mama tacchrotumarhathaḥ  BndP pitāmahamahaṃ draṣṭumutkaṇṭhitamanāściram tasmāttatpārśvamadhunā gamiṣye vāmanujñayā  BndP āhūtaścāsakṛttāta sotkaṇṭhaṃ prīyamāṇayā pitāmahyā bahumukhairicchantyā mama darśanam  BndP pitṝnpitāmahasyāpi priyameva pradarśanam sadīyaṃ tena tatpārśvaṃ gantuṃ māmanujānata  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācaiti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā saṃbhrāntaṃ samudīritam harṣeṇa mahatā yuktau sāśrunetrau babhūvatuḥ  BndP tamāliṅgya mahābhāgaṃ mūrdhnyupāghrāya sādaram abhinandyāśiṣā tāta hyubhau tāvidamāhatuḥ  BndP pitāmahagṛhaṃ tāta prayāhi tvaṃ yathāsukham pitāmahapitāmahyoḥ prītaye darśanāya ca  BndP tatra gatvā yathānyāyaṃ taṃ śuśrūṣā parāyaṇaḥ kañcitkālaṃ tayorvatsa prītaye vasa tadgṛhe  BndP sthitvā nāticiraṃ kālaṃ tayorbhūyo pyanuśaya atrāgaccha mahābhāga kṣemeṇāsmaddidṛkṣayā  BndP kṣaṇārddhamapi śaktāḥ stho na vinā putradarśanam tasmātpitāmaha gṛhe na cirātsthātumarhasi  BndP tadājñayātha vā putra prapitāmahasannidhim gato pi śīghramāgaccha krameṇa tadanujñayā  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācaityuktastau parikramya praṇamya ca mahāmatiḥ pitarāvapyanujñāpya pitāmahagṛhaṃ tataḥ  BndP sa gatvā bhṛguvaryasya ṛcīkasya mahātmanaḥ praviveśāśramaṃ rāmo muniśiṣyopaśobhitam  BndP svādhyāyaghoṣairvipulaiḥ sarvataḥ pratināditam praśāntavaira sattvāḍhyaṃ sarvasattvamanoharam  BndP sa praviśyaśramaṃ ramyamṛcīkaṃ sthitamāsane dadarśa rāmo rājendra sa pitāmahamagrataḥ  BndP jājvalyamānaṃ tapasā dhiṣṇyasthamiva pāvakam upāsitaṃ satyavatyā yathā dakṣiṇāyadhvaram  BndP svasamīpamupāyāntaṃ rāmamālokya tau nṛpa suciraṃ taṃ vimarśetāṃ samājñāpūrvadarśanau  BndP ko yameṣa taporāśiḥ sarvalatraṇapūjitaḥ bālo yaṃ balavānbhātigāṃbhīryātpraśrayeṇa ca  BndP evaṃ tayościntayatoḥ saharṣaṃ hṛdi kautukāt āsasāda śanai rāmaḥ samīpe vinayānvitaḥ  BndP svanāmagotre matimānuktvā pitrormudānvitaḥ saṃspṛśaṃścaraṇau mūrdhnā hastābhyāṃ cābhyavādayat  BndP tatastau prītamanasau samuthāpya ca sattamam āśīrbhirabhinandetāṃ pṛthak pṛthagubhāvapi  BndP tamāśliṣyāṅkamāropya harṇāśruplutalocanau vīkṣantau tanmukhāṃbhojaṃ paraṃ harṣamavāpatuḥ  BndP tataḥ sukhopaviṣṭaṃ tamātmavaṃśasamudvaham anāmayamapṛcchetāṃ tāvubhau daṃpatī tadā  BndP pitarau te kuśalino vatsa kiṃbhrātarastathā anāyāsena te vṛttirvartate cātha karhicit  BndP samastābhyāṃ tato rājannācacakṣe yathoditaḥ tathā svānugataṃ pitrorbhrātṝṇāṃ caiva ceṣṭitam  BndP evaṃ tayormahārāja satprītijanitaiguṇaiḥ prīyamāṇo vasadrāmaḥ pituḥ pitrornniveśane  BndP sa tasminsarvabhūtānāṃ manonayananandanaḥ uvāsa katicinmāsāṃstacchuśrūṣāparāyaṇaḥ  BndP athānujñāpya tau rājanbhṛguvaryo mahāmanāḥ pitāmahagurorgantumiyeṣāśrayamāśramam  BndP sa tābhyāṃ prītiyuktābhyāmāśīrbhirabhinanditaḥ yathā cābhyāṃ pradiṣṭena yayā vaurvāśramaṃ prati  BndP taṃ namaskṛtya vidhivaccyavanaṃ ca mahātapāḥ sapraharṣaṃ tadājñātaḥ prayayāvāśramaṃ bhṛgoḥ  BndP sa gatvāmunimukhyasya bhṛgorāśramamaṇḍalam dadarśa śāntacetobhirmunibhiḥ sarvato vṛtam  BndP susnigdhaśītalacchāyaiḥ sarvartukaguṇānvitaiḥ tarubhiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ prītaḥ phalapuṣpottarānvitaiḥ  BndP nānākhagakulārāvairmanaḥśrotrasukhāvahaiḥ brahmaghoṣaiśca vividhaiḥ sarvataḥ pratināditam  BndP samantrāhutihomotthadhūmagandhena sarvataḥ nirastanikhilāghaughaṃ vanāntaravisarpiṇā  BndP samitkuśāharairdaṇḍamekhalājinamaṇḍitaiḥ abhitaḥ śobhitaṃ rājanramyairmunikumārakaiḥ  BndP prasūnajalasaṃpūrmapātrahastābhirantarā śobhitaṃ munikalyābhiścarantībhiritastataḥ  BndP sapotahariṇīyūthairvisraṃbhādaviśaṅkibhiḥ uṭajāṅgaṇaparyantatarucchāyāsvadhiṣṭhitam  BndP romanthataḥ parāmṛṣṭiyūtha sākṣikamutpradaiḥ prārabdhatāṇḍavaṃ kekīmayūrairmadhurasvaraiḥ  BndP pravikīrṇakaṇoddeśaṃ mṛgaśabdaiḥ samīpagaiḥ anālīḍhātapacchāyāśuṣyannīvārarāśibhiḥ  BndP hūyamānānalaṃ kāle pūjyamānātithivrajam abhyasyamānacchandaughaṃ cintyamānagamoditam  BndP paṭhyamānākhilasmārttaṃ śrautārthapravicāraṇam prārabdhapitṛdevejyaṃ sarvabhūtamanoharam  BndP tapasvijanabhūyiṣṭhamākāpuruṣasevitam tapovṛddhikaraṃ puṇyaṃ sarvasattvasukhāspadam  BndP tapodhanānandakaraṃ brahmalokamivāparam prasūnasaurabhabhrāmyanmadhupārāvanāditam  BndP sarvato vījyamānena vividhena nabhasvatā evaṃvidhaguṇopetaṃ paśyannāśramamuttamam  BndP praviveśa vinītātmā sukṛtīvāmarālayam saṃpraviśyaśramopāntaṃ rāmaḥ svaprapitāmaham  BndP dadarśa parito rājanmuniśiṣyaśatāvṛtam vyākhyānavedikāmadhye niviṣṭaṃ kuśaviṣṭare sitaśmaśrujaṭākūrcabrahmasūtropaśobhitam  BndP vāmetarorumadhyāsta vāmajaṅghena jānunā  BndP yogapaṭṭena saṃvītasvadehamṛṣipuṅgavam vyākhyānamudrāvilasatsavyapāṇitalāṃbujam  BndP yogapaṭṭoparinyastavibhrājadvāmapāṇikam samyagāraṇyavākyānāṃ sūkṣmatattvārthasaṃhatim  BndP vivṛtya munimukhyebhyaḥ śrāvayantaṃ taponidhim pituḥ pitāmahaṃ ddaṣṭvā rāmastasya mahātmanaḥ  BndP śanairivamahārāja samīpaṃ samupāgamat tamāgatamupālakṣya tatprabhāvapradharṣitāḥ  BndP śaṅkāmavāpurmunayo dūrādevākhilā nṛpa tāvadūbhṛgurameyātmā tadāgamanatoṣitaḥ  BndP nivṛttānyakathālāpastaṃ paśyannāsa pārthiva rāmo pi tamupāgamya vinayāvanatānanaḥ  BndP avandata yathānyayamupendra iva vedhasam abhivādya yathānyāyaṃ khyātiṃ ca vinayānvitaḥ  BndP tāṃśca saṃbhāvayāmāsa munīnrāmoyathāvayaḥ taiśca sarvairmudopetairāśīrbhirabhivarddhitaḥ  BndP upāviveśa medhāvī bhūmau teṣāmanujñayā upaviṣṭaṃ tato rāmamāśīrbhirabhinanditam  BndP papracchakuśalapraśnaṃ tamālokya bhṛgustadā kuśalaṃ khalu te vatsa pitrośca kimanāmayam  BndP bhrātṝṇāṃ caiva bhavataḥpituḥ pitrostathaiva ca kimarthamāgato tra tvamadhunāmama sannidhim  BndP kenāpi vā tvamādiṣṭaḥ svayamevāthavāgataḥ tatorāmo yathānyāyaṃ tasmai sarvamaśeṣataḥ  BndP kathayāmāsa yatpṛṣṭaṃ tadā tena mahātmanā piturmātuśca vṛttānta bhrātṝṇāṃ ca mahātmanām  BndP pituḥ pritroścakauśalya darśanaṃ ca tayornṛpa etadanyacca sakalaṃ bhṛgoḥ sapraśrayaṃ mudā  BndP nyavedayadyathānyāyamātmanaśca samīhitam śrutvaitadakhilaṃ rājanrāmeṇa samudīritam  BndP taṃ ca dṛṣṭvā viśeṣeṇa bhṛguḥ prīto bhyanandata evaṃ tasya priyaṃ kurvannutkṛṣṭairātmakarmabhiḥ  BndP tatrāśrame vasadrāmo dināni katicinnṛpa tataḥ kadācidekānte rāmaṃ munivarottamaḥ  BndP vatsāgaccheti taṃ rājannupāhvayadupahvare so bhigamya tamāsīnamabhivādya kṛtāñjaliḥ  BndP tasthau tatpurato rāmaḥ suprītenāntarātmanā āśīrbhirabhinandyātha bhṛgustaṃ prīta mānasaḥ  BndP prāha nādhigatāśaṅkaṃ rāmamālokya sādaram śruṇu vatsa vaco mahya yattvāṃ vakṣyāmi sāṃpratam  BndP hitārthaṃ sarvalokānāṃ tava cāsmākameva ca gaccha putra mamādeśāddhimavantaṃ mahāgirim  BndP adhunaivāśramādasmāttapase dhṛtamānasaḥ tatragatvā mahābhāga kṛtvāśramāpadaṃ śubham  BndP ārādhaya mahādevaṃ tapasā niyamena ca prītimutpādya tasya tvaṃ bhaktyānanyagayā cirāt  BndP śreyo mahadavāpnoṣi nātra kāryā vijāraṇā tarasā tava bhaktyā ca prīto bhavati śaṅkaraḥ  BndP kariṣyati ca te sarvaṃ manasā yadyadicchasi tuṣṭe tasmiñjagannāthe śaṅkare bhaktavatsale  BndP astragrāmamaśeṣaṃ tvaṃ vaṇu putra yathepsitam tvayā hitārthaṃ devānāṃ karaṇīyaṃ suduṣkaram  BndP vidyate bhyadhikaṃ karma śastrasādhyamanekaśaḥ tasmāttvaṃ devadeveśaṃ samārādhaya śaṅkaram  BndP bhaktyā paramayā yuktastato bhīṣṭamavāpsyasi  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīya upoddhātapāde ekaviṃśati tamaudhyāyaḥ  vasiṣṭha uvācaityevamukto bhṛguṇā tathetyuktvā praṇamya ca rāmastenābhyanujñātaścakāra gamane manaḥ  BndP bhṛguṃ khyātiṃ ca vidhivatparikramya praṇamyaca pariṣvaktastathā tābhyāmāśīrbhirābhinanditaḥ  BndP munīṃśca tānnamaskṛtya taiḥ sarvairanumoditaḥ niścakramāśramāttasmāttapase kṛtaniścayaḥ  BndP tato guruniyogena taduktenaiva vartmanā himavantaṃ girivaraṃ yayau rāmo mahāmanāḥ  BndP so tītya vividhāndeśānparvatānsaritastathā vanāni munimukhyānāmāvāsāṃścātyagācchanaiḥ  BndP tatratatra nivāseṣu munīnāṃ nivasanpathi tīrtheṣu kṣetramukhyeṣu nivasanvā yayau śanaiḥ  BndP atītya subahūndeśānpaśyannapi manoramān āsasādaca laśreṣṭhaṃ himavantamanuttamam  BndP sa gatvā parvatavaraṃ nānādrumalatāsthitam dadarśa vipulaiḥ śṛṅgairullikhantamivāṃbaram  BndP nānādhātuvicitraiśca pradeśairupaśobhitam ratnauṣadhībhirabhitaḥ sphuradbhirabhiśobhitam  BndP marutsaṃghaṭṭanāghṛṣṭanīrasāṃghripajanmanā sānilenānalenocchairdahyamānaṃ navaṃ kvacit  BndP kvacidravikarāmarśajvaladarkepalāgnibhiḥ dravaddhimāśilājātujalaśāntadavānalam  BndP sphaṭikāñjanadurvarṇasvarṇarāśiprabhākaraiḥ sphuratparasparacchāyāśarairddīptavanaṃ kvacit  BndP upatyakaśilāpṛṣṭhavālātapaniṣevibhiḥ tuṣāraklinnasiddhaughaurudbhāsitavanaṃ kvacit  BndP kvacidarkāśusaṃbhinnaścāmīkaraśilāśritaiḥ yakṣaughairbhāsitopāntaṃ viśadbhirivapāvakam  BndP darīmukhaviniṣkrāntatarakṣūtpatanākulaiḥ mṛgayūthārttasannādairāpūritaguhaṃ kvacit  BndP yuddhyadvarāhaśārdūlayūthapairita steram prasabhonmṛṣṭakāntoruśilātarutaṭaṃ kvacit  BndP kalabhonmeṣaṇākṛṣṭakariṇībhiranudrutaiḥ gavayaiḥ khurasaṃkṣuṇṇaśilāprasthataṭaṅkvacit  BndP vāsitarthe bhisaṃvṛddhamadonmattamataṅgajaiḥ yuddhyadbhiścūrṇitānekagaṇḍaśailavanaṃ kvacit  BndP bṛṃhitaśravaṇāmarṣānmātaṃ gānabhidhāvatām siṃhānāṃ caraṇakṣuṇṇanakhabhinnoparaṃ kvacit  BndP sahasā nekaśabaraprasaktairṛyūthapaiḥ itaretarasaṃmardaṃ viprabhagnadṛṣatkvacit  BndP girikuñjeṣu saṃkrīḍatkariṇīmadvipaṃ kvacit kareṇumādravanmattagajākalitakānanam  BndP svapatsiṃhamukhaśvāsamarutpurmadarīśatam gahaneṣu gurutrāsasāśaṅkaviharanmṛgam  BndP kaṇṭākaśliṣṭalāṅgūlalomatruṭanakātaraiḥ krīḍitaṃ camarīyūthairmandamandavicāribhiḥ  BndP girikandarasaṃsaktakinnarīsamudīritaiḥ satālanādairudinairbhṛtāśeṣadiśāmukham  BndP araṇyadevatānāṃ ca caretīnāmitastataḥ alaktakarasaklinnacaraṇāṅkitabhūtalam  BndP mayūrakekirīvṛndaiḥ saṃgīta madhurasvaraiḥ pravṛttanṛttaṃ parito vitatodagrabarhibhiḥ  BndP jalasthalaruhānekakusumotkaravarṣibhiḥ gātrāhlādakarairmandaṃ vījyamānaṃ vanānilaiḥ  BndP bhūtārttavarasāsvādamādyatpuṃskokilāravaiḥ ākulīkṛtaparyantasahakāravanāntaram  BndP nānāpuṣpāsavonmādyadbhṛṅgasaṃgītanāditam anekavihagārāvabadhirīkṛtakānanam  BndP madhudravārdrāviralapratyagrakusumotkaraiḥ vanāntamārutākīrṇairalaṅkṛtamahītalam  BndP upariṣṭānnipatatāṃ viṣamopalasaṃkaṭe nirjharāṇāṃ mahārāvaiḥ samantādbadhirīkṛtam  BndP vitatānekasaṃsaktaśākhāgrāviralacchadaiḥ pāṭalairviṭapacchāyairupaśalyasamutthitaiḥ  BndP kadaṃbaniṃbahintālasarjabedhūkatindukaiḥ kapitthapanasāśokasahakāregudāśanaiḥ  BndP nāgacaṃpakapunnāgakovidārapriyaṅgubhiḥ kumudotpalamaṇḍitaiḥ  BndP nānāvihagasaṃghuṣṭaiḥ samantādupaśobhitam samāsādyatha śailendraṃ tuṣāraśiśiraṃ girim  BndP āruroha bhaguśreṣṭhastarasā taṃ mudānvitaḥ tasya praviśya gahanaṃ vanaṃ rāmo mahāmanāḥ  BndP vicacāra śanai rājannupaśalyamahīruham sa tatra vicarandikṣu hariṇībhiḥ samantataḥ  BndP vikṣyamāṇo mudaṃ lebhe sāśaṅkaṃ mugdhadṛṣṭibhiḥ sa tatra kusumāmodagandhibhirvanavāyubhiḥ  BndP vījyamāno jaharṣe sa vīkṣyodārāṃ vanaśriyam vividhāśca stharīḥ sūkṣmamuparikramya bhārgavaḥ  BndP dvandvāṃśca dhātūnvividhānpaśyannevamatarkayat aho yaṃ sarvaśailānāmādhipatye bhiṣecitaḥ  BndP brahmaṇā yajñabhākcaiva sthāne saṃpratipāditaḥ asya śailādhirājatvaṃ suvyaktamabhilakṣyate  BndP ravaiḥ kīcakaveṇunāṃ madhurīkṛtakānanaḥ nitaṃbasthalasaṃsaktatuṣāranicayaigyam  BndP vibhātīvāhitasvacchaparītadhavalāṃśukaḥ nibiḍaśritanīhāranikareṇa tathopari  BndP nānāvarṇottarāsaṃgāvṛttāṅga ivalkṣyate candanāgurukarpūrakastūrīkuṅkumādibhiḥ  BndP alaṅkṛtāgaḥ suvyaktaṃ dṛśyate hī kumudotpalakahlāranikarairupasobhitam  BndP paṅkajairutpalaiścaiva raktapītaiḥ sitāsitaiḥ anyaiśca jalacairvakṣaiḥ sarvataḥ samalaṅkṛtam  BndP haṃsasārasadātyūhakāraṇḍavaśatairapi niyatendriyaḥ  BndP tapaścacāra deveśaṃ viniveśyātmamānase bhṛgūpadiṣṭamārgeṇa bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ  BndP pūjayāmāsa deveśamekāgramanasā nṛpa aniketaḥ sa varṣāsu śiśire jalasaṃśrayaḥ  BndP grīṣme pañjāgnimadhyasthaścacāraivaṃ tapaściram ripūnnirjitya kāmādīnūrmiṣaṣaṭkaṃ vidhūya ca  BndP dvandvairanudvejitadhīstāpadoṣairanākulaḥ yamaiḥ saniyamaiścaiva śuddhadehaḥ samāhitaḥ  BndP vaśī cakāra pavanaṃ prāṇāyāmena dehagam jitapadmāsano maunī sthiracitto mahāmuniḥ  BndP vaśī cakāra cākṣāṇi pratyāhāraparāyaṇaḥ dhāraṇābhiḥ sthirīcakre manaścañcalamātmavān  BndP dhyānena devadeveśaṃ dadarśa parameśvaram svasthāntaḥ karaṇo maitraḥ sarvabādhāvivarjitaḥ  BndP cintayāmāsa deveśaṃ dhyāne dṛṣṭvā jagadgurum dhyeyāvasthi tacittātmā niścaledriyadehavān  BndP ākālāvadhi so tiṣṭhannivātasthapradīpavat japaṃśca devadeveśaṃ dhyāyaṃśca svamanīṣayā  BndP ārādhayadameyātmā sarvabhāvasthamīśvaram tataḥ sa niṣphalaṃ rūpamaiśvaraṃ yannirañjanam  BndP paraṃ jyotiracintyaṃ yadyogidhyeyamanutta mam nityaṃ śuddhaṃ sadā śāntamatīndriyamanaupamam ānandamātramacalaṃ vyāptāśeṣacarācaram  BndP cintayāmāsa tadrūpaṃ devadevasya bhārgavaḥ nityaṃ śuddhaṃ sadā śāntamatīndriyamanaupamam  BndP  iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīye upoddhātapāde vasiṣṭhasagarasaṃvāde arcunopākhyāne jāmadagnyatapaścaraṇaṃ nāma dvāviṃśatitamo  dhyāyaḥ   vasiṣṭha uvācatapasvinaṃ tadā rāmamekāgramanasaṃ bhave rahasyekāntanirataṃ niyataṃ śaṃsitavratam  BndP śrutvā tamṛṣayaḥ sarve taponirdhūtakalmaṣāḥ jñānakarmavayovṛddhā mahāntaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ  BndP didṛkṣavaḥ samājagmuḥ kutūhalasamanvitāḥ khyāpayantastapaḥ śreṣṭhaṃ tasya rājanmahātmanaḥ  BndP bhṛgvatrikratujābālivāmadevamṛkaṇḍavaḥ saṃbhāvayantaste rāmaṃ munayo vṛddhasaṃmatāḥ  BndP ājagmurāśramaṃ tasya rāmasya tapasastapaḥ dūrādeva mahāntaste puṇyakṣetranivāsinaḥ  BndP garīyaḥ sarvalokeṣu tapo gryaṃ jñānameva ca praśasya tasya te sarveprayayuḥ svaṃ svamāśramam  BndP evaṃ pravarttatastasya samīpamupasṛtya ca  BndP rāmāya seṣucāpābhyāṃ karābhyāṃ vidadheṃjalim sajalāṃbhodasannādagaṃbhīreṇa svareṇa ca  BndP jagāda bhṛguśārdūlaṃ guhāntaravisarpiṇā toṣapravarṣavyādho haṃ vasāmyasminmahāvane  BndP īśo hamasya deśasya saprāṇitaruvīrudhaḥ carāmi samacittātmā nānāsattvā miṣāśanaḥ  BndP samaśca sarvabhūteṣu na ca pitrādayo pi me abhakṣyāgamyapeyādicchandavastuṣu kutracit  BndP kṛtyākṛtyavidhaucaiva na viśeṣitadhīraham prapanno nābhigamanaṃ nivāsamapi kasyacit  BndP śakrasyāpi balenāhamanumanye na saṃśayaḥ jānate tadhyathā sarve deśo yaṃ madupāśrayaḥ  BndP tasmānna kaścidāyāti mamātrānumatiṃ vinā ityeṣa mama vṛttāntaḥ kārtsnyena kathitastava  BndP tvaṃ ca me brūhi tattvena nijavṛttamaśeṣataḥ kastvaṃ kasmādihāyātaḥ kimarthamiha dhiṣṭhitaḥ udyato nyatra vā gantuṃ kiṃ vā tava cikīrṣitam  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācaityevamuktaḥ prahasaṃstena rāmo mahādyutiḥ tūṣṇīṃ kṣaṇamiva sthitvā dadhyau kiñcidavāṅmukhaḥ  BndP ko yameva durādharṣaḥ sajalāṃbhodanisvanaḥ bravīti ca giro tyarthaṃ vispaṣṭārthapadākṣarāḥ  BndP kiṃ tu me mahatīṃ śaṅkāṃ tanurasya tanoti vai vijātisaṃśrayatvena ramaṇīyā tathā śarāḥ  BndP evaṃ cintayatastasya nimittāni śubhāni vai babhūvurbhuvi dehe ca svābhipretārthadānyalam  BndP tato vimṛśya bahuśo manasābhṛgupuṅgavaḥ uvāca śanakairvyādhaṃ vacanaṃ sūnṛtākṣaram  BndP jāmadagnyo smi bhadraṃ te rāmo nāmnā tu bhārgavaḥ tapaścartumihāyātaḥ sāṃprataṃ guruśāsanāt  BndP tapasā sarvalokeśaṃ bhaktyā ca niyamena ca ārādhayitumasmiṃstu cirāyāhaṃ samudyataḥ  BndP tasmātmarveśvaraṃ sarvaśaraṇyamabhayapradam trinetraṃ pāpadamanaṃ śaṅkaraṃ bhaktavatsalam  BndP tapasā toṣayiṣyāmi sarvajñaṃ tripurāntakam āśrame sminasarastīre niyamaṃ samupāśritaḥ  BndP bhaktānukaṃpī bhagavānyāvatpratyakṣatāṃ haraḥ upaiti tāvadatraiva sthāsyāmīti matirmama  BndP tasmāditastvayādyaiva gantumanyatra yujyate na cedbhavati me hāniḥ svakṛterniyamasya ca  BndP mānanīyo tha vāhaṃ te bhaktyā deśāntarātithiḥ svanivāsamupāyātastapasvī ca tathā muniḥ  BndP tvatasaṃnidhau nivāso me bhavetpāpāya kevalam tava cāpyasukhodarkaṃ matsamīpaniṣevaṇam  BndP sa tvaṃmadāśramopānte paricaṅkramaṇādikam parityajya sukhībhūyā lokayorubhayorapi  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācaiti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā sa bhūyo bhṛgupuṅgavam uvāca roṣatāmrākṣastāmrākṣamidamuttaram  BndP brahman kimidamatyarthaṃ samīpe vasatiṃ mama parigarhayase yena kṛtaghnasyeva kāṃpratam  BndP kiṃ mayāpakṛtaṃ loke bhavato nyasya vā kvacit anāgaskāriṇaṃ dāntaṃ ko vamanyeta nāmataḥ  BndP sannidhiḥ pariharttavyo yadi me viprapuṅgava darśanaṃ saha saṃvāsaḥ saṃbhāṣaṇamathāpi ca  BndP āyuṣmatādhunaivāsmādapasarttavyamāśramāt svasaṃśrayaṃ parityajya kvāhaṃ yāsye bubhukṣitaḥ  BndP svādhivāsaṃ parityajya bhavatā yoditaḥ katham ito nyasmin gāmiṣyāmi dūre nāhaṃ viśeṣataḥ  BndP gamyatāṃ bhavatānyatra sthīyatāmatra vecchayā nāhaṃ cālayituṃ śakyaḥ sthānādasmātkathañcana  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācatacchrutvā vacanaṃ tasya kiñcitkopasamanvitaḥ tamuvāca punarvākyamidaṃ rājanbhṛgūdvahaḥ  BndP vyādhajātiriyaṃ krūrā sarvasattvabhayāvahā khalakarmaratā nityaṃ dhikkṛtā sarvajantubhiḥ  BndP tasyāṃ jāto si pāpīyānsarvaprāṇivihiṃsakaḥ sa kathaṃ na parityājyaḥ sujanaiḥ syāttu durmate  BndP tasmādvihīnajātīyaṃ viditvātmānamabyatha śīghramasmādvrajānyatra nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  BndP śarīratrāṇakāruṇyātsamīpaṃ nopasarpasi yathā tvaṃ kaṇṭakādīnāmasahiṣṇutayā vyathām  BndP tathāvehi samastānāṃ priyāḥ prāṇāḥ śarīriṇām vyathā cābhihatānāṃ tu vidyate bhavato nyathā  BndP ahiṃsā sarvabhūtānāmiti dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ etadviruddhācaraṇānnityaṃ sadbhirvigarhitaḥ  BndP ātmaprāṇābhirakṣārthaṃ tvamaśeṣaśarīriṇaḥ haniṣyasi kathaṃ satsunāpnoṣi vacanīyatām  BndP tasmācchīghraṃ tu bhogaccha tvameva puruṣādhama tvayā me kṛtyadoṣasya hāniśca na bhaviṣyati  BndP na catsvayamito gaccheśtatastava balādapi apasarpaṇatābuddhimahamutpādaye sphuṭam  BndP kṣaṇārddhamapi te pāpa śreyasī neha saṃsthitiḥ viruddhācaraṇo nityaṃ dharmadriṣ ko labhecca śām  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācarāmasya vacanaṃ śrutvā prīto pi tamidaṃ vacaḥ uvāca saṃkruddha iva vyādharūpī pinākadhṛk  BndP sarvametadahaṃ manyaṃ vyarthaṃ vyavasitaṃ tava kutastvaṃ prathamo jñānī kutaḥ śaṃbhuḥ kutastapaḥ  BndP kutastvaṃ kliśyase mūḍha tapasā tena te dhunā ghruvaṃ mithyāpravṛttasya na hi tuṣyati śaṅkaraḥ  BndP viruddhalokācaraṇaḥ śaṃbhustasya vituṣṭaye pratapatyabudho marttyastvāṃ vinā kaḥ mudurmate  BndP atha vā ca gataṃ me dya yuktametadasaṃśayam saṃpūjya pūjakaviddhau śaṃbhostava ca saṃgamaḥ  BndP tvayā pūjayituṃ yuktaḥ sa eva bhuvane rataḥ saṃpūjako pi tasya tvaṃ yogyo nātra vicāraṇā  BndP pitāmahasya lokānāṃ brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ śiraśchittvā punaḥ śaṃbhurbrahmahatyāmavāptavān  BndP brahmahatyābhibhūtena prāyastvaṃ śaṃbhunā dvija upadiṣṭo si tatkartuṃ nocedevaṃ kathaṃ kṛthāḥ  BndP gurustrībrahmahatyotthapātakakṣapaṇāya ca tapaścarasi nānena tapasā tatpraṇaśyati  BndP pātakānāṃ kilānyeṣāṃ prāyaścittāni saṃtyapi mātṛdruhāmavehi tvaṃ na kvacitkila niṣkṛtiḥ  BndP ahiṃsālakṣaṇo cettadadhikaṃ tarhi yujyeyamenasā  BndP yāvatpoṣaṇaghātena na vayaṃ syāma ninditāḥ tadetatsaṃpradhārya tvaṃ nindavā māṃ praśaṃsa vā  BndP sādhu vāsādhu vā karma yasya yadvihitaṃ purā tadeva tena karttavyamāpadyapi kathañcana  BndP nirūpaya svabhuddhyā tvamātmano mama cāntaram ahaṃ tu sarvabhāvena mitrādibharaṇe rataḥ  BndP saṃtyajya pitaraṃ vṛddhaṃ vinihatya ca mātaram bhūtvā tu dhārmikastvaṃ tu tapaścartumihāgataḥ  BndP ye tu mūlavidasteṣāṃ vispaṣṭaṃ yatra darśanam yathājihvaṃ bhavennātra vacasāpi samīhitum  BndP ahaṃ tu samyagjānāmi tava vṛttamaśeṣataḥ tasmādalaṃ te tapasā niṣphalena bhṛgūdvaha  BndP sukhamicchasi cettyaktvā kāyakleśakaraṃ tapaḥ yāhi rāma tvamanyatra yatra vā na vidurjanāḥ  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīya upoddhātapāde trayoviṃśatitamo dhyāyaḥvasiṣṭha uvācaityuktastena bhūpāla rāmo matimatāṃ varaḥ nirūpya manasā bhūyastamuvācābhivismitam  BndP rāma uvācakastvaṃ brūhi mahābhāga na vai prākṛtapūruṣaḥ indrasyevānubhāvena vapurālakṣyate tava  BndP vicitrārthapadaudāryaguṇagāṃbhīryajātibhiḥ sarvajñasyaiva te vāṇī śrūyate timanoharā  BndP indro vahniryamo dhātā varuṇo vā dhanādhipaḥ īśānastapano brahmā vāyuḥ somo gururguhaḥ  BndP eṣāmanyatamaḥ prāyo bhavānbhavitumarhati anubhāvena jātiste hṛdiśaṅkāṃ tanoti me  BndP māyāvī bhagavānviṣṇuḥ śrūyate puruṣottamaḥ ko vā tvaṃ vapuṣānena brūhi māṃ samupāgataḥ  BndP atha vā jagatāṃ nāthaḥ sarvajñaḥ parameśvaraḥ paramātmātmasaṃbhūtirātmārāmaḥ sanātanaḥ  BndP svacchandacārī bhagavāñchivaḥ sarvajaganmayaḥ vapuṣānena saṃyukte bhavānbhavitumarhati  BndP nānyasyedṛgbhavelloke prabhāvānugataṃ vapuḥ jātyarthasauṣṭhavopetā vāṇī caudāryaśālinī  BndP manye haṃ bhaktavātsalyādvānena vapuṣāharaḥ pratyakṣatāmupagato saṃdeho smatparīkṣayā  BndP na kevalaṃ bhavān vyādhasteṣāṃ nedṛgvidhākṛtiḥ tasmāttubhyaṃ namastasmai surupaṃ saṃpradarśaya  BndP āviṣkurvanprasīdātmamahimānuguṇaṃ vapuḥ mamānekavidhā śaṅkāmucyeta yena mānasī  BndP prasīda sarvabhāvena buddhimohau mamādhunā praṇāśaya svarūpasya grahaṇādeva kevalam  BndP prārthayetvāṃ mahābhāga praṇamya śirasāsakṛt kastvaṃ me darśayātmānaṃ baddho yaṃ te mayāñjaliḥ  BndP ityuktvā taṃ mahābhāga jñātumicchanbhṛgūdvahaḥ upaviśya tato bhūmau dhyānamāste samāhitaḥ  BndP baddhapadmāsano maunī yatavākkāyamānasaḥ niruddhaprāṇasaṃcāro dadhyau ciramudāradhīḥ  BndP sanniyamyendriyagrāmaṃ mano hṛdi śaraṇaṃ bhava me śarva tvadbhaktasya jagatpate bhūyo nanyāśrayāṇāṃ tu tvameva hi parāyaṇam  BndP yanmayāpakṛtaṃ deva duruktaṃ vāpi śaṅkara ajānatā tvāṃ bhagavanmama tatkṣantumarhasi  BndP ananyavedyarupasya sadbhāvamihakaḥ pumān tvāmṛte tava sarveśa samyak śakroti veditum  BndP tasmāttvaṃ sarvabhāvena prasīda mama śaṅkara nānyāsti me gatistubhyaṃ namo bhūyo namo namaḥ  BndP vasiṣṭha BndP dāsye cābhi mataṃ save bhavate haṃ tvayā vṛtam bhakto hi me tvamatyarthaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  BndP mayaivāvagataṃ sarvaṃ tdṛdi vatte dyavarttate tasmādbravīmi yattvāhaṃ tatkuruṣvāviśaṅkitam BndP papāta saṃspṛśanmūrdhnā caraṇau puravidviṣaḥ paśyatāṃ devavṛndānāṃ madhye bhṛgukulodvaham  BndP tamutthāpya śivaḥ prītaḥ prasannamukhapaṅkajam rāmaṃ madhurayā vācā prahasannāha sādaram  BndP ime vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīya upoddhātapāderjunopākhyāne caturviṃśatitamo dhyāyaḥ  vasiṣṭha uvācatatasta draktiyogena sa prītātmā jagatpatiḥ pratyakṣamagamattasya sarvaiḥ saha marudgaṇaiḥ  BndP taṃ sakalādhyakṣa namaste bhaktavatsala namaste sarvabhūteśa namaste vṛṣabhadhvaja  BndP namaste sakalādhīśa namaste karuṇākara namaste sakalāvāsa namaste nīlalohita  BndP namaḥ sakaladevārigaṇanāśāya śūline kapāline namastubhyaṃ sarvalokaikapāline  BndP śmaśānavāsine nityaṃ namaḥ kailāsavāsine namo stu pāśine tubhyaṃ kālakūṭaviṣāśine  BndP vibhave maravandyāya prabhave te svayaṃbhuve namo khilajagatkarmasākṣibhūtāya śaṃbhave  BndP namastripatha gāphenabhāsigārddhandumauline mahābhogīndrahārāya śivāya paramātmane  BndP bhasmasaṃcchannadehāya namorkāgnīnducakṣuṣe kapardine namastubhyamandhakāsuramarddine  BndP tripuradhvaṃsine dakṣayajñavidhvaṃsine namaḥ girijākucakāśmīravirañjitamahorase  BndP mahādevāya maha te namaste kṛttivāsase yogidhyeyasvarūpāya śivāyācintyatejase  BndP svabhaktahṛdayāṃbhojakarṇikāmadhyavarttine sakalāgamasiddhāntasārarūpāya te namaḥ  BndP namo nikhilayogendrabodhanāyāmṛtātmane śaṅkarāyākhilavyāptamahimne paramātmane  BndP namaḥ śarvāya śāntāya brahmaṇe viśvarupiṇe ādimadhyāntahīnāya nityāyāvyaktamūrttaye  BndP vyaktāvyaktasvarūpāya sthūlasūkṣmātmane namaḥ namo vedāntavedyāya viśvavijñānarūpiṇe  BndP namaḥ surāsuraśreṇimaulipuṣpārcitāṅghraye śrīkaṇṭhāya jagaddhātre lokakartre namonamaḥ  BndP rajoguṇātmane tubhyaṃ viśvasṛṣṭividhāyine hiraṇyagarbharūpāya harāya jagadādaye  BndP namo viśvātmane lokasthitivyā pārakāriṇe sattvavijñānarupāya parāya pratyagātmane  BndP tamoguṇavikārāya jagatsaṃhārakāriṇe klpānte rudrarūpāya parāpara vide namaḥ  BndP avikārāya nityāya namaḥ sadasadātmane buddhibuddhiprabodhāya buddhīndriyavikāriṇe  BndP vasvādityamarudbhiśca sādhyarudrāśvibhedataḥ yanmāyābhinnamatayo devāstasmai namonamaḥ  BndP avikāramajaṃ nityaṃ sūkṣmarūpamanaupamam tava yattanna jānanti yogino pi sadāmalāḥ  BndP tvāmavijñāya durjñeyaṃ samyagbrahmādayo pi hi saṃsaranti bhave nūnaṃ na tatkarmātmakāściram  BndP yāvannopaiti caraṇau tavājñānavighātinaḥ tāvadbhramati saṃsāre paṇḍito cetano pi vā  BndP sa eva dakṣaḥ sa kṛtī sa muniḥ sa ca paṇḍitaḥ bhavataścaraṇāṃbhoje yena buddhiḥ sthirīkṛtā  BndP susūkṣmatvena gahanaḥ sadbhāvaste trayīmayaḥ viduṣāmapi mūḍhena sa mayā jñāyate katham  BndP aśabdagojaratvena mahimnastava sāṃpratam stotumapyanalaṃ samyaktvā mahaṃ jaḍadhīryataḥ  BndP tasmādajñānato vāpi mayā bhaktyaiva saṃstutaḥ prītaśca bhava deveśa nanu tvaṃ bhaktavatsalaḥ  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācaiti stutastadā tena bhaktyā rāmeṇa śaṅkaraḥ meghagaṃbhīrayā vācā tamuvāca hasanniva  BndP bhagavānuvācarāmāhaṃ suprasanno smi śorṃyaśālitayā tava tapasā mayi bhaktyā ca stotreṇa ca viśeṣataḥ  BndP varaṃ varaya tasmāttvaṃ yadyadicchasi cetasā tubhyaṃ tattadaśeṣeṇa dāsyāmyahamaśeṣataḥ  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācaityukto devadevena taṃ praṇamya bhṛgūdvahaḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā rājannidamuvāca ha  BndP yadi deva prasannastvaṃ vārarhe smi ca yadyaham bhavatastadabhīpsāmi hetumastrāṇyaśeṣataḥ  BndP astre śastre ca śāstre ca na matto bhyadhiko bhavet lokeṣu māṃraṇejetā na bhavettvatprasādataḥ  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācatathetyuktvā tataḥ śaṃbhurastraśastrāṇyaśeṣataḥ dadau rāmāya suprītaḥ samantrāṇi kramānnṛpa  BndP saprayogaṃ sasaṃhāramastragrāmaṃ caturvidham prasādābhimukho rāmaṃ grāhayāmāsa śaṅkaraḥ  BndP asaṃgavegaṃ śubhrāśvaṃ sudhvajaṃ ca rathottamam iṣudhī cākṣayaśarau dadau rāmāya śaṅkaraḥ  BndP abhedyamajaraṃ divyaṃ dṛḍhajyaṃ vijayaṃ dhanuḥ sarvaśastrasahaṃ citraṃ kavacaṃ ca mahādhanam  BndP ajeyatvaṃ ca yuddheṣu śauryaṃ cāpratimaṃ bhuvi svecchayā dhāraṇe śāktiṃ prāṇānāṃ ca narādhipa  BndP khyātiṃ ca bījametreṇa tannāmnā sarvalaukikīm tapaḥ prabhāvaṃ ca mahatpradadau bhārgavāya saḥ  BndP bhakti cātmani rāmāya dattvā rājanyathocitām sahitaḥ sakalairbhūtaiścāmaraiścandraśekharaḥ  BndP tenaiva vapuṣā śaṃbhuḥ kṣipramantaradhāddharaḥ kṛtakṛtyastato rāmo labdhvā sarvamabhīpsitam  BndP adṛśyatāṃ gate śarve mahodaramuvāca ha mahodara madarthe tvamidaṃ sarvamaśeṣataḥ  BndP rathacāpādikaṃ tāvatparirakṣitumarhasi yadā kṛtyaṃ mamaitena tadānīṃ tvaṃ mayā smṛtaḥ rathacāpādikaṃ sarvaṃ prahiṇu tvaṃ madantikam  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācatathetyuktvā gate tasminbhṛguvaryo mahodare kṛtakṛtyo gurujanaṃ draṣṭuṃ gantumiyeṣa saḥ  BndP gacchannatha tadāsau tu himādrivanagahvare viveśa kandaraṃ rāmo bhāvikarmapracoditaḥ  BndP sa tatra dadṛśe bālaṃ dhṛtaprāṇamanudrutam vyāghreṇa vipratanayaṃ rudantaṃ bhītabhītavat  BndP dṛṣṭvānukaṃpahṛdayastatparitrāṇakātaraḥ tiṣṭhatiṣṭheti taṃ vyāghraṃ vadannuccairathānvayāt  BndP tamanudrutya vegena cirādiva bhṛgūdvahaḥ āsasāda vane ghoraṃ śārdūlamatibhīṣaṇam  BndP vyāghreṇānudrutaḥ so pi palāyanvanagahvare nipapāta dvijasutastrastaḥ prāṇabhayāturaḥ  BndP rāmo pi krodharaktākṣo vipraputraparīpsayā tṛṇamūlaṃ samādāya kuśāstreṇābhyamantrayat  BndP tāvattarakṣurbalavānādravatpatitaṃ dvijam dṛṣṭvā nanādasubhṛśaṃ rodasī kampayanniva  BndP dagdhvā tvastrāgninā vyāghraṃ praharantaṃ nakhāṅkuraiḥ akṛtavraṇamevāśu mokṣayāmāsa taṃ dvijam  BndP so pi brahmāgninirdagdhadehaḥ pāpmā nabhastale gāndharvaṃ vapurāsthāya rāmamāheti sādaram  BndP vipraśāpena bhopūrvamahaṃ prāptastarakṣutām gacchāmi mocitaḥ śāpāttvayāhamadhunā divam  BndP ityuktvā tu gate tasminrāmo vegena vismitaḥ patitaṃ dvijaputraṃ taṃ kṛpayā vyavapadyata  BndP mābhairevaṃ vadanvāṇīmārādeva dvijātmajam paramṛśattadaṅgāni śanairujjīvayannṛpa  BndP rāmeṇotthāpitaścaivaṃ sa tadonmīlya locane vilokayandadarśāgre bhṛguśreṣṭhamavasthitam  BndP bhasmīkṛtaṃ ca śārdūlaṃ dṛṣṭavā vismayamāgataḥ gatabhīrāha kastvaṃ bhoḥ kathaṃ veha samāgataḥ  BndP kena vāyaṃ nihantuṃ māmudyato bhasmasātkṛtaḥ tarakṣurbhīṣaṇākāraḥ sākṣānmṛtyurivāparaḥ  BndP bhayasaṃmūḍhamanamo mamādyāpi mahāmate hate pi tasminnakhilā bhānti vai tanmayā diśaḥ  BndP tvāmeva manye sakalaṃ pitā mātā sutdṛdgurū paramāpadamāpannaṃ tvaṃ māṃ samupajīvayan  BndP āsīnmunivaraḥ kaścicchānto nāma mahātapāḥ putrastasyāsmi tīrthārthī śālagrāmamayāsiṣam  BndP tasmātsaṃprasthitaśśailaṃ didṛkṣurgandhamādanam nānāmunigaṇairjuṣṭaṃ puṇyaṃ badarikāśramam  BndP gantukāmo pahāyāhaṃ panthānaṃ tu himācale praviśangahanaṃ ramyaṃ pradeśālokanākulam  BndP diśaṃprācīṃ samuddiśya krośamātramayāsiṣam tato diṣṭavaśenāhaṃ prādravaṃ bhayapīḍitaḥ  BndP patitaśca tvayā bhūyobhūmerutthāpito dhunā pitreva nitarāṃ putraḥ premṇātyarthaṃ dayālunā ityeṣa mama vṛttāntaḥ sākalyenoditastava  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācaiti pṛṣṭastadā tena svavṛttāntamaśeṣataḥ kathayāmāsa rājendra rāmastasmai yathākramam  BndP tatastau prītisaṃyuktau kathayantau parasparam sthitvā nāticiraṃ kālamatha gantumiyeṣa saḥ  BndP anvīyamānastenātha rāmastasmādguhāmukhāt niṣkramyāvasathaṃ pitroḥ saṃpratasthe mudānvitaḥ  BndP akṛtavraṇa evāsau vyāghreṇa bhuvi pātitaḥ rāmeṇa rakṣitaścābhudyasmāddhyāghraṃ vinighnatā  BndP tasmāttadeva nāmāsya babhūva prathitaṃ bhuvi vipraputrasya rājendra tadetatso kṛtavraṇaḥ  BndP tadā prabhṛti rāmasya cchāyevātapagā bhuvi babhūva mitramatyarthaṃ sarvāvasthāsu pārthiva  BndP sa tenānugato rājanbhṛgorāsādya sannidhim dṛṣṭvā khyātiṃ ca so bhyetya vinayenābhyavādayat  BndP sa tābhyāṃ priyamāṇābhyāmāśīrbhirabhinanditaḥ dināni katicittatra nyavasattatpriyepsayā  BndP tatastayoranumate cyavanasya mahāmuneḥ āśramaṃ praticakrāma śiṣyasaṃghaiḥ samāvṛtam  BndP niyantritāntaḥ karaṇaṃ taṃ ca saṃśāntamānasam sukanyācāpi tadbhāryāmavandata mahāmanāḥ  BndP tābhyāṃ ca prītiyuktābhyāṃ rāmaḥ samabhinanditaḥ aurvāśramaṃ samāpede draṣṭukāmastaponidhim  BndP taṃ cābhivādya medhāvī tena ca pratinanditaḥ uvāsa tatra tatprītyā dināni katicinnṛpa  BndP visṛṣṭastena śanakairṛcīkabhavanaṃ mudā pratasthe bhārgavaḥ śrīmānakṛtavraṇasaṃyutaḥ  BndP avandata pituḥ pitrornatvā pādau pṛthak pṛthak tau ca taṃ nṛpa saṃharṣāccāśiṣā pratyanandatām  BndP pṛṣṭaśca tābhyāmakhilaṃ nijavṛttamudāradhīḥ kathayāmāsa rājendra yathāvṛttamanukramāt  BndP sthitvā dināni katicittatrāpi tadanujñayā jagāmāvasathaṃ pitrormudā paramayā yutaḥ  BndP abhyetya pitarau rājannāsī nāvāśramottame avandata tayoḥ pādau yathāvadbhṛgunandana  BndP pādapraṇāmāvanataṃ samutthāpya ca sādaram āśliṣya netrasalilairnandantau paryaṣiñcatām  BndP āśīrbhirabhinandyāṅke samāropya suhurmukham vikṣantau tasya cāṅgāni parispṛśyāpaturmudam  BndP apṛcchatāñca tau rāmaṃ kalenaitāvatā tvayā kiṃ kṛtaṃ putra ko vāyaṃ kutra vā tvamupasthitaḥ  BndP kathaṃ saha sakāśe tvamāsthito vātra vāgataḥ tvayetadakhilaṃ vatsa kathyatāṃ tathyamāvayoḥ  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīyaupoddhātapāderjunopākhyāne bhārgavacarite pañcaviṃśatitamo dhyāyaḥ  vaśiṣṭha uvācaiti pṛṣṭastadā tābhyāṃ rāmo rājankṛtāñjaliḥ tayorakathayatsarvamātmanā yadanuṣṭhitam  BndP nideśādvai kulagurostapaścaraṇamātmanaḥ śaṃbhornideśāttīrthānāmaṭanaṃ ca yathākramam  BndP tadājñayaiva daityanāṃ vadhaṃ cāmarakāraṇāt haraprasādādatrāpi hyakṛtavraṇadarśanam  BndP etatsarvamaśeṣeṇa yadanyaccātmanā kṛtam kathayāmāsa tadrāmaḥ pitroḥ saṃprīyamāṇayoḥ  BndP tau ca tenoditaṃ sarvaṃ śrutvā tatkarma vistaram hṛṣṭau harṣāntaraṃ bhūyo rājannāpnuvatāvubhau  BndP evaṃ pitrormahārāja śuśrūṣāṃ bhṛgupuṅgavaḥ prakurvaṃstadvidheyātmā bhrātṝṇāṃ cāviśeṣataḥ  BndP etasminneva kāle tu kadāciddhaihayeśvaraḥ ityeṣa mṛgayāṃ gāntuṃ caturaṅgabalānvitaḥ  BndP saṃrajyamāne gagane bandhūkakusumāruṇaiḥ tārājāladyutiharaiḥ samantādaruṇāṃśubhiḥ  BndP mandaṃ vījati proddhūtaketakīvanarājibhiḥ prābhātike gandhavahe kumudākarasaṃspṛśi  BndP vayāṃsi narmadātīratarunīḍāśrayeṣu ca vyāharansvākulā vāco manaḥśrotrasukhāvahāḥ  BndP narmadātīratīrthaṃ tadavatīryāghahāriṇi tattoye munivṛndeṣu gṛṇātsubrahma śāśvatam  BndP vidhivatkṛtamaitreṣu sannivṛtya sarittaṭāt āśamaṃ prati gacchatsu munimukhyeṣu karmiṣu  BndP pratyekaṃ vīrapatnīṣu vyagrāsu gṛhakarmasu homārthaṃ munikalpābhirduhyamānāsu dhenuṣu  BndP sthāne munikumāreṣu taṃ dohaṃ hi nayatsu ca agnihotrākule jāte sarvabhūtasukhāvahe  BndP vikasatsu sarojeṣu gāyatsu bhramareṣu ca vāśatsu nīḍānniṣpatya patatriṣu samantataḥ  BndP anati vyagramattebhaturaṅgarathagāminām gātrālhādavivarddhanyāṃ velāyāṃ mandavāyunā  BndP gacchatsu cāśramopāntaṃ prasūnajalahāriṣu svādhyā yadakṣairbahubhirajināṃbaradhāribhiḥ  BndP samyak prayojyamāneṣu savitaryudayaṃ yāti naiśe tamasi naśyati  BndP tārakāsu vilīnāsu kāṣṭhāsu vimalāsu ca kṛtamaitrādiko rājā mṛgayāṃ haihayeśvaraḥ  BndP niryayau nagarāttasmātpurohitasamanvitaḥ balaiḥ sarvaiḥ samuditaiḥ svabalaughapadakṣepaprakṣuṇṇāvanireṇubhiḥ  BndP yayau saṃcchādayanvyoma vimānaśatasaṃkulam saṃpravaśya vanaṃ ghoraṃ vindhyodrerbalasaṃcayaiḥ  BndP bhṛśaṃ vilolayā māsa samantādrājasattamaḥ parivārya viddhasarvāṅgāḥ siṃharkṣaśarabhādayaḥ  BndP vasudhāmanvakīryanta śoṇitārdrāḥ samantataḥ evaṃ savāguraiḥ kaiścitpatadbhiḥ patitairapi  BndP śvabhiścānudrutaiḥ kaiściddhāvamānaistathā mṛgaiḥ āttairvikrośamānaiśca bhītaiḥ prāṇabhayāturaiḥ  BndP yugāpāye yathātyarthaṃ vanamākulamābabhau varāhasiṃhaśārdūlaśvāvicchaśakulāni ca  BndP camarīrurugomāyugavayarkṣavṛkānbahūn hatvā mṛgān ghorānhiṃsraprāyānaśeṣataḥ  BndP śrameṇa mahatā yuktā babhūvurnṛpasainikāḥ madhye dinakare prāpte sasainyaḥ sa tadā nṛpaḥ  BndP narmadāṃ dharmasaṃtaptaḥ pipāsuragamacchanaiḥ avatīya suciramuttīrya sabalo nṛpaḥ  BndP viśaśrāma ca tattīre tarukhaṇḍopamaṇḍite ālaṃbapāne tigmāṃśau sasainyaḥ sānugo nṛpaḥ  BndP niścakrāma puraṃ gantuṃ vindhyādrivanagahvarāt sa gacchanneva dadṛśe BndP niṣasādāsane śubhra purastasya mahāmuneḥ tamāsīnaṃ nṛpavaraṃ kuśāsanagato muniḥ  BndP papraccha kuśalapraśnaṃ putramitrādibandhuṣu saha saṃkathayaṃstena rājñā munivarottamaḥ  BndP sthitvā nāticiraṃ kālamātithyārthaṃ nyamantrayat tataḥ sa rājā suprīto jamadagni mabhāṣata  BndP maharṣe dehi me nujñāṃ gamiṣyāmi svakaṃ puram samagravāhanabalo hyahaṃ tasmānmahāmune  BndP kartu na śakyamā tithyaṃ tvayā vanyāśinā vane athavā tvaṃ tapaḥśaktyā kartumātithyamadya me  BndP śaknoṣyapi purīṃ gantuṃ māmanujñāturhasi anyathā cetkhalaiḥ sainyairatyarthaṃ munisattama  BndP tapasvināṃ bhavetpīḍā niyamakṣayakārikā vasiṣṭha uvācaityevamuktaḥ sa munistaṃ prāhasthīyatāṃ kṣaṇam  BndP sarvaṃ saṃpādayithye hamātithyaṃ sānugasya te ityuktvāhūya tāṃ dogdhrīmuvācāyaṃ mamātithiḥ  BndP upāga tastvayā tu nṛpatau tasminnakṛtavraṇasaṃyutaḥ samidānayanārthāya rāmo pi prayayau vanam  BndP tataḥ sa mantrī sabalaḥ samāsādya tadāśramam praṇamya muniśārdūlamidaṃ vacanamabravīt  BndP candragupta uvācabrahmannṛpatinājñaptaṃ rājā tu bhuvi ratnabhāk ratnabhūtā ca dhenuḥ sā bhuvi dogdhrīṣvanuttamā  BndP tasmādratnaṃsuvarṇaṃ vā mūlyamuktvā yathocitam ādāya goratnabhūtāṃ dhenuṃ me dātumarhasi  BndP jamadagniruvācahomadhenuriyaṃ mahyaṃ na dātavyā hi kasyacit rājā vadānyaḥ sa kathaṃ brahmasvamabhivāñchati  BndP mantryuvācaratnabhāktvaṃna nṛpatirddhenuṃ te pratikāṅkṣati gavāyutena tasmāttvaṃ tasmai tāṃ dātumarhasi  BndP jamadagniruvācakrayavikrayayornāhaṃ karttā jātu kathañcana havirdhānīṃ ca vai tasmānnotsahe dātumañjasā  BndP mantryuvācarājyārdhenātha vā brahmansakalenāpi bhūbhṛtaḥ dehi dhenumimāmekāṃ tatte śreyo bhaviṣyati  BndP jamadagniruvācajīvannāhaṃ tu dāsyāmi vāsavasyāpi durmate guruṇā yācitaṃ kiṃ te vacasā nṛpateḥ punaḥ  BndP mantryuvācatvameva svecchayā rājñe dehi dhenuṃ suhṛttayā yathā balena nītāyāṃ tasyāṃ tvaṃ kiṃ kariṣyasi  BndP jamadagniruvācadātā dvijānāṃ nṛpatiḥ sa yadyapyāhariṣyati vipro haṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi svecchāvitaraṇaṃ vinā  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācaityevamuktaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ sa mantrī pāpacetanaḥ prasahya netumārebhe munestasya payasvinīm  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe voyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīyaupoddhātapāde ṣṭāviṃśatitamo dhyāyaḥ  vasiṣṭha uvācajamadagnistato bhūyastamuvāca ruṣānvitaḥ brahmasvaṃ nāpaharttavyaṃ puruṣeṇa vijānatā  BndP prasahya gāṃ me harato pāpamāpsyasi durmate āyurjāne parikṣīṇaṃ na cedetatkariṣyati  BndP balādicchasi yannetuṃ tanna śakyaṃ kathañcana svayaṃ vā yadi sāyucyedvinaśiṣyati pārthivaḥ  BndP dānaṃ vināpaharaṇaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ tapasvinām śatāyuṣorjunādanyaḥ ko nvicchati jijīviṣuḥ  BndP ityuktastena saṃkruddhaḥ sa mantrīkālacoditaḥ baddhvā tāṃ gāṃ dṛḍhaiḥ pāśairvicakarṣa balānvitaḥ  BndP jamadagniratha krodhādbhāvikarmapracoditaḥ rurodha taṃ yathāśakti vikarṣantaṃ pāyasvinīm  BndP jīvanna pratimokṣyāmi gāmenāmityamarṣitaḥ jagrāha sudṛḍhaṃ kaṇṭhe vāhubhyāṃ tāṃ mahāmuniḥ  BndP tataḥ krodhaparītātmā candragupto tinirghṛṇaḥ utsārayadhvamityenamādideśa svasainikān  BndP apradhṛṣyatamaṃ loke tamṛṣiṃ
