vyathitaḥkṣamayānvitaḥ na cukrodhākrodhanatvaṃ sato hi paramaṃ dhanam  BndP sa ca śaktaḥ svatapasā saṃharttumapi rakṣitum jagatsarvaṃ kṣayaṃ tasya cintayanna pracukrudhe  BndP sapūrvaṃ krodhano tyarthaṃ māturarthe prasāditaḥ rāmeṇābhūttato nityaṃ śānta eva mahātapāḥ  BndP sa hanyamānaḥ subhṛśaṃ cūrṇitāṅgāsthivandhanaḥ nipapāta mahātejā dharaṇyāṃ gatacetanaḥ  BndP tasminmunau nipatite sa durātmā viśaṅkitaḥ kiṅkarānādiśacchīghraṃ dhenorānayane balāt  BndP tataḥ savatsāṃ tā dhenuṃ baddhvā pāśairdṛḍhairnṛpaḥ kaśābhirabhihanyanta cakṛṣuśca ninīṣayā  BndP ākṛṣyamāṇā bahubhiḥ kaśābhirlaguḍairapi hanyamānā bhṛśaṃ taiśca cukrudhe ca payasvinī  BndP vyathitātikaśāpātaiḥ krodhena mahātānvitā ākṛṣya pāśān sudṛḍhān kṛtvātmānamamocayat  BndP vimuktapāśavandhāsā sarvato bhivṛtā balaiḥ huṃhāravaṃ prakurvāṇā sarvato hyapatadruṣā  BndP viṣāṇakhurapucchāgrairabhihatya samantataḥ rājamantribalaṃ sarvaṃ vyadrāvayadamarṣitā  BndP vidrāvya kiṅkarānsarvāṃstarasaiva payasvinī paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ gaganaṃ pratyapadyata  BndP tataste bhagnasaṃkalpāḥ saṃbhagnakṣatavigrahāḥ prasahya baddhvā tadvatsaṃ jagmurevātinirghṛṇāḥ  BndP payasvinīṃ vinā vatsaṃ gṛhītvā kiṅkaraiḥ saha sa pāpastarasā rājñaḥ sannidhiṃ samupāgamat  BndP gatvā samīpaṃ nṛpateḥ praṇamyāsmai praśaṃsakṛt tadvrattāntamaśeṣeṇa vyācacakṣe sasādhvasaḥ  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyamabhāge tṛtīyaupoddhātapāderjunopākhyāne ekonatriṃśattamo dhyāyaḥ  vāsiṣṭha uvācaśrusvaitatsakalaṃ rājā jamadagnivadhādikam udvignacetāḥ subhṛśaṃ cintayāmāsa naikadhā  BndP aho me sunṛsaṃsasya lokayorubhayorapi brahmasvaharaṇe vāñchā taddhatyā cātigarhitā  BndP aho nāśrauṣamasyāhaṃ brāhmaṇasya vijānataḥ vacanaṃ tarhi tāṃ jahyāṃ vimūḍhātmā gatatrapaḥ  BndP iti saṃcitayannaṃva hṛdayena vidūyatā svapuraṃ praticakrāma sabalaḥ sānugastataḥ  BndP purīṃ pratigate rājñi tasminsaparivārake āśramātsahasā rājanviniścakrāma reṇukā  BndP atha sakṣatasarvāṅgaṃ rudhireṇa pariplutam niśceṣṭaṃ paritaṃ bhūmau dadarśa patimātmanaḥ  BndP tataḥ sā vihataṃ matvā bharttāraṃ gatacetanam anvāhatevāśaninā mūrchitānyapatadbhuvi  BndP cirādiva punarbhūmerutthāyātīva duḥkhitā patitvotthāya sā bhūyaḥ susvaraṃ praruroda ha  BndP vilalāpa ca sātyarthaṃ dharaṇīdhūlidhūsarā aśrupūrmamukhī dīnā patitā śokasāgare  BndP hā nātha piya dharmajña dākṣiṇyāmṛtasāgara hā dhigatyantaśānta tvaṃ naiva kāṅkṣeta cedṛśam  BndP āśramādabhiniṣkrāntaḥ sahasā vyasānarṇave kṣiptvānāthāmagādhe māṃ kva ca yāto si mānada  BndP satāṃ sāptapade maitre muṣitāhaṃ tvayā saha yāsi yatra tvamekākī tatra māṃ netumarhasi  BndP dṛṣṭvā tvāmīdṛśāvasthamacirāddhṛdayaṃ mama na dīryate mahābhāga kaṭhināḥ khalu yoṣitaḥ  BndP ityevaṃ vilapantī sā rudatī ca muhurmuhuḥ cukrośa rāmarāmeti bhṛśaṃ duḥkhapariplutā  BndP tāvadrāmo pi sa vanātsamidbhārasamanvitaḥ akṛtavraṇasaṃyuktaḥ svāśramāya nyavarttata  BndP apaśyadbhayaśaṃsīni nimittāni bahūni saḥ paśyannudvignahṛdayastūrṇaṃ prāpāśramaṃ vibhuḥ  BndP tamāyāntamabhiprekṣya rudatī sā bhṛśāturā navibhūteva śokena prārudadreṇukā punaḥ  BndP rāmasya purato rājanbhartṛvyasanapīḍitā ubhābhyāmapi hastābhyāmudaraṃ samatāḍayat  BndP mārge viditavṛttāntaḥ samyagrāmo pi mātaram kurarīmiva śokārttā dṛṣṭvā duḥkhamupeyivān  BndP dhairyamāropya medhāvī duḥśaśokapariplutaḥ netrābhyāmaśrupūrṇābhyāṃ tasthau bhūmāvardhomukhaḥ  BndP taṃ tathāgatamālokya rāmaṃ prāhākṛtavraṇaḥ kimidaṃ bhṛguśārdūla naitatvayyupapādyate  BndP na tvādṛśā mahābhāga bhṛśaṃ śocanti kutracit dhṛtimanto mahāntastu duḥkhaṃ kurvati na vyaye  BndP śokaḥ sarvendriyāṇāṃ hi pariśoṣapradāyakaḥ tyaja śokaṃ mahābāho na tatpātraṃ bhavadṛśāḥ  BndP ehikāmuṣmikārthānāṃ nūnamekāntarodhakaḥ śokastasyāvakāśaṃ tvaṃ kathaṃ tdṛdi niyacchasi  BndP tattvaṃ dhairyadhano bhūtvā parisāṃtvaya mātaram rudatīṃ bata vaidhavyaśaṃ kāpahatacetanām  BndP naivāgamanamastīha vyatikrāntasya vastunaḥ tasmādatītamakhilaṃ tyaktvā kṛtyaṃ vicintaya  BndP ityevaṃ sāṃtvamānaśca tena duḥśasamanvitaḥ rāmaḥ saṃstaṃbhayāmāsa śanairātmānamātmanā  BndP duḥkhaśokaparītā hi reṇukā tvarudanmuhaḥ triḥsaptakṛtvo hastābhyāmudaraṃ samatāḍayat  BndP tāvattadantikaṃ rāmaḥ samabhyetyāśrulocanaḥ rudatīmalamaṃbeti sāṃtvayāmāsa mātaram  BndP uvācāpanayanduḥkhādbhartṛśokaparāyaṇām triḥsaptakṛtvo yadidaṃ tvayā vakṣaḥ samāhatam  BndP tāvatasaṃkhyamahaṃ tasmātkṣattrajāramaśeṣataḥ haniṣye bhuvi sarvatra satyametadbravimi te  BndP tasmāttvaṃ śokamutsṛjya dhairyamātiṣṭa sāṃpratam nāstyeva nūnamāyātamatikrāntasya vastunaḥ  BndP ityuktā reṇukā tena bhṛśaṃ duḥkhānvitāpi sā kṛcchrāddhairyaṃ samālaṃbya tatheti pratyabhāṣata  BndP tato rāmo mahābāhuḥ pituḥ saha sahodaraiḥ agnau satkarttumārebhe dehaṃ rājanyathavidhi  BndP bhartṛśokaparitāṅgī reṇukāpi dṛḍhavratā putrānsarvānsamāhūya tvidaṃ vacanamabravīt  BndP reṇukovāca ahaṃ vapitaraṃ putrāḥ svargataṃ puṇyaśīlinam anugantumihecchāmi tanme nujñātumarhatha  BndP asahyaduḥśaṃ vaidhavyaṃ sahamānā kathaṃ punaḥ bhartrā virahitā tena pravarttiṣye vininditā  BndP tasmādanugamiṣyāmi bharttāraṃ dayitaṃ mama yathā tena pravarttiṣye paratrāpi sahāniśam  BndP jvalantamimamevāgniṃ saṃpraviśya cirādiva bharturmama bhaviṣyāmi pitṛlokapriyātithiḥ  BndP anuvādamṛte kimidaṃ vṛttaṃ tatsarvaṃ te nyavedayan  BndP tacchrutvā sa bhṛguḥ śīghraṃ jalamādāya mantravit saṃjīvinyā vinayā taṃ siṣeca proccarannidam  BndP yajñasya tapaso vīya mamāpi śubhamasti cet tenāsau BndP punīhyātmakulaṃ svasya caraṇāṃbukaṇairvibho ityuktvā sahasānītaṃ rāmeṇārdhyaṃ mudānvitaḥ  BndP pradadau pādayostasya bhaktyāna mitakandharaḥ tajjalaṃ śirasādhatta sakuṭuṃbo mahāmanāḥ  BndP atha satkṛtya sa bhṛguṃ papraccha vinayānvitaḥ bhagavan kiṃ kṛtaṃ tena rājñā duṣṭena pātakam  BndP yasyātithyaṃ hi kṛtavānahaṃ samyagvidhānataḥ sādhubuddhyāsa duṣṭātmā kiṃ cakāra mahāmate  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācaevaṃ sa pṛṣṭo matimānbhṛguḥ sarvavidīśvaraḥ ciraṃ dhyātvā samālocya kāraṇaṃ prāha bhūpate  BndP bhṛguruvācaśṛṇu tāta mahābhāga bījamasya hi karmaṇaḥ yaśca vai kṛtavānpāpaṃ sarvajñasya tavānagha  BndP śaptaḥ purā vasiṣṭhena nāśārthaṃ sa mahīpatiḥ dvijāparādhato mūḍha vīryaṃ te vinaśiṣyate  BndP tatkathaṃ vacanaṃ tasya bhaviṣyatyanyathā muneḥ ayaṃ rāmo mahāvīryaṃ prasahyanṛpapuṅgavam  BndP haniṣyati mahābāho pratijñāṃ kṛtavānpurā yasmāduraḥ pratihataṃ tvayā mātarmamāgrataḥ  BndP ekaviṃśativāraṃ hi bhṛśaṃ duḥkhaparītayā triḥ saptakṛtvo niḥkṣatrāṃ kariṣye pṛthivīmimām  BndP ato yaṃ vāryamāṇo pi tvāyā pitrā nirantaram bhāvinorthasya ca balātkariṣyatyeva mānada  BndP sa tu rājā mahābhāgo vṛddhānāṃ paryupāsitā dattātreyāddhareraṃśāllabdhabodho mahāmatiḥ  BndP sākṣādbhakto mahātmā bhārgavacarite triṃśattamo dhyāyaḥ  sagara uvācabrahmaputra mahābhāga vada bhārgavaceṣṭitam yaccakāra mahāvīryyo rājñaḥ kruddho hi karmaṇā  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācagate tasminmahābhāge bhṛgo pitṛparāyaṇaḥ rāmaḥ provāca saṃkruddho muñcañchvāsānmuharmuhuḥ  BndP paraśurāma uvācaaho paśyata mūḍhatvaṃrājño hyutpathagāminaḥ kārttavīryasya yo vidvāṃścakre brahmavadhodyamam  BndP daivaṃ hi balavanmanye yatprabhāvāccharīriṇaḥ śubhaṃ vāpyaśubhaṃ sarve prakurvanti vimohitāḥ  BndP śṛṇavantu ṛṣayaḥ sarve pratijñā kriyate mayā kārttavīryaṃ nihatyājau piturvairaṃ prasādhaye  BndP yadi rājā suraiḥ sarvairindrāddairdānavaistathā rakṣiṣyate tathāpyenaṃ saṃhariṣyāmi nānyathā  BndP evamuktaṃ samākarṇya rāmeṇa samuhātmanā jamadagniruvācedaṃ putraṃ sāhasabhāṣiṇam  BndP jamadagniruvācaśruṇu rāma mahābhāgā ye ca dāntāstapasvinaḥ teṣāṃ caivākṣayā lokāḥ satataṃ sādhukāriṇām  BndP yastu duṣṭaistu daṇḍādyairvacasāpi ca tāḍitaḥ na ca kṣobhamavāpnoti sa sādhuḥ parikīrtthate  BndP tāḍayettāḍayantaṃ samādiṣṭaṃ vijñāya nṛpanandana rāmaḥ provāca pitaraṃ kṣamāśīlamarindamam  BndP paraśurāma uvācaśṛṇu tāta mahāprājña viptiṃ mama sāṃpratam bhavatā śama uddiṣṭaḥ sādhūnāṃ sumahātmanām  BndP ma śamaḥ sādhudīneṣu guruṣvīśvarabhāvanaiḥ karttavyo duṣṭaceṣṭeṣu na śamaḥ sukhado bhavet  BndP tasmādasya vadhaḥ kāryaḥ kārttavīryasya vai mayā dehyājñāṃ mānanīyādya sādhaye vairamātmanaḥ  BndP jamadagniruvācaśṛṇu rāma mahābhāga vaco mama samāhitaḥ kariṣyasi yathā bhāvi tathā naivānyathā bhavet  BndP ito vrajatvaṃ brahmāṇāṃ bṛccha tāta hitāhitam sa yadvadiṣyati vibhustatkarttā nātra saṃśayaḥ dravyāṇyaharaharbhṛgoḥ ānīya kānanādbhūpa prāyacchadakṛtavraṇaḥ  BndP satataṃ dhyānasaṃyukto rāmo matimatāṃ varaḥ ārādhayāmāsa vibhuṃ kṛṣṇaṃ kalmaṣanāśanam  BndP tasyaivaṃ yajamānasya rāmasya jagatīpate gataṃ varṣaśataṃ tatra dhyānayuktasya nityadā  BndP ekadā tu mahārāja rāmaḥ snātuṃ gato mahān madhyamaṃ puṣkaraṃ tatra dadarśāśvaryamuttamam  BndP mṛga ekaḥ samāyāto mṛgya yuktaḥ palāyitaḥ vyādhasya mṛgayāṃ prāpto dharmatapto tipīḍitaḥ  BndP pipāsito mahābhāga jalapānasamutsukaḥ rāmasya paśyatastatra sarasastaṭamāgataḥ  BndP paścānmṛgī samāyātā bhītā sā cakitekṣaṇā ubho tau pibatastatra bhṛgunandanāt  BndP ayaṃ rāmo mahāvīro duṣṭānāmantakārakaḥ kathametasya hanmyetau paśyato mṛgayāmṛgau  BndP iti cintā samāviṣṭo vyādho rājanyasattama tasthau tatraiva rāmasya bhayātsaṃtrastamānasaḥ  BndP rāmastu tau mṛgoṃ dṛṣṭvā pibantau sabhyaṃ jalam tarkayāmāsa medhāvī kimatra bhayakāraṇam  BndP naivātra vyāghrasenādo na ca vyādho hi dṛśyate kenaitau kāraṇenāho śaṅkitau cakitekṣaṇau  BndP atha vacane mṛgyā rāmar śanatuṣṭayā mṛgaścovāca harṣeṇa samāviṣṭaḥ priyāṃ svakām  BndP evameva mahābhāge yadvai vadasi bhāmini jāne hamapi rāmasya prabhāvaṃ sumahātmanaḥ  BndP yo yaṃ saṃdṛśyate cāsya śubhāśubhanidarśakam adyaiva viditaṃ me bhūdrāsasyāsya mahātmanaḥ  BndP caritaṃ puṇyadaṃ caiva pāpaghnaṃ śṛṇvatāmidam yadyatkariṣyate caiva tadapi jñānagocaram  BndP yottamā bhaktirākhyātā tāṃ vinā naiva siddhyati kavacaṃ mantrasahitaṃ hyapi varṣāyutāyutaiḥ  BndP yadyayaṃ bhārgavo bhadre hyagastyānugrahaṃ labhet kṛṣṇapremāmṛtaṃ nāma stotramuttamabhaktidam  BndP jñātvā ca lapsyate siddhiṃ mantrasya kavacasya ca sa munirjñātatattvārthaḥ sānukaṃpo bhayapradaḥ  BndP upadekṣyati caivainaṃ tattvajñānaṃ mudāvaham śrīkṛṣṇacāritaṃ sarvaṃ nāmabhirgrathitaṃ yataḥ  BndP kṛṣṇapremāmṛtastotrājjñāsyate sya mahāmatiḥ tataḥ saṃsiddha kavacau rājanaṃ haihayādhipam  BndP hatvā saputrāmātyaṃ ca sasuhṛdbalavāhanam triḥ saptakṛtvo nirbhūpāṃ kariṣyatyavanīṃ priya  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācaevamuktvā mṛgo rājanvirarāma mṛgīṃ tataḥ ātmano mṛgabhāvasya kāraṇaṃ jñātavāṃśca ha  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīyaupoddhātapāde bhārgavacarite catustriṃśattamo viceṣṭitam  BndP bhūtaṃ bhavadbhaviṣyaṃ ca nārāyaṇakathānvitam punaḥ prapaccha kiṃ nātha tanme vada savistaram  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācaśṛṇu rājanpravakṣyāmi mṛgasya caritaṃ mahat yathā pṛṣṭaṃ tayā so syai nipātya bhūmau rathamārddayattribhiḥ  BndP tyaktvā rathaṃ bhūmigataṃ ca maṅgalaṃ paraśvadhenāśu jaghāna mūrddhani sa bhinnaśīrṣo rudhiraṃ vamanmuhurmarcchāmavāpyātha mamāra ca kṣaṇāt  BndP tatsainyamastreṇa ca saṃpradagdhaṃ vināśamāyādatha bhasmasātkṣaṇāt tasminnipatite rājñi candravaṃśasamudbhave  BndP maṅgale nṛpatiśreṣṭhe rāmo harṣamupāgataḥ  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyama bhāge tṛtīyaupoddhātapāde bhārgavacarite aṣṭātriṃśattamo dhyāyaḥ  vasiṣṭha uvācamatsyarāje nipatite rājā yuddhaviśāradaḥ rājendrānprerayāmāsa kārttavīryo mahābalaḥ  BndP bṛhadbalaḥ somadatto vidarbho mithileśvaraḥ niṣadhādhipatiścaiva magadhādhipatistathā  BndP āyayuḥ samare yoddhaṃ bhārgavedreṇa bhūpate varṣantaḥ śarajālāni nānāyuddhaviśāradāḥ  BndP vīrābhimāninaḥ sarve haihayasyājñayā tadā pinākahastaḥ sa bhṛgurjvaladagniśikhopamaḥ  BndP cikṣepa nāgapāśaṃ ca ābhimantrya śarottamam tadastraṃ bhārgave dreṇa kṣiptaṃ saṃgrāmamūrddhani  BndP cakartta gāruḍāstreṇa somadatto mahābalaḥ tataḥ kruddho mahābhāgo rāmaḥ śatruvidāraṇaḥ  BndP rudradattena śūlena somadattaṃ jaghāna ha bṛhadbalaṃ ca gadayā vidarbhaṃ muṣṭinā tathā  BndP maithilaṃ mudgareṇaiva śaktyā ca niṣadhādhipam māgadhañcaraṇāghātairastrajālena sainikān  BndP nihatya nikhilāṃ senāṃ saṃhārāgnisamīraṇe dudrāva kārttavīryaṃ ca jāmadagnyo mahābalaḥ  BndP dṛṣṭvā taṃ yoddhumāyāntaṃ rājāno nye mahārathāḥ kāryyākāryavidhānajñāḥ pṛṣṭe kṛtvā ca haihayam  BndP rāmeṇa yuyudhuścaiva darśayantaśca sauhṛdam kānyakubjāśca śataśaḥ saurāṣṭrāvantayastathā  BndP cakruśca śarajālāni rāmasya ca samantataḥ śarajālāvṛtasteṣāṃ rāmaḥ saṃgrāmamūrddhani  BndP na cādṛśyata rājendra tadā sa tvakṛtavraṇaḥ sasmāra rāmacaritaṃ yaduktaṃ hariṇena vai  BndP kuśalaṃ bhārgavendrasya yācamāno hariṃ muniḥ etasminneva kāle tu rāmaḥ śastrāstrakovidaḥ  BndP vidhūya śarajālāni vāyavyāstreṇa mantravit udatiṣṭhadraṇākāṅkṣī nīhārādiva bhāskaraḥ  BndP trirātraṃ samare rāmastaiḥ sārddhaṃ yuyudhe balī dvādaśākṣauhiṇīstatra ciccheda laghuvikramaḥ  BndP rambhāstambhavanaṃ yadvat paraśvadhavarāyudhaḥ sarvāṃstānbhūpavargāṃśca tadīyaśca mahācamūḥ  BndP dṛṣṭvā vinihatāṃ tena rāmeṇa sumahātmanā ājagāma mahāvīryaḥ sucandraḥ sūryavaṃśajaḥ  BndP lakṣarājanyasaṃyuktaḥ saptākṣauhiṇisaṃyutaḥ tatrānekamahāvīrā garjantastoyadā iva  BndP kaṃpayanto bhuvaṃ rājan yuyudhurbhārgaveṇa ca teḥ prayuktāni śastrāṇi mahāstrāṇi ca bhūpate  BndP kṣaṇena nāśayāmāsa bhārgavendraḥ pratāpavān gṛhītvā paraśuṃ divyaṃ kālātakayamopamam  BndP kālayansakalā senāṃ ciccheda bhugunandanaḥ karṣakastu yathā kṣetre pakvaṃ dhānyaṃ tathā tṛṇam  BndP niśeṣayati dātreṇa tathā rāmeṇa tatkṛtam lakṣarājanyasainyaṃ tadadṛṣṭvā rāmeṇa dāritam  BndP sucandraḥ pṛthivīpālo yuyudhe saṃgare nṛpa tāvubhau tatra saṃkṣubdhau nānāśastrāstrakovidau  BndP yuyudhāte mahāvīrau munīśanṛpatīśvarau rāmo smai yāni śastrāṇi cikṣepāstrāṇi cāpi hi  BndP tāni sarvāṇi ciccheda sucandro yuddha paṇḍitaḥ tataḥ kruddho raṇe rāmaḥ sucandraṃ pṛthivīśvaram  BndP kṛtapratikṛtābhijñaṃ jñātvopaspṛśya vāryatha nārāyaṇāstraṃ viśikhe saṃdadhe cānivāritam  BndP tadastraṃ śatasūryābhaṃ kṣiptaṃ rāmeṇa dhīmatā hṛṣṭottīrya rathātsadyaḥ sucandraḥ praṇanāma ha  BndP sarvāstrapūjyaṃ taccāpi nārāyaṇavinirmitam tamevaṃ praṇataṃ tyaktvā yathau nārāyamantikam  BndP vismito bhūttadā rāmaḥ samare śatrasūdanaḥ dṛṣṭvā vyarthaṃ mahāstraṃ tadbhūpaṃ svasthaṃ vilokya ca  BndP rāmaḥ śaktiṃ ca musalaṃ tomaraṃ paṭṭiśaṃ tathā gadāṃ ca paraśuṃ kopācchikṣepa nṛpamūrddhani  BndP jagrāha tāni sarvāṇi sucandro līlayaiva hi cikṣepa śivaśūlaṃ ca rāmo nṛpataye yadā  BndP babhūva puṣpamālāṃ ca tacchūlaṃ nṛpatergale dadarśa ca purastasya bhadrakālīṃ jagatprasūm  BndP vahantīṃ muṇḍamālāṃ ca vikaṭāsyāṃ bhayaṅkarīm siṃhasthāṃ ca trinetrāṃ ca triśūlavaradhāriṇīm  BndP dṛṣṭvā vihāya śastrāstraṃ namaskṛtya samaiḍata rāma uvācanamostu te śaṅkaravallabhāyai jagatsavitryai samalaṅkṛtāyai  BndP nānāvibhūṣābhiribhārigāyai prapannarakṣāvihitodyamāyai dakṣaprasūtyai himavadbhavāyai maheśvarārddhaṅgasamāsthitāyai  BndP kālyai kalānāthakalādharāyai bhaktapriyāyai bhuvanādhipāyai tārābhidhāyai śivatatparāyai gaṇeśvarārādhitapādukāyai  BndP parātparāyai parameṣṭhidāyai tāpatrayonmūlanacintanāyai jagaddhitāyāstapuratrayāyai bālādikāyai tripurābhidhāyai  BndP samastavidyāsuvilāsadāyai jagajjananyai nihitāhitāyai bakānanāyai bahusākhyadāyai vidhvastanānāsuradānvāyai  BndP varābhayālaṅkṛtadorlatāyai samastagīrvāṇanamaskṛtāyai pītāṃbarāyai pavanāśugāyai śubhapradāyai śivasaṃstutāyai  BndP nāgārigāyai navakhaṇḍapāyai nīlācalābhāṃ galasatprabhāyai laghukramāyai lalitābhidhāyai lekhādhipāyai lavaṇākarāyai  BndP lolekṣaṇāyai layavarjitāyai lākṣārasālaṅkṛtapaṅkajāyai ramābhidhāyai ratisupriyāyai rogāpahāyai racitākhilāyai  BndP rājyapradāyai ramaṇotsukāyai ratnaprabhāyai rucirāṃbarāyai namo namaste parataḥ purastāt pārśvādharordhvaṃ ca namo namaste  BndP sadā ca sarvatra namo namaste namo namaste khilavigrahāyai prasīda deveśi mama pratijñāṃ purā kṛtāṃ pālaya bhadrakāli  BndP tvameva mātā ca pitā tvameva jagattrayasyāpi namo namaste vasiṣṭha uvācaevaṃ stutā tadā devī bhadrakālī tarasvinī  BndP uvāca bhārgavaṃ prītā varadānakṛtotsavā bhadrakālyuvācavatsa rāma mahābhāga prītāsmi tava sāṃpratam  BndP varaṃ varaya matto yastvayā cābhyarthitā hṛdi rāma uvācamātaryadi varo deyastvayā me bhaktava tsale  BndP tatsucandraṃ jaye yuddhe tavānugrahabhājanam iti me bhihitaṃ devi kuru prītena cetasā  BndP yena kenāpyupāyena jaganmātarnamo stu te bhadrakālyuvācaāgneyāstreṇa rājendraṃ sucandraṃ naya madgṛham  BndP mamātipriyamadyaiva pārṣado me bhavatvayam vasiṣṭha uvācaityuktamākarṇya sa bhārgavendro devyāḥ priyaṃ kartumathodyato bhūt  BndP prāṇānniyamyācamanaṃ ca kṛtvā sucandramuddiśya ca tatsamādadhe astraṃ prayuktaṃ nṛpatervadhāya rāmeṇa rājan prasabhaṃ tadā tat  BndP dagdhvā vapurbhūtamayaṃ tadīyaṃ nināya lokaṃ paradevatāyāḥ tatastu rāmeṇa kṛtapraṇāmā sā bhadrakālo jagadādikartrī  BndP antarhitābhūdatha jāmadagnyastasthau raṇebhūpavadhābhikāṅkṣī  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyabhāge tṛtīyaupoddhātapāde bhārgavacarite ekonacatvāriṃśattamo dhyāyaḥ  vasiṣṭha uvācasucandre patite rājan rājendrāṇāṃ śiromaṇau tatputraḥ puṣkarākṣastu rāmaṃ yoddhumathāgataḥ  BndP sa rathastho mahāvīryaḥ sarvaśastrāstrakovidaḥ abhivīkṣya raṇetyugraṃ rāmaṃ kālātakopamam  BndP cakāra śarajālaṃ ca bhārgavendrasya sarvataḥ muhūrttaṃ jāmadagnyo pi bāṇaiḥ saṃjhadito bhavat  BndP tato niṣkamya sahasā bhārgavendro mahābalaḥ śarabandhānmahārāja samudaikṣata sarvataḥ  BndP dṛṣṭvā taṃ puṣkārākṣaṃ tu sucandratanayaṃ tadā krodhamāhārayāmāsa didhakṣanniva pāvakaḥ  BndP sa krodhena samāviṣṭo vāruṇaṃ samavāsṛjat tato meghāḥ samutpannā garjanto bhairavānnavān  BndP vavṛṣurjaladhārābhiḥ plāvayanto dharāṃ nṛpa puṣkarākṣo mahāvīryo vāyavyāstrumavāsṛjat  BndP tena te darśanaṃ nītāḥ sadya eva balāhakāḥ atha rāmo bhṛśaṃ kruddho brāhmaṃ tatrābhisaṃdadhe  BndP puṣkarākṣo pi tenaiva vicakarṣa mahābalaḥ brāhma so pyāhitaṃ dṛṣṭvā daṇḍāhata ivāragaḥ  BndP ghoraṃ paraśumādāya niḥśvasaṃstamadhāvata rāmasyādhāvatastatra puṣkarākṣo dhanurdharaḥ  BndP saṃdadhe pañcaviśikhāndīptāsyānuragāniva ekaikena ca bāṇena hṛdi śīrṣe bhujadvaye  BndP śikhāyāṃ ca kramādbhittvā tastaṃbha bhṛśa māturam sa caivaṃ pīḍīto rāmaḥ puṣkarākṣeṇa saṃyuge  BndP kṣaṇaṃ sthitvā bhṛśaṃ dhāvanparaśuṃ mūrdhnyapatayāt śikhāmārabhya pādāntaṃ puthkarākṣaṃ dvidhākarot  BndP patite śakale bhūmau tatkālaṃ paśyatā nṛṇām āścaryaṃ sumāhajjātaṃ divi caiva divau kasām  BndP vidārya rāmastaṃ krodhātpuṣkarākṣa mahābalam tatsainyamadahatkruddhaḥ pāvako vipinaṃ yathā  BndP yato yato dhāvati bhārgavendro mano nilaujāḥ praharanparaśvadham tatastato vājirathebhamānavā nikṛttagātrāḥ śataśo nipetuḥ  BndP rāmeṇa tatrā tibalena saṃgare nihanyamānāstu paraśvadhena hā tāta mātastviti jalpamāṃnā bhasmībabhūvuḥ suvicūrṇitāstadā  BndP muhūrttamātreṇa ca bhārgaveṇa tatpuṣkarākṣasya balaṃ samagram anekarājanyakulaṃ hateśvaraṃ itaṃ navākṣauhiṇikaṃ bhṛśāturam  BndP patite puṣkarākṣe tu kārttavīryārjunaḥ svayam ājagāma mahāvīryaḥ suvarṇarathamāsthitaḥ  BndP nānāśastrasamākīrṇaṃ nānāratnaparicchadam daśanalvapramāṇaṃ ca śatavājiyutaṃ nṛpaḥ  BndP yute bāhusahasreṇa nānāyudhadhareṇa ca babhau svarlokamārokṣyandehati sukṛtī yathā  BndP putrāstasya mahāvīryāḥ śataṃ yuddhaviśāradāḥ senāḥ saṃvyūhya saṃtasthuḥ saṃgrāme piturājñayā  BndP kārttavīryastu balavānrāmaṃ dṛṣṭvā raṇājire kālāntakayamaprakhyaṃ yoddhuṃ samupacakrame  BndP dakṣe pañcaśataṃ bāṇānvāme pañcaśataṃ dhanuḥ jagrā ha bhārgavendrasya samare jetumudyataḥ  BndP bāṇavarṣaṃ cakārātha rāmasyopari bhūpate yathā balāhako vīra parvatopari varṣati  BndP bāṇavarṣeṇa nenājau satkṛto bhṛgunandanaḥ jagrāha svaghanurdivyaṃ bāṇavarṣaṃ tathākarot  BndP tāvubhauraṇasaṃdṛptau tadā bhārgavahaihayau cakraturyaddhamatulaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam  BndP brahmāstraṃ ca sabhūpālaḥ saṃdadhe raṇamūrddhani vadhāya bhārgavendrasya sarvaśastrāstradhṛgabalī  BndP rāmo pi vāryupaspṛśya brahmaṃ brāhmaya saṃdadhe tato vyomni sadā sakte dve cāpya stre narādhipa  BndP vavṛdhāte jagatprānte tejasā jvalanārkavat trayo lokāḥ sapātālā dṛṣṭvā tanmahadadbhutam  BndP jvaladastrayugaṃ taptā menire syopasaṃyamam rāmastadā vīkṣya jagatpraṇāśaṃ jagannivāsoktamathāsmarattadā  BndP rakṣā vidheyādya mayāsya saṃyamo nivāraṇīyaḥ paramāṃśadhāriṇā iti vyavasya prabhurugratejā netradvayenātha tadastrayugamam  BndP pītvātirāmaṃ jagadākalayya tasthau kṣaṇaṃ dhyānagato mahātmā dhyānaprabhāveṇa tatastu tasya brahmāstrayugmaṃ vigataprabhāvam  BndP papāta bhūmau sahasātha tatkṣaṇaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsvāsthyamupājagāma sa jāmadagnyo mahātāṃ mahīyānsraṣṭuṃ tathā pālayituṃ nihantum  BndP vibhustathāpīha nijaṃprabhāvaṃ gopāyituṃ lokavidhiṃ cakāra dhanurddharaḥ śūratamo mahasvānsadagraṇīḥ saṃsadi tathyavaktā  BndP kalākalāpeṣu kṛtaprayatno vidyāsu śāstreṣu budho vidhijñaḥ evaṃ nṛloke prathayansvabhāvaṃ sarvāṇi kalyāni karoti nityam  BndP sarve tu lokā vijitāstu tena rāmeṇa rājanyaniṣūdanena evaṃ sa rāmaḥ prathitaprabhāvaḥ praśāmayitvā tu tadastrayugmam  BndP punaḥ pravṛtto nidhanaṃ prakartuṃ raṇāgaṇe haihayavaṃśaketoḥ tuṇīrataḥ patriyugaṃ gṛhītvā puṅkhe nidhāyātha dhanurjyakāyām  BndP ālakṣya lakṣyaṃ nṛpakarṇayugmaṃ cakartta cūḍāmaṇihartukāmaḥ sa kṛttakarṇo nṛpatirmahātmā vinirjitāśeṣajagatpravīraḥ  BndP mene nijaṃ vīryamiha praṇaṣṭaṃ rāmeṇa bhūmīśatiraskṛtātmā kṣaṇaṃ dharādhīśatanurvivarṇā gatānubhāvā nṛpaterbabhūva  BndP lekhyeva saccitrakaraprayuktā sudīnacittasya vilakṣyate ga tataḥ sa rājā nijavīryavaibhavaṃ samastalokādhikatāṃ prayātam  BndP vicintya paulastyajayādilabdhaṃ śocannivāsītsa jayābhikāṅkṣīṃ dadhyau punarmīlitalocano nṛpau dattaṃ tamātreyakulapradīpam  BndP yasya prabhāvānugṛhīta ojasā tiraścakārā khilalokapālakān yadāsya hṛdyeṣa mahānubhāvo dattaḥ prayāto na hi darśanaṃ tadā  BndP khinno timātraṃ dharaṇīpatistadā punaḥ punardhyānapathaṃ jagāma sa dhyāyamāno pi na cājagāma datto manogocaramasya rājan  BndP tapasvino dāntatamasya sādhoranāgaso duṣkṛtikāriṇo vibhuḥ evaṃ yadātrestanayo mahātmā dṛṣṭo na ca dhyānapathe nṛpeṇa  BndP tadātiduḥ khena vidūyamānaḥ śokena mohena yuto babhūva taṃ śokamagnaṃ nṛpatiṃ mahātmā rāmo jagādākhilacittadarśī  BndP mā śokabhāvaṃ nṛpate prayāhi naivānuśocanti mahānubhāvāḥ yaste varāyābhavamādisarge sa eva cāhaṃ taṃva sādanāya  BndP samāgatastvaṃ bhavadhīracittaḥ saṃgrāmakāle na viṣādacarcā sarvo hi lokaḥ svakṛtaṃ bhunakti śubhāśubhaṃ daivakṛtaṃ vipāke  BndP anyonako pyasya śubhāśubhasya viparyayaṃ kartumalaṃ nareśa yatte supuṇyaṃ bahujanmasaṃcitaṃ teneha dattasya varārhapātram  BndP jāto bhavānadya tu duṣkṛtasya phalaṃ prabhuṅkṣva tvamihārjitasya gururvimatyāpakṛtastvayā me yatastataḥ karṇanikṛntanaṃ te  BndP kṛtaṃ mayā paśya harantamojasā cūḍāmaṇiṃ māmapatdṛtya te yaśaḥ ityevamuktvā sa bhṛgurmahātmā niyojya bāṇaṃ ca vikṛṣya cāpam  BndP cikṣepa rājñaḥ sa tu lāghavena cchittvā maṇiṃ rāmamamupājagāma tadvīkṣya karmāsya muneḥ sutasya sa cārjuno haihayavaṃśadharttā  BndP samudyato bhūtpunarapyudāyudhastaṃ hantumājau dvijamātmaśatrum śūlaśaktigadācakrakhaḍhgapaṭṭiśatomaraiḥ  BndP nānāpraharaṇaiścānyairājaghāna dvijātmajam sa rāmo lāghavenaiva saṃprakṣiptānyanena ca  BndP śūlādīni cakarttāśu madhya eva nijāśugaiḥ sa rājā vāryupaspṛśya sasarjāgneyamuttamam  BndP astraṃ rāmo vāruṇena śamayāmāsa satvaram gāndharvaṃ vidadhe rājā vāyavyenāhanadvibhum  BndP nāgāstraṃ gāruḍenāpi rāmaściccheda bhūpate dattena dattaṃ yacchūlamavyarthaṃ mantrapūrvakam  BndP jagrāha samare rājā bhārgavasya vadhāya ca tacchūlaṃ śatasūryābhamanivāryaṃ surāsuraiḥ  BndP cikṣepa rāmamuddiśya samagreṇa balena saḥ mūrdhni tadbhārgavasyātha nipapāta mahīpate  BndP tena śūlaprahāreṇa vyathito bhārgavastadā mūrcchāmavāpa rājendra papāta ca hariṃ smaran  BndP patite bhārgave tatra sarve devā bhayākulāḥ samājagmuḥ puraskṛtya brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarān  BndP śaṅkarastu mahājñānī sākṣānmṛtyuñjayaḥ prabhuḥ bhārgavaṃ jīvayāmāsa saṃjīvanyā sa vidyayā  BndP rāmastu cetanāṃ prāpya dadarśa purataḥ surān praṇanāma ca rājendra bhaktyā brahmādikāṃstu tān  BndP te stutā bhārgavendreṇa sadyo darśanamāgatāḥ sa rāmo vāryuspṛśya jajāpa kavacaṃ tu tat  BndP utthitaśca susaṃrabdho nirdahanniva cakṣuṣā smṛtvā pāśupataṃ cāstraṃ śivadattaṃ sa bhārgavaḥ  BndP sadyaḥ saṃhṛtavāṃstattu kārttavīryaṃ mahābalam sa rājā dattabhaktastu viṣṇoścakraṃ sudarśanam praviṣṭo bhasmasājjātaṃ śarīraṃ bāhunandana  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyamabhāge tṛtīyaupoddhātapāde bhārgavacarite kārttavīryavadho nāma catvāriṃśattamo dhyāyaḥ  vasiṣṭha uvācadṛṣṭvā piturvadhaṃ ghoraṃ tatputrāste śataṃ tvarā vārayāmāsuratyugraṃ bhārgavaṃ svabaleḥ pṛthak  BndP ekaikākṣaihiṇīyuktāḥ sarve te yuddhadurmadāḥ saṃgrāmaṃ tumulaṃ cakruḥ saṃrabdhāstu piturvadhāt  BndP rāmastu dṛṣṭvā tatputrāñchūrānraṇaviśāradān paraśvadhaṃ samādāya yuyudhe taiśca saṃgare  BndP tāṃ senāṃ bhagavānrāmaḥ śatākṣauhiṇisaṃmitām nijaghāna tvarāyukto muhurttadvayamātrataḥ  BndP niḥśeṣitaṃ svasainyaṃ tu kuṭhāreṇaiva līlayā dṛṣṭvā rāmeṇa tesarve yuyudhurvīryasaṃmatāḥ  BndP nānāvidhāni divyāni praharanto mahojasaḥ parito maṇḍalaṃ cakrurbhārgavasya mahātmanaḥ  BndP atha rāmo pi balavāṃsteṣāṃ maṇḍalamadhyagaḥ vireje bhagavānsākṣādyathā nābhistu cakragā  BndP nṛtyannivācau virarāja rāmaḥ śataṃ punaste parito bhramantaḥ rejuśca gopī gaṇamadhyasaṃsthaḥ kṛṣṇo yathā tāḥ parito bhramantyaḥ  BndP tadā tu sarve druhiṇapradhānāḥ samāgatāḥ svasvavimānasaṃsthāḥ samākirannandanamālyavarṣaiḥ samantato rāmamahīnavīryam  BndP yaḥ śastrapādādudatiṣṭhata dhvanir huṃkāragarbho divamaspṛśansa vai tauryatrikasyeva śarakṣatāni bhāntīva yadvannakhadantapātāḥ  BndP krandanti śastraiḥ kṣatavikṣatāṅgā gāyanti yadvatkila gītavijñāḥ evaṃ pravṛttaṃ nṛpayuddhamaṇḍalaṃ paśyanti devā bhṛśavismitākṣaḥ  BndP tatastu rāmo vanipālaputrāñjighāṃsurājau vividhāstrapūgaiḥ pṛthakcakārātiba lāṃstu maṇḍaladvicchidya paṅktiṃ prabhurāttacāpaḥ  BndP ekaikaśastānnijaghāna vīrāñchataṃ tadā pañca tataḥ palāyitāḥ śūro vṛṣāsyo vṛṣaśūrasenau jayadhvajaścāpi vibhinnadhairyāḥ  BndP mahābhayenātha parītacitā himādripādāntarakānanaṃ ca pṛthaggatāste suparīpsavo nṛpā na ko pi kāṃsviddadṛśe bhṛśārttaḥ  BndP rāmo pi hatvā nṛpacakramājau rājñaḥ sahāyarthamupāgataṃ ca samanvito sāvakṛtavraṇena sasnau mudāgatya ca narmadāyām  BndP srātvā nityakriyāṃ kṛtvā saṃpūjya vṛṣabhadhvajam pratasthe draṣṭumurvīśa śivaṃ kailāsavāsinam  BndP gurupatnīmumāṃ cāpi sutau skandavināyakau manoyāyī mahātmāsāvakṛtavraṇasaṃyutaḥ  BndP kṛtakāryo mudā yuktaḥ kailāsaṃ prāpya tatkṣaṇam dadarśa tatra nagarīṃ mahatīmalakābhidham  BndP nānāmaṇigaṇākīrṇabhavanairupaśobhitām nānārupadharairyakṣaiḥ śobhitāṃ citrabhūṣaṇaiḥ  BndP nānāvṛkṣasamākīṇairvanaiścopavanairyutām dīrghikābhiḥ sudīrghābhistaḍāgaiścopaśobhitām  BndP sarvato pyāvṛtāṃ bāhye sītayālakanandayā tatra devāṅganāsnānamuktakuṅkumapiñjaram  BndP tṛṣāvira hitāścāṃbhaḥ pibanti kariṇo mudā yatra saṃgītasaṃnādā śrūyante tatratatra ha  BndP gandharvairapsarobhiśca satataṃ sahakāribhiḥ tāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhārgavo rājanmudā paramayā yutaḥ  BndP yayau tadūrdhvaṃ śikharaṃ yatra śevaparaṃ gṛham tato dadarśa rājendra snigdhacchāyaṃ mahāvaṭam  BndP tasyādhastādvarāvāsaṃ susevyaṃ siddhasaṃyutam dadarṃśa tatra prākāraṃ śatayojanamaṇḍalam  BndP nānāratnācitaṃ ramyaṃ bhrātastiṣṭhātra sāṃpratam vināyakacaścaivaṃ śrutvā bhārgavanandanaḥ  BndP pravaktumupacakrāma gaṇeśaṃ tvarayānvitaḥ rāma uvācagatvā hyantaḥpuraṃ bhrātaḥ praṇamya jagadīśvarau  BndP pārvatīśaṅkarau sadyo yāsyāmi nijamandiram kārttavīryaḥ sucandraśca saputrabalabāndhavaḥ  BndP anye sahasraśo bhūpāḥ kāṃbojāḥ paṅlavāḥ śākāḥ kānyakubjāḥ kośaleśā māyāvanto mahābalāḥ  BndP nihatāḥ samare sarve mayā śaṃbhuprasādataḥ tamimaṃ praṇipatyaiva yāsyāmi svagṛhaṃ prati  BndP ityuktvā bhārgavastatra tasthau gaṇapateḥ puraḥ provāca madhuraṃ vākyaṃ bhārgave sa gaṇādhipaḥ  BndP vināyaka uvācajñaṇaṃ tiṣṭa mahābhāga darśanaṃ te bhaviṣyati adya viśveśvaro bhrātarbhavānyā saha varttate  BndP strīpuṃsoryukta yostāta sahaikāsanasaṃsthayoḥ karoti sukhabhaṅgaṃ yo narakaṃ sa vrajeddhruvam  BndP viśeṣatastu pitaraṃ guruṃ vā bhūpatiṃ dvijaḥ rasyaṃ samupāsinaṃ na paśyediti niścayaḥ  BndP kāmato kāmato vāpi paśyedyaḥ suratonmukham strīvicchedo bhavettasya dhruvaṃ saprasu janmasu  BndP śroṇiṃ vakṣaḥ sthalaṃ vaktraṃ yaḥ paśyati parastriyaḥ māturvāpi bhaginyā vā duhituḥ sa narādhamaḥ  BndP bhārgava uvācaaho śrutamapūrvaṃ kiṃ vacanaṃ tava vaktrataḥ brāntyā vinirgataṃ vāpi hāsyārthamathavoditam  BndP kāmināṃ savikārāṇāmetacchāstranidarśanam nirvikārāsya ca śiśorna doṣaḥ kaścideva hi  BndP yāsyāmyantaḥ puraṃ bhrātastava kiṃ tiṣṭha bālaka yathādṛṣṭaṃ kariṣyāmi tatra yatsamayocitam  BndP tatraiva mātā tātaśca tvayā nāma nirūpitau jagatāṃ pitarau tau ca pārvatīparameśvarau  BndP ityuktvā bhārgavo rājannantargantuṃ samudyataḥ vināyakastadotthāya vārayāmāsa satvaram  BndP vāgyuddhaṃ ca tayorāsīnmitho hastavikarṣaṇam dṛṣṭvā sakandastu saṃbhrānto bodhayāmāsa tau tadā  BndP bāhubhyāṃ dvau samudgṛhya pṛthagutsāritau tathā atha kruddho gaṇeśāya bhārgavaḥ paravīrahā paraśvadhaṃ samādāya saprakṣeptuṃ samudyataḥ  BndP taṃ dṛṣṭvā gajānano bhṛguvaraṃ krodhātkṣipantaṃ tvarā svātmārthaṃ paraśuṃ tadā nijakareṇoddhṛtya vegena tu bhūrlokaṃ bhuvaḥ svarapi tasyordhvaṃ maharvaijanaṃ lokaṃ cāpi tapo tha satyamaparaṃ vaikuṇṭhamapyānayat  BndP tasyordhvaṃ ca vidarśayanbhṛguvaraṃ golokamīśātmajo niṣpātyādharalokasaptaka mapītthaṃ darśayāmāsa ca uddhṛtyātha tato hi garbhasalile prakṣaptamātraṃ tvarā bhītaṃ prāṇaparipsumānayadatho tatraiva yatrāsthitaḥ  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyamabhāge tṛtīya upoddhātapāde bhārgavacarite ekacatvāriṃśattamo dhyāyaḥ  vasiṣṭha uvācaevaṃ saṃbhrāmito rāmo gaṇādhīśena bhūpate harṣaśokasamāviṣṭo vicintyātmaparābhavam  BndP gaṇeśaṃ cābhito vīkṣya nirvikāramavasthitam krodhāviṣṭo bhṛśaṃ bhūtvā prākṣipatsvaparaśvadham  BndP gaṇeśastvabhivīkṣyātha pitrā dattaṃ paraśvadham amoghaṃ karttukāmastu vāme taṃ daśane grahīt  BndP sa tu dantaḥ kuṭhāreṇa vicchinno bhūtale patat bhuvi śoṇitasaṃdigdho vajrāhata ivācalaḥ  BndP dantapātena vidvastā sābdhidvīpadharā dharā cakaṃpe pṛthivīpāla lokāstrāsamupāgatāḥ  BndP hāhākāro mahānāsī ddevānāṃ divi paśyatām kārttikeyādayastatra cukruśurbhṛśamāturāḥ  BndP atha kolāhalaṃ śrutvā dantapātadhvaniṃ tathā pārvatīśaṅkarau tatra samājagmaturīśvarau  BndP herambaṃ purato dṛṣṭvā vakratuṇḍaikadantinam papraccha skandaṃ pārvatī kimetaditi kāraṇam  BndP sa tu pṛṣṭastadā mātrā senānīḥ sarvamāditaḥ vṛttāntaṃ kathayāmāsa mātre rāmasya śṛṇvataḥ  BndP sā śrutvodantamakhilaṃ jagatāṃ jananī nṛpa uvāca śaṅkaraṃ ruṣṭā pārvatī prāṇanāyakam  BndP pārvatyuvācaayaṃ te bhārgavaḥ śaṃbho śiṣyaḥ putraḥ samo bhavat tvattolabdhvā paraṃ tejo varma trailokyajidvibho  BndP kārttavīryārjunaṃ saṃkhye jitavānūrjitaṃ nṛpam svakāryaṃ sādhayitvā tu prādāttubhyaṃ ca dakṣiṇām  BndP yatte sutasya daśana dṛṣṭvā śivaḥ saṃhṛṣṭamānasaḥ  BndP praṇipatya yathānyāyaṃ pūjayāmāsa cāgatam praveśyābhyantare veśmarādhayā sahitaṃ vibhum  BndP ratnasiṃhāsane namye sadāraṃ sa nyaveśayat tha tatra gatā devī pārvatī tanayānvitā  BndP nanāma caraṇānprabhvoḥ putrābhyāṃ sahitā mudā tha rāmo pi tatraiva gatvā namitakandharaḥ  BndP pārvatyāścaraṇopānte papātākulamānasaḥ sā yadā nābhyanandattaṃ bhārgavaṃ praṇataṃ puraḥ  BndP tadovāca jagannāthaḥ pārvatīṃ prīṇayangirā  BndP śrīkṛṣma uvācaayi naganaṃ dini ninditacandramukhi tvamimaṃ jamadagnisutam naya nijahastasarojasamarpitamstakamaṅkamanantaguṇe  BndP bhavabhayahāriṇi śaṃbhuvihāriṇi kalmaṣanāśini kuṃbhigate tava caraṇe patitaṃ satataṃ kṛtakilbiṣamapyava dehi varam  BndP śruṇu devi mahābhāge vedoktaṃ vacanaṃ mama yacchrutvā harṣitā nūnaṃ bhaviṣyasi BndP tuṣṭāva prayato bhūtvā nirviśeṣa viśeṣavat advayaṃ dvaitamāpannaṃ nirguṇaṃ saguṇātmakam  BndP rāma uvācaprakṛtivikṛtijātaṃ viśvametadvidhātuṃ mama kiyadanubhātaṃ vaibhavaṃ tatpramātum bodhayatīśavaktraṃvigalatpremāmṛtāsvādanam rāseśī rasikeśvarī ramaṇatdṛnniṣṭhānijānandinī netrī sā paripātu māmavanataṃ rādheti ya kīrtyate  BndP yasyā garbhasamudbhavo hyativirāḍyasyāṃśabhūto virāṭ yannābhyaṃburuhodbhavena vidhinaikāntopadiṣṭenavai sṛṣṭaṃ sarvamidaṃ carācaramayaṃ viśvaṃ ca yadromasu brahmāṇḍāni vibhānti tasyajananī śaśvatprasannāstu sā  BndP pāyādyaḥ sa carācarasya jagato vyāpī vibhuḥ saccidānandābdhiḥ prakaṭasthito vilasati premāndhayā rādhayā kṛṣṇaḥ pūrṇatamo mamopari dayāklinnāntaraḥ stātsadā yenāhaṃ sukṛtī bhavāmi ca bhavāmyānandalīnāntaraḥ  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācastutvaivaṃ jāmadagnyastu virarāma ha tatparam vijñātākhilatattvārtho hṛṣṭaromā kṛtārthavat  BndP athovāca prasannātmā kṛṣṇaḥ kamalalocanaḥ bhārgavaṃ praṇataṃ bhaktyā kṛpāpātraṃ purasthitam  BndP kṛṣma uvācasiddho si bhārgavendra tvaṃ prasādānmama saṃpratam adya prabhṛti vatsāsmiṃlloke śreṣṭhatamo bhava  BndP tubhyaṃ varo mayā dattaḥ purā viṣṇupadāśrame tatsarvaṃ kramato bhāvyaṃ samā bahvīstvayā vibho  BndP dayā vidheyā dīneṣu śreya uttamamicchatā yogaśca sādanīyo vai śatrūṇāṃ nigrahastathā  BndP tvatsamo nāsti loke smiṃstejasā ca balena ca jñānena yaśasā vāpi sarvaśreṣṭhatamo bhavān  BndP atha svagṛhamāsādya pitroḥ śuśrūṣaṇaṃ kuru tapaścara yathākālaṃ tena siddhiḥ karasthitā  BndP rādhotsaṃgātsamutthāpya gaṇeśaṃ rādhikeśvaraḥ āliṅgya gāḍhaṃ rāseṇa maitrīṃ tasya cakāra ha  BndP athobhāvapi saṃprītau tadā rāmagaṇeśvarau kṛṣṇājñayā mahābhāgau babhūvaturarindama  BndP etasminnantare devī rādhā kṛṣṇapriyā satī ubhābhyāṃ ca varaṃ prādātprasannāsyā mudānvitā  BndP rādhovāca  BndP athovāca jaganmātā bhavānī bhavavallabhā vatsa rāma prasannāhaṃ tubhyaṃ kaṃ pradade varam taṃ prabrūhi mahābhāga bhayaṃ tyaktvā sudūrataḥ rāma uvācajanmānta rasahasreṣu yeṣuyeṣu vrajāmyaham  BndP kṛṣṇayorbhavayorbhakto bhaviṣyāmīti dehi me abhedena ca paśyāmi kṛṣṇau cāpi bhavau tathā  BndP pārvatyuvācaevamastu mahābhāga bhakto si bhavakṛṣṇayoḥ cirañjīvī bhavāśu tvaṃ prasādānmama suvrata  BndP athovāca dharādhīśaḥ prasannastamumāpatiḥ praṇataṃ bhārgavendraṃ tu varārhaṃ jagadīśvaraḥ  BndP śiva uvācarāmabhakto si me vatsa yaste datto varo mayā sa bhaviṣyati kārtsyena satyamuktaṃ na cānyathā  BndP adyaprabhṛti loke smin bhavato balavattaraḥ na ko pi bhavatādvatsa tejasvī ca bhavatparaḥ  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācaatha kṛṣṇo pyanujñāpya śivaṃ ca naganandinīm golokaṃ prayayau yuktaḥ śrīdāmnā cāpi rādhayā  BndP atha rāmo pi dharmātmā bhavānīṃ ca bhavaṃ tathā saṃpūjya cābhivādyātha pradakṣiṇamupā kramīt  BndP gaṇeśaṃ kārttikeyaṃ ca natvāpṛcchya ca bhūpate akṛtavraṇasaṃyukto dūrādevāpayāsyanti pravāte śuṣkaparṇavat tatkṣetracaryāgamanaṃ martyānāmasatāmiha  BndP na labhyate mahārāja jātu janmaśatairapi samantapañcakaṃ tīrthaṃ kurukṣetre tipāvanam  BndP yatra snātaḥ sarvatīrthaiḥ snāto bhavati mānavaḥ kṛtakṛtyastato rāmaḥ samyak pūrṇamanorathaḥ  BndP uvāsa tatra niyataḥ kañcitkālaṃ mahāmatiḥ tataḥ saṃvatsarasyānte brāhmaṇaiḥ sahito vaśī  BndP pitṛpiṇḍapradānāya jāmadagnyo gamadgayām tato gatvā tataḥ śrāddhe yathāśāstramarindamaḥ  BndP brāhmaṇāṃstarpayāmāsa pitṝnuddiśya satkṛtān śaivaṃ tatra paraṃ sthānaṃ candrapādamiti smṛtam  BndP pitṛtṛptikaraṃ kṣetraṃ tādṛgloke na vidyate yatrārcitāḥ svakulajairyathāśakti manāgapi  BndP pitaraḥ piṇḍadānādyaiḥ prāpsyanti gatimakṣayām pitṝnuddiśya tatrāsau tarppiteṣu dvijātiṣu  BndP dadau ca vidhivatpiṇḍaṃ pitṛbhaktisamanvitaḥ tatastatpitaraḥ sarve pitṛlokādupāgatāḥ  BndP jagṛhustatkṛtāṃ pūjāṃ jamadagnipurogamāḥ atha saṃprītamanasaḥ sametya bhṛgunandanam  BndP ūcustatpitaraḥ sarve dṛśyā bhūtvāntarikṣagāḥ pitara ūcuḥmahatkarma kṛtaṃ vīra bhavatānyaiḥ suduṣkaram  BndP asmānapi yathānyāyaṃ samyak tarpitavānasi asmākamakṣayāṃ prītiṃ tathāpi tvaṃ na yacchasi  BndP kṣatrahatyāṃ hi kṛtvā tu kṛtakarmābhavadyataḥ kṣetrasyāsya prabhāveṇa bhaktyā ca tava darśanam  BndP prāptāḥsma pūjitāḥ kiṃ tu nākṣayyaphalabhāginaḥ tsamāttvaṃ vīrahatyādipāpapraśamanāya hi  BndP prāyaścittaṃ yathānyāyaṃ kuru dharmaṃ ca śāśvatam vadhācca vinivartasva kṣatriyāṇāmataḥ param  BndP piturnna te parādhyante na svatantraṃ yato jagat tannimittaṃ tu maraṇaṃ pituste vihitaṃ purā  BndP hantuṃ kaṃ kaḥ samarthaḥ syālloke rakṣitumeva vā nimittamātrameveha sarvaḥ sarvasya caitayoḥ  BndP dhruvaṃ karmānurūpaṃ te ceṣṭante sarva eva hi kālānuvṛttaṃ balavānnṛloko nātra saṃśayaḥ  BndP bādhituṃ bhuvi bhūtāni bhūtānāṃ na vidhiṃ vinā śakyate vatsa sarvo pi yataḥ śaktyā svakarmakṛt  BndP kṣatraṃ prati tato roṣaṃ vimucyāsmatpriyepsayā śamamā pnuhi bhadraṃ te sa hyasmākaṃ paraṃ balam  BndP vasiṣṭha uvācaityuktvāntardadhuḥ sarve pitaro bhṛgunandanam sa cāpi tadvacaḥ sarvaṃ pratijagrāha sādaram  BndP akṛtavraṇasaṃyukto mudā paramayā yutaḥ prayayau ca tadā rāmastasmātsiddhavanāśramam  BndP tasminsthitvā bhṛguśreṣṭho brāhmaṇaiḥ sahito nṛpa tapase dhṛtasaṃkalpo babhūva sa mahāmanāḥ  BndP sarathaṃ sahasāhaṃ ca dhanuḥsaṃhananāni ca punarāgamasaṃketaṃ kṛtvā prāsthāpayattadā  BndP tataḥ sa sarvatīrtheṣu cakre snānamatandritaḥ parītyapṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ pitṛdevādibūjakaḥ  BndP evaṃ krameṇa pṛthivīṃ trivāraṃ bhugunandanaḥ paricakrāma rājendra lokavṛttamanuvrataḥ  BndP tataḥ sa parvataśreṣṭhaṃ mahendraṃ punarapyatha jagāma tapase rājanbāhmaṇairabhisaṃvṛtaḥ  BndP sa tasmiṃścirarātrāya muni siddhaniṣevite nivāsamātmano rājankalpayāmāsa dharmavit  BndP munayastaṃ tapasyantaṃ sarvakṣetranivāsinaḥ draṣṭukāmāḥ samājagmurniyatā brahmavādinaḥ  BndP dadṛśuste munigaṇāstapasyāsaktamānasam kṣātraṃ kakṣamaśeṣeṇa dagdhvā śāntamivānalam  BndP atha tānāgatāndṛṣṭvā munīndivyāṃstapomayān arghyādisamudācāraiḥ pūjayāmāsa bhārgavaḥ  BndP kṛtakauśalasaṃpraśnapūrvakāḥ sumahodayāḥ teṣāṃ tasya ca saṃvṛttāḥ kathāḥ puṇyā manoharāḥ  BndP tatasteṣāmanumate munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām hayamedhaṃ mahāyajñamāhartumupacakrame  BndP saṃbhṛtya sarvasaṃbhārānaurvādyaiḥ sahito nṛpa viśvāmitrabharadvājamārkaṇḍeyādibhistathā  BndP teṣā manumate kṛtvā kāśyapaṃ gurumātmanaḥ vājimedhaṃ tato rājannājahāra mahākratum  BndP tasyābhūtkāśyapo dhvaryurudgātā gautamo muniḥ viśvāmitro bhavaddhotā rāmasya viditātmanaḥ  BndP brahmatvamakarottasya mārkaṇḍeyo mahāmuniḥ bharadvājāgniveśyādyā veda vedāṅgapāragāḥ  BndP munayaścakruranyāni karmāṇyanye yathākramam puttraiḥ śiṣyaiḥ praśiṣyaiśca sahito bhagavānbhṛguḥ  BndP sādasyamakarodrājannanyaiśca munibhiḥ saha sa taiḥ sahākhilaṃ karma samāpya bhṛgupuṅgavaḥ  BndP brahmāṇaṃ pūjayāmāsa yathāvadguruṇā saha alaṅkṛtya yathānyāya kanyāṃ rūpavatīṃ mahīm  BndP puragrāmaśatopetāṃ samudrāṃbaramālinīm āhūya bhṛguśārdūlaḥ saśailavanakānanām  BndP kāśyapāya dadau sarvāmṛte taṃ śailamuttamam ātmanaḥ sannivāsārthaṃ taṃ rāmaḥ paryakalpayat  BndP tataḥ prabhṛtirājendra pūjayāmāsa śāstrataḥ hiraṇyaratnavastraśvagogajānnādibhistathā  BndP purā samāpya yajñānte tathā cāvabhṛthāplutaḥ cakre dravyaparityāgaṃ teṣāmanumate tadā  BndP dattvā ca sarvabhūtānāmabhayaṃ bhṛgunandanaḥ tatrāpi parvatavare tapaścartuṃ samārabhat  BndP tatastaṃ samanujñāya sadasyā ṛtvijastathā yayuryathāgataṃ sarve munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ  BndP gateṣu teṣu bhagavānakṛtavraṇasaṃyutaḥ tapo mahatsamāsthāya tatraiva nyavasatsukhī  BndP kāśyapī tu tato bhūmirjananāthā hyanekaśaḥ sarvaduḥkhapraśāntyarthaṃ mārīcānumatena tu  BndP tatra dīpapratiṣṭhākhyavrataṃ viṣṇumukhoditam cacāra dharaṇī samyak dukhairḥmuktābhavacca sā  BndP ityeṣa jāmadagnyasya prādurbhāva udāhṛtaḥ yasmiñśrute naraḥ sarvapātakairvipramucyate  BndP prabhāvaḥ kārttavīryasya loke prathitatejasaḥ prasaṃgātkathitaḥ samyaṅnātisaṃkṣepavistaraḥ  BndP evaṃprabhāvaḥ sa nṛpaḥ kārttavīryo bhavadbhuvi na tādṛśaḥ pumātkaścidbhāvī bhūtāthavā śrutaḥ  BndP dattātreyādvaraṃ vavre mṛtimuttamapūruṣāt yatpurā so gamanmuktiṃ raṇe rāmeṇa ghātitaḥ  BndP tasyāsītpañcamaḥ putraḥ pakhyāto yo jayadhvajaḥ putrastasya mahābāhustālajaṅgho bhavannṛpa  BndP abhūttasyāpi putrāṇāṃ śatamuttamadhanvinām tālajaṅghābhidhā yeṣāṃ vītihotro grajo bhavat  BndP putraiḥ savītihotrādyairhaihayādyaiśca rājabhiḥ kālaṃ mahāntamavasaddhimādrivānagahvare  BndP yaḥ pūrvaṃ rāma bāṇena dravanpṛṣṭhe bhitāḍitaḥ tālajaṅgho patadbhūmau mūrchito tataḥ śāntiṃ gate rāme tapasyāsaktamānase jālajaṅghaḥ svakaṃ rājyaṃ saputraḥ pratyapadyata  BndP sanniveśya purīṃ bhūyaḥ pūrvavannṛpasattamaḥ vasaṃstadā nijaṃ rājyamāpālayadarindamaḥ  BndP suputraḥ sānugabalaḥ pūrvavairamanusmaran abhyāyayau mahārāja tālajaṅghaḥ puraṃ tava  BndP caturaṅgabalopetaḥ kaṃpayanniva medinīm rurodābhyetya nagarīmayodhyāṃ sa mahīpatiḥ  BndP tato niṣkramya didṛkṣurāśramopānte tasyaiva nyavasatsukham suṣāva ca tataḥ kāle sā tvāmaurvāśrame tadā  BndP jātakarmādikaṃ sarvaṃ bhavataḥ so karonmuniḥ aurvāśrame vivṛddhaśca bhavāṃstenānukaṃpitaḥ  BndP tvayaiva BndP nighnandṛptānanekāndvipaturagarathavyūhasaṃbhinnavīrānsadyaḥ śobhāṃ dadhāno suranikaracamūrnighnataścandramauliḥ dūrādevābhiśaṃsannarinagaranirodheṣu karmābhiṣaṅge teṣāṃ BndP sa hantyasamānaśeṣeṇa vairāntakaraṇonmukhaḥ tasmādbhayāddhi niṣkrāntā vayaṃ jīvitakāṅkṣiṇaḥ  BndP vibhinnarājyabhogarddhisvadārāpatyabāndhavāḥ kevalaṃ prāṇarakṣārthaṃ tvāṃ tvayaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  BndP na hyanyo sti pumāṃlloke sauhṛdena balena vā yastaṃ nivarttayitvāsmānpālayenmahato bhayāt  BndP tvaṃ kilārkānvayabhuvāṃ rājñāṃ kulagurur vṛtaḥ tadvaṃśapūrvajairbhūpaistvataprabhāvaśca tādṛśaḥ  BndP tenāyaṃ sagaro pyadya gurugauravayantritaḥ bhavannideśaṃ nātyeti velāmiva mahodadhiḥ  BndP tvaṃ naḥ suhṛtpitā mātā lokānāṃ ca gururvibho tasmādasmānmahābhāga paritrātuṃ tvamarhasi  BndP jaiminiruvācaiti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā vasiṣṭho bhagavānṛṣiḥ śanairvilokayāmāsa śaraṇaṃ samupāgatān  BndP vṛddhastrībālabhūyiṣṭhānhataśeṣānnṛpānvayān dṛṣṭvā tvatapyadbhagavānsarvabhūtānukaṃpakaḥ  BndP diṣṭyātvayā jitāḥ sarve ripavo nṛpasattama diṣṭyā ca sakalaṃ rājyaṃ tvayā dharmeṇa rakṣyate  BndP dharma eva sthitiryeṣāṃ teṣāṃ nāstyatraviplavaḥ na taṃ rakṣati kiṃ dharmaḥ svayaṃ yenābhirakṣitaḥ  BndP pūrvamevāhamaśrauṣaṃ vijitya sakalāṃ mahīm sabalonagarīṃ prāptaḥ kṛtadāro bhavāniti  BndP rājñāṃ tu pravaro dharmo yatprajāparipālanam bhavanti sukhino nūnaṃ tenaiveha paratra ca  BndP sa bhavānrājya bharaṇaṃ parityajya madantikam bhāryābhyāṃ sahito rājansamāyāto si me vada  BndP jaiminiruvācaevamuktastu muninā sagaro rājasattamaḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā prāha taṃ madhuraṃ vacaḥ  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyamabhāge tṛtīya upoddhātapāde sagarasyaurvāśramagamanaṃ nāma pañcaśattamo dhyāyaḥ  sagara uvācakuśalaṃ mama sarvatra maharṣe nātra saṃśayaḥ yasya me tvamanudhyātā śamaṃ bhārgavasattamaḥ  BndP yastathā śikṣitaḥ pūrvamastre śastre ca sāṃpratam so haṃ kathamaśaktaḥ syāṃ sakalārivinigrahe  BndP tvaṃ me guruḥ suhṛddaivaṃ bandhurmitraṃ ca kevalam na hyanyamabhijānāmi tvāmṛte pitaraṃ ca me  BndP tvayopadiṣṭenāstreṇa sakalā bhūbhṛto mayā vijitā yadanusmṛtyā śaktiḥ sā tapasastava  BndP tapasā tvaṃ jagatsarvaṃ punāsi paripāsi ca sraṣṭuṃ saṃharttumapi ca śaknoṣyeva na saṃśayaḥ  BndP mahānananyasāmānyaprabhāvastapasaśca te iha tasyaikadeśo pi dṛśyate vismayapradaḥ  BndP paśyasiṃhāsane bālyādupetya mṛgapotakaḥ pibatyaṃbhaḥ śanairbrahmanniḥśaṅkaṃ te tapovane  BndP dhayatyatrātivisraṃbhāt kṛśāpi hariṇī stanam karoti mṛgaśṛṅgāgre gaṇḍakaṇḍūyanaṃ ruruḥ  BndP navaprasūtāṃ hariṇīṃ hatvā vṛttyai vanāntare vyāghrī tvattapasāvāse saiva puṣṇāti tacchiśūn  BndP gajaṃ drutamanudrutya siṃho yasmādidaṃ vanam praviṣṭo nusarantau tvadbhayādekatra tiṣṭhataḥ  BndP nakulastvāśumārjāramayūraśaśapannagāḥ vṛkasūkaraśārdūlaśarabharkṣaplavaṅgamāḥ  BndP sṛgālā gavayāgāvo hariṇā mahiṣāstathā vane tra sahajaṃ vairaṃ hitvā maitrīmupāgatāḥ  BndP evaṃvidhā tapaḥśaktirlokavismayadāyinī na kvāpi dṛśyate brahmaṃstvāmṛte bhuvi durlabhā  BndP ahaṃ tu tvatprasādena vijitya vasudhāmi mām ripubhiḥ saha viprarṣe svarājyaṃ samupāgataḥ  BndP vaśyāmātyastrivarge pi yathāyogyakṛtādaraḥ tvayopadiṣṭamārgeṇa samyagrājyamapālayam  BndP evaṃ pravarttamānasya mama rājye vatiṣṭhataḥ bhavaddidṛkṣā saṃjātā sāpekṣā bhṛgupuṅgava  BndP kiṃ tvadya mayi paryāptamanapatyatayaiva me pitṛpiṇḍapradānena saha saṃrakṣaṇaṃ bhuvaḥ  BndP tadidaṃ duḥśamatyarthamanivāryaṃ manogatam nānayo paharttāṃ lokaṃsmin mameti tvāmupāgataḥ  BndP ityuktaḥ sagareṇātha sthitvā so tarmanāḥ kṣaṇam uvāca bhagavānaurvaḥ sanideśamidaṃ vacaḥ  BndP niyamya saha bhāryābhyāṃ kiñcitkālamihāvasa avāpsyati tato bhīṣṭaṃ bhavānnātra vicāramā  BndP sa ca tatrāvasatprītastacchuśrūṣāparāyamaḥ patnībhyāṃ saha dharmātmā bhaktiyuktaściraṃ tadā  BndP rājapatnyau ca te tasya sarvakālamatandrite muneratanutāṃ prītiṃ vinayācārabhaktibhiḥ  BndP bhaktyā śuśrūṣayā caiva tayostuṣṭo mahāmuniḥ rājapatnyau samāhūya idaṃ vacanama bravīt  BndP bhavatyau varamasmatto vriyatāṃ kāmamīpsitam dāsyāmi taṃ na saṃdeho yadyapi syātsudurllabham  BndP tataḥ praṇamyaśirasā te pyubhe taṃ mahāmunim ūcaturbhagavānputrānkāmayāveti sādaram  BndP tataste bhagavānāha bhavatībhyāṃ mayā punaḥ rājñaścapriyakāmena varo datto yamīpsitaḥ  BndP putravatyau mahābhāge bhavatyau matprasādataḥ bhavetāṃ dhruvamanyacca śrūyatāṃ vacanaṃ mama  BndP putro bhaviṣyatyekasyāmekaḥ so natidhārmikaḥ tathāpi tasya kalpāntaṃ saṃbhūtiśca bhaviṣyati  BndP ṣaṣṭiḥ putrasahasrāṇāmaparasyāṃ ca jāyate akṛtārthāśca te sarve vinaṅkṣyantyacirādiva  BndP evaṃvidhaguṇepeto varau dattau mayā yuvām abhīpsitaṃ tu yadyasyāḥ svecchayā tatprakīrtyatām  BndP evamukte tu muninā vaidarbhyānvayavarddhanam varayāmāsa tanayaṃ putrānanyāstathā parā  BndP iti dattvā varaṃ rājñe sagarāya mahāmuniḥ sabhāryāmanumānyainaṃ visasarja purīṃ prati  BndP muninā samanujñātaḥ kṛta kṛtyo mahīpatiḥ rathamāruhya vegena sapriyaḥ prayayau purīm  BndP sa praviśya purīṃ ramyāṃ tdṛṣṭapuṣṭajanāvṛtām ānanditaḥ paurajanai reme paramayā mudā  BndP etasminneva kāle tu rājapatnyāvubhe nṛpa rājñe prāvocatāṃ garbhaṃ mudā paramayā yute  BndP vavṛdhe ca tayorgarbhaḥ śuklapakṣe yathoḍurāṭ saha saṃtoṣasaṃpattyā pitroḥ paurajanasya ca  BndP saṃpūrṇe tu tataḥ kāle muhūrte keśinīśubhe asūyatāgnigarbhābhaṃ kumāramamitadyutim  BndP jātakarmādikaṃ tasya kṛtvā caiva yathāvidhi asamañcasa ityeva nāma tasyā karonnṛpaḥ  BndP sumatiścāpi tatkāle garbhālābamasūyata saṃprasūtaṃ tu taṃ tyaktaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājākaronmanaḥ  BndP tajjñātvā bhagavānaurvastatrāgacchadyadṛcchayā samyak saṃbhāvito rājñā tamuvāca tvarānvitaḥ  BndP garbhālāburayaṃ rājanna tyaktuṃ bhavatārhati putrāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭisāhasrabījabhūto yatastava  BndP tasmāttatsakalīkṛtya ghṛtakuṃbheṣu yatnataḥ niḥkṣipya sapidhāneṣu rakṣaṇīyaṃ pṛthakpṛthak  BndP samyagevaṃ kṛte rājanbhavato matprasādataḥ yathoktasaṃkhyā patrāṇāṃ bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ  BndP kāle pūrṇe tataḥ kumbhānbhittvā niryānti te pṛthak evaṃ te ṣaṣṭisāhasraṃ putrāṇāṃ jāyate nṛpa  BndP ityuktvā bhagavānaurvastatraivāntaradhādvibhuḥ rājā ca tattathā cakre yathaurveṇa samīritam  BndP tataḥ saṃvatsare pūrṇe ghṛtakuṃbhātkrameṇa te bhittvābhittvā punarjajñuḥ sahasaivānuvāsaram  BndP evaṃ krameṇa saṃjātāstanayāste mahīpate vavṛdhuḥ saṃghaśo rājanṣaṣṭisāhasrasaṃkhyāyā  BndP apṛthagdharmacaraṇā mahābalaparākramāḥ babhūvuste durādharṣāḥ krūrātmāno viśeṣataḥ  BndP sa nātiprītimāṃsteṣu rājā matimatāṃ varaḥ keśinītanayaṃ tvekaṃ bahumāna sutaṃ priyam  BndP vivāhaṃ vidhivattasmai kārayāmāsa pārthivaḥ sacāpyānandayāmāsa svaguṇaiḥ suhṛdo khilān  BndP evaṃ pravarta mānasya keśinītanayasya tu ajāyata sutaḥ śrīmānaṃśumāniti viśrutaḥ  BndP sa bālya eva matimānudāraiḥ svaguṇairbhṛśam prīṇayāmāsa sutdṛdaḥ svapitāmahameva ca  BndP etasminnantare rājñastasya putro samañjasaḥ āviṣṭo naṣṭaceṣṭo bhūtsa piśācena kena cit  BndP sa tu kaścidabhūdvaiśyaḥ pūrvajanmani dharmavit kasyācidviṣaye rājñaḥ prabhūtadhanadhānyavān  BndP sa kadācidaraṇyeṣu vicarannidhimuttamam dṛṣṭvā grahītumārebhe vaṇiglobhavariplutaḥ  BndP tatastadrakṣako bhyetya piśācaḥ prāha taṃ tadā kṣudhito haṃ cirādasminnivasannidhipālakaḥ  BndP tasmāttatparihārāya mama dattvā gavāmiṣam kāmataḥ pratigṛhṇīṣva nidhimenaṃ mamājñayā  BndP satasmai tatpariśrutya dāsyāmīti gavāmiṣam ādatta ca nidhiṃ taṃ tu piśācenānumoditaḥ  BndP na prādācca tato mauḍhyāttasmai yattatpratiśrutam pratiśrutāpradānottharoṣaṃ na śraddadhe nṛpa  BndP tamevaṃ suciraṃ kālaṃ pratīkṣyāśanakāṅkṣayā apanītadhanaḥ so pi mamāra vyathitaḥ kṣudhā  BndP vaiśyo pi bālo maraṇaṃ saṃprāpya sagarasya tu babhūva kāle keśinyāṃ tanayo nvayavarddhanaḥ  BndP aśarīraḥ piśāce pi pūrvavairamanusmaran vāyubhūto viśaddehaṃ rājaputrasya bhūpate  BndP tenāviṣṭastataḥ so pi krūracitto bhavattadā mativibhraṃśamāsādya muhustena balātkṛtaḥ  BndP asamañjasatvaṃ nagare cakre so pi nṛśaṃsavat bālāṃśca yūnaḥ sthavirānyoṣitaśca sadā khalaḥ  BndP hatvāhatvā pracikṣepa sarayvāmatinirdayaḥ tataḥ paurajanāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā tasya kadaryatām  BndP bahuśo nikṛtāstena gatvā rājñe vyajijñāpan rājā ca tadupaśrutya tamāhūya prayatnataḥ  BndP vārayāmāsa bahudhā duḥkhena mahatānvitaḥ bahuśaḥ pratiṣiddho pi pitrā tena mahātmanā  BndP jale tapte ca saṃtaptāḥ saṃbabhūvuryathā yavāḥ nāśakattaṃ yadā pāpādvinivarttayituṃ nṛpaḥ  BndP lokāpavādabhīrutvādviṣayānatyajattadā  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyamabhāge tṛtīya upoddhātapāde sagaracarite samañjasatyāgo nāmaikapañcāśattamo dhyāyaḥ  jaiminiruvācatyaktvā putraṃ sa dharmātmā sagaraḥ prema tadgatam dharmaśīle tadā vāle cakārāṃśumati prabhuḥ  BndP etasminneva kāle tu sumatyāstanayā nṛpa vavṛdhuḥ saghaśaḥ sarve parasparamanuvratāḥ  BndP vajrasaṃhananāḥ krūrā nirdayā nirapatrapāḥ adharmaśīlā nitarāmekagharmāṇa eva ca  BndP ekakāryābhiniratāḥ krodhanā mūḍhacetasaḥ adhṛṣyāḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ janopadravakāriṇaḥ  BndP vinayācā rasanmārganirapekṣāḥ samantataḥ babādhire jagatsarvamasurā iva kāmataḥ  BndP vidhvastayajñasanmārgaṃ bhuvanaṃ tairupadrutam niḥsvādhyāya vaṣaṭkāraṃ babhūvārtaṃ viśeṣataḥ  BndP vidhvasyamāne subhṛśaṃ sāgarairvaradarpitaiḥ prakṣobhaṃ paramaṃ jagmurdevāsuramahoragāḥ  BndP dharāsā sāgarākrāntā na calāpi tadā calā tapaḥ samādhibhaṅgaśca prababhūva tapasvinām  BndP havyakavyaparibhraṣṭāstridaśāḥ pitṛbhiḥ saha duḥśena mahātāviṣṭā viriñjabhavanaṃ yayuḥ  BndP tatra gatvā yathānyāyaṃ devāḥ śarvapurogamāḥ śaśaṃsuḥ sakalaṃ tasmai sāgarāṇāṃ viceṣṭitam  BndP tacchratvā vacanaṃ teṣāṃ brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ kṣaṇamantarmanā bhūtvā jagāda surasattamaḥ  BndP devāḥśṛṇuta bhadraṃ vo vāṇīmavahitā mama vinaṅkṣyantyaciremaiva sāgarā nātra saṃśayaḥ  BndP kālaṃ kañcitpratīkṣadhvaṃ tena sarvaṃ niyamyate nimittamātramanyattu sa eva sakaleśitā  BndP tasmādyuṣmaddhitārthāya yadvakṣyāmi surottamāḥ sarvairbhavadbhiradhunā tatkarttavyamataṃ dritaiḥ  BndP viṣṇoraṃśena bhagavānkapilo jayatāṃ varaḥ jāto jagaddhitārthāya yogīndrapravaro bhuvi  BndP agastyapītasalile divyavarṣaśatāvadhi dhyāyannāste dhunāṃbhodhāvekānte tatra kutra cit  BndP gatvā yūyaṃ mamādeśātkapilaṃ munipuṅgavam dhyānāva sānamicchantastiṣṭhadhvaṃ tadupahvare  BndP samādhiviratau tasya svābhiprāyamaśeṣataḥ natvā tasmai vadiṣyadhvaṃ sa vaḥ śreyo vidhāsyati  BndP samādhibhaṅgaśca muneryathā syātsāgaraiḥ kṛtaḥ kurudhvaṃ ca tathā yūyaṃ pravṛttiṃ vibudhottamāḥ  BndP jaiminiruvācaityuktāstena vibudhāstaṃ praṇamya vitāmaham gatvā taṃ vibudhaśreṣṭaṃ te kṛtāñjalayo bruvan  BndP devā ūcuḥprasīda no muniśreṣṭha vayaṃ tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ upadrutaṃ jagatsarvaṃsāgaraiḥ saṃpraṇaśyati  BndP tvaṃ kilākhilalokānāṃ sthitisahārakāraṇaḥ viṣṇoraṃśena yogīndrasvarūpī bhuvi saṃsthitaḥ  BndP puṃsāṃ tāpatrayārttānāmārtināśāya kevalam svecchayā te dhṛto deho na tu tvaṃ tapatāṃ varaḥ  BndP manasaiva jagatsarvaṃ sraṣṭuṃ saṃhartumeva ca vidhātuṃ svecchayā brahmanbhavāñchakrotyasaṃśayam  BndP tvaṃ no dhātā vidhātā ca tvaṃ gurustvaṃ parāyaṇam paritrātā tvamasmākaṃ vinivarttaya cāpadam  BndP śaraṇaṃ bhava viprendra vipredrāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ sāgarairdahyamānānāṃ lokatrayanivāsinām  BndP nanu vai sāttvikī ceṣṭā bhavatīha bhavādṛśām trātumarhasi tasmāttvaṃ lokānasmāṃśca suvrata  BndP na cedakāle bhagavanvinaṅkṣyatyakhilaṃ jagat jaiminiruvācaityuktaḥ sakalairdevairunmīlya nayane śanaiḥ  BndP vilokya tānuvācedaṃ kapilaḥ sūnṛtaṃ vacaḥ svakarmaṇaiva nirdagdhāḥ pravinaṅkṣyanti sāgarāḥ  BndP kāle prāpte tu yuṣmābhiḥ satāvatparipālyatām ahaṃ tu kāraṇaṃ teṣāṃ vināśāya durātmanām  BndP bhaviṣyāmi suraśreṣṭhā bhavatāmarthasiddhaye mama krodhāgni vipluṣṭāḥ sāgarāḥ pāpacetasaḥ  BndP bhaviṣyantu cireṇaiva kālopahatabuddhayaḥ tasmādgatajvarā devā lokāścaivākutobhayāḥ  BndP bhavantu te durācārāḥ kṣipraṃ yāsyanti saṃkṣayam tadyūyaṃ nirbhayā bhūtvā vrajadhvaṃ svāṃ purīṃ prati  BndP kālaṃ kañcitpratīkṣadhvaṃ tato bhīṣṭamavāpsyatha kapilenaivamuktāste devāḥ sarve savāsavāḥ  BndP taṃ praṇamya tato jagmuḥ pratītāgnidivaṃ prati etasminnantare rājā sagaraḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ  BndP vājimedhaṃ mahāyajñaṃ kartuṃ cakre manoratham āhṛtya sarvasaṃbhārānvasiṣṭhānumate tadā  BndP aurvādyaiḥ sahito viprairyathāvaddīkṣito bhavat dīkṣāṃ praviṣṭo nṛpatirhayasaṃcāraṇāya vai  BndP putrānsarvānsamāhūya saṃdideśa mahayaśāḥ saṃcārayitvā turagaṃ parītya pṛthivītale  BndP kṣipraṃ mamāntikaṃ putrāḥ punarāhartumarhatha jaiminiruvācatataste piturādeśāttamādāya turaṅgamam  BndP paricaṅkramayāmāsuḥ sakale kṣitimaṇḍale vidhicodanayaivāśvaḥ sa bhūmau parivartitataḥ  BndP na tu digvijayārthāya karādānārthameva ca pṛthivībhūbhujā tena pūrvameva vinirjitā  BndP nṛpāścodāravīryeṇa karadāḥ samare kṛtāḥ tataste rājatanayā nistoye lavaṇāṃbudhau  BndP bhūtale viviśurhṛṣṭāḥ parivārya turaṅgamam  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyamabhāge tṛtīya uvoddhātapāde sagaravarite śvamocanaṃ nāma dvipañcāśattamo dhyāyaḥ  jaiminiruvācateṣu tatra niviṣṭeṣu vāsavena pracoditaḥ jahāraṃ turagaṃ vāyustatkṣaṇena rasātalam  BndP adṛṣṭamaśvaṃ taiḥ sarvairapahṛtya sadāgatiḥ anayattatpathā rājankapilasyāntikaṃ muneḥ  BndP tataḥ samākulāḥ sarve vinaṣṭe śve nṛpātmajāḥ parītya vasudhāṃ sarvāṃ pramārgantasturagamam  BndP vicitya pṛthivīṃ te tu sa purācalakānanām apaśyanto yajñapaśuṃ duḥkhaṃ mahadavāpnuvan  BndP tato yodhyāṃ samāsādya ṛṣibhiḥ parivāritām dṛṣṭvā praṇamya pitaraṃ tasmai sarvaṃ nyavedayan  BndP parītya pṛthvīmasmābhirniviṣṭe varuṇālaye rakṣyamāṇo pi paśyadbhiḥ kenāpi turago hṛtaḥ  BndP ityuktastai ruṣāviṣṭastānuvāca nṛpottamaḥ prayāsyadhvamadharmiṣṭhāḥ sarve nāvṛttaye punaḥ  BndP kathaṃ bhavadbhirjīvadbhirvinaṣṭo vai darātmabhiḥ turageṇa vinā satyaṃ nehāga manamasti vaḥ  BndP tataḥ sametya tasmātte saprayātāḥ parasparam ūcurna dṛśyate dyāpi turagaḥ kiṃ prakumaha  BndP vasudhā vicitāsmābhiḥ saśailavanakānanā na cāpi dṛśyate vājī tadvārttāpi na kutracit  BndP tasmādabdheḥ samārabhya pātālāvadhi medinīm vibhajya ravātvā pātālaṃ viviśāma turaṅgamam  BndP iti kṛtvā matiṃ sarve sāgarāḥ krūraniścayāḥ nicakhnurbhūmimaṃbodhestaṭā dārabhya sarvataḥ  BndP taiḥ khanyamānā vasudhā rarāsa bhṛśavihvalā cukruśuścāpi bhūtāni dṛṣṭvā teṣāṃ viceṣṭitam  BndP tataste bhārataṃ khaṇḍaṃ khātvā saṃkṣibya bhūtale bhūmeryojanasāhasraṃ yojayāmāsuraṃbudhau  BndP āpātālatalaṃ te tu khananto medinītalam carantamaśvaṃ pātāle dadṛśurnṛpanandanāḥ  BndP saṃprahṛṣṭāstataḥ sarve sametya pitṛdevadvijārcanam anyasmātkoṭiguṇitaṃ bhavettasminphalaṃ nṛpa  BndP aṃbhodhisalile magna tasmin kṣetre tipāvane mahatā tapasā yuktā munayastannivāsinaḥ  BndP sahyaṃ śikhariṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ nilayārthaṃ samāruhan vasaṃtastatra te sarve saṃpradhārya parasparam  BndP sahendrādrau tapasyantaṃ rāmaṃ gantuṃ pracakramuḥ rājovāca agastyapītatoye bdhau parito rājanandanaiḥ  BndP khātvādhaḥ pātite kṣetre satīrthāśramakānane bhūbhāgeṣu tathānyeṣu puragramākarādiṣu  BndP vināśiteṣu deśeṣu samudropāntavarttiṣu kimakārṣurmuniśreṣṭha janāstannilayāstataḥ  BndP tatraiva cāvasankṛcchrātprasthitānyatra vā tataḥ kiyatā caiva kālena saṃpūrṇo bhūdapāṃnidhiḥ kena vāpi prakāreṇa brahmannetadvadasva me  BndP jaiminiruvācaanūpeṣu pradeśeṣu nāśiteṣu durātmabhiḥ  BndP janāstannilayāḥ sarve saṃprayātā itastataḥ tatraiva cāvasankṛcchrātkecitkṣetranivāsinaḥ  BndP etasminneva kāle tu rājannaṃśumataḥ sutaḥ babhūva bhuvidharmātmā dilīpa iti viśrutaḥ  BndP rājye bhiṣicya taṃ samyagbhuktabhogoṃśumānnṛpaḥ vanaṃ jagāma medhāvī tapase dhṛtamānasaḥ  BndP dilīpastu tataḥśrīmānaśeṣāṃ pṛthivīmimām pālayāmāsa dharmeṇa vijitya sakalānarīn  BndP bhagīratho nāma sutastasyāsīllokaviśrutaḥ sarvadharmārthakuśalaḥ śrīmānamitavikramaḥ  BndP rājye bhiṣicya taṃ rājā dilīpo pi vanaṃ yayau sa cāpi pālayannurvīṃ samyagvihatakaṇṭakām  BndP mumude vividhairbhogairdivi devapatiryathā sa śuśrāvātmanaḥ pūrvaṃ pūrvajānāṃ mahīpatiḥ  BndP niraye patanaṃ ghoraṃ viprakopasamudbhavam brahmadaṇḍahatānsarvānpitañchrutvātiduḥkhitaḥ  BndP rājye bandhuṣu bhoge vā nirvedaṃ paramaṃ yayau sa mantripravare rājyaṃ vinyasya tapase vanam  BndP prayayau svapitṝnnākaṃ ninīṣurnṛpasattamaḥ tapasā mahātā pūrvamāyuṣe kamalodbhavam  BndP ārādhya tasmāllebhe ca yāvadāyurnijepsitam tato gaṅgāṃ mahārāja samārādhya prasādya ca  BndP varamāgamanaṃ vavre divastasyā mahīṃprati tatastāṃ śirasā dharttu tapasārādhayacchivam  BndP sa cāpi tadvaraṃ tasmai pradadau bhaktavatsalaḥ merormūrdhnastato gaṅgāṃ pataṃ tī śirasātmanaḥ  BndP sagrāhanakramakarāṃ jagrāha jagatāṃ patiḥ sā tacchiraḥ samāsādya mahāvegapravāhinī  BndP tajjaṭāmaṇḍale śubhre vililye sātigahvare culakodakavacchaṃbhorvilīnāṃ śirasi prabhoḥ  BndP vilokya tadyajñavāṭamakhilaṃ plāvayāmāsa sarvataḥ sa tu rājaṛṣiḥ kruddho yajñavāṭe khile tayā  BndP magne gaṇḍūṣajalavatsa papau tāmaśeṣataḥ atandrito varṣaśataṃ śuśrūṣitavā sa taṃ punaḥ  BndP tamāruhya śanaistasyakhyātamāśramamaṇḍalam praśāntakrūrasattvāḍhyaṃ śubhaṃ madhye tapovanam  BndP sarvarttuphalapuṣpāḍhyatarukhaṇḍamanoharam snigdhacchāyamanaupamyaṃ svāmodisukhamārutam  BndP taṃ munīnbhṛgukulodvahaḥ arghapādyādibhiḥ samyakpūjayāmāsa sādaram  BndP tānāsīnānkṛtātithyānṛṣīndeśāntarāgatān uvāca bhṛguśārdūlaḥ smitapūrvamidaṃ vacaḥ  BndP svāgataṃ vo mahābhāgā yūyaṃ sarve samāgatāḥ BndP viśrutaṃ yattrilokeṣu tīre nadanadīpateḥ tīrthaṃ tadantarīkṛtya sruvo rāmakarāccyutaḥ  BndP nipapāta mahārāja sūcayanrāmavikramam yatrābhūdrāmasṛṣṭāyā bhuvo niṣṭhātha pārthiva  BndP tīrthaṃ śūrpārakaṃ tattu śrīmallokapariśrutam utsārayitvā salilaṃ samudrastāvadātmanaḥ  BndP atiṣṭhadapasṛtyorvīṃ dattvā rāmāya pārthiva anatikrāntamaryādo yathākālaṃ bhṛgūdvahaḥ  BndP samayaṃ svāpayāmāsa pūrvavattasminnabdherapasṛteṃbhasi tatra daivāttathā sthānānnimnatvātsa pralakṣya tu  BndP tatasteṣāṃ bhṛguśreṣṭho munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām yathābhilaṣitaṃ sthānaṃ pradadau prītipūrvakam  BndP tataste munayaḥ sarve harṣeṇa mahātānvitāḥ kṛtakṛtyā bhṛśaṃ rāmamāśiṣā samapūjayan  BndP athaitairabhyanujñāto yayau prāptamanorathaḥ gate munivare rāme deśāttasmānnijāśramam  BndP saṃbhūya munayaḥ sarve prajagmustīramaṃbudheḥ paricaṅkramya tāṃ bhūmiṃ yatnena mahātānvitāḥ  BndP dadṛśuḥ sarvato rājanhyarmavāntaḥ sthitāṃ mahīm nityatvā tsarvadevānāmadhiṣṭhānatayā tathā  BndP kātamabdhau nipatitaṃ naṣṭatoyaṃ ciroṣitam api rudraprabhāvema prāyānnātyantaviplavam  BndP tatteyaniḥsṛtaṃ kṣetramabhūtpūrvavadeva hi etaddhi devasāmarthyamacintyaṃ nṛpasattama  BndP evaṃ rāmeṇa jaladheḥ punaḥ sṛṣṭā vasuṃdharā dakṣiṇottarato rājanayojanānāṃ catuḥśatam  BndP nātikrāmati so dyāpi sīmānaṃ payasāṃ nidhiḥ kṛtaṃ rāmeṇa mahatā na tu sajjaṃ mahaddhanuḥ  BndP evaṃ prabhāvo rāmo sau sagaraśca mahīpatiḥ yasya putrairayaṃ khaṇḍo bhārato bdhau nipatitaḥ  BndP yojanānāṃ sahasrantu varddhitaśca mahodadhiḥ rāmeṇābhūtpunaḥ sṛṣṭaṃ yojanānāṃ tu ṣaṭśatam  BndP sagarasya sutairyasmādvarddhito makarālayaḥ tataḥ prabhṛti lokeṣu sāgarākhyāmavāptavān  BndP etatte bhihitaṃ samyaṅmahataścaritaṃ mayā rāmasya kārttavīryasya sagarasya mahīpateḥ  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokta madhyamabhāge tṛtīya upāddhātapāde ṣṭapañcaśattamo dhyāyaḥ  bṛhaspatiruvācaṛṣayastveva muktāstu paraṃ harṣamupāgatāḥ paraṃ śuśrūṣayā bhūyaḥ papracchustadanantaram  BndP ṛṣaya ūcuḥvaṃśānāmānupūrvyeṇa rājñāṃ cāmitatejasām sthitiṃ caiṣāṃ prabhāvaṃ ca brūhi naḥ paripṛcchatām  BndP evamuktastatastaistu tadāsau lomaharṣaṇaḥ śṛṇvatāmuttarākhyāne ṛṣīṇāṃ vākya kovidaḥ  BndP akhyānakuśalo bhūyaḥ paraṃ vākyamuvāca ha bruvato me nibodhaṃśca ṛṣirāha yathā mama  BndP vaṃśānāmānupūrvyeṇa rājñāṃ cāmitatejasām sthitiṃ caiṣāṃ prabhāvaṃ ca kramato me nibodhata  BndP varuṇasya sapatnīkān stutā devī udāhṛtā tasyāḥ putrau kalirvaidyaḥ stutā ca surasuṃdarī  BndP kaliputrau mahāvīryauṃ jayaśca vijayaśca ha vaidyaputrau ghṛṇiścaiva muniścaiva mahābalau  BndP prattānāmanu kāmānāmanyonyasya prabhakṣiṇau bhakṣyitvā tāvanyonyaṃ vināśaṃ samavāpnutaḥ  BndP kaliḥ surāyāḥ saṃjñeyastasya putro madaḥ smṛtaḥ smṛtā hiṃsā kalerbhāryā śreṣṭhā yā nikṛtasmṛtiḥ  BndP prasūtānye kaleḥ putrāścatvāraḥ puruṣādakāḥ nāke vighnaśca vikhyāto bhadramovidhamastathā  BndP aśiraskatayā vighno nākaścaivāśarīravān bhadramaścaikahasto bhūdvidhamaścaikapātsmṛtaḥ  BndP bhadramasya tathāpatnī tāmasī pūtanā tathā revatī vidhamasyāpi tayoḥ putrāḥ sahasraśaḥ  BndP nākasya śakuniḥ patnī vighnasya ca ayo mukhī rākṣasāstu mahāvīryāḥ saṃdhyādvayavicārimaḥ  BndP revatīpūtanāputrā naiṛtā nāmataḥ smṛtāḥ grahaste rākṣasāḥ sarve bālānāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ  BndP skandasteṣāmadhipatirbrahmaṇo numataḥ prabhuḥ bṛhaspateryā bhaginī varastrī brahmacāriṇī  BndP yogasiddhā jagatkṛtsnamasaktā carate sadā prabhāsasya tu sā bhāryā vasūnāmaṣṭamasya ca  BndP viśvakarmā surastasyā jātaḥ śilpiprajāpatiḥ tvaṣṭā virājo rūpāṇi dharmapautra udāradhīḥ  BndP karttā śilpisahasrāṇāṃ tridaśānāṃ tu yogataḥ yaḥsarveṣāṃ vimānāni devatānāṃ cakāra ha  BndP mānuṣāścopajīvanti yasya śilpaṃ mahātmanaḥ prahrādī viśrutā tasya patnī tvaṣṭurvirocanā  BndP virocanasya bhaginī mātā triśirasastathā devācāryasya mahato viśvarūpasya dhīmataḥ  BndP viśvakarmātmajaśvaiva viśvakarmā mayaḥ smṛtaḥ sureṇuriti vikhyātā svasā tasya yavīyasī  BndP tvāṣṭrī yā saviturbhāryā punaḥ saṃjñeti viśrutā prāsūta sā mahābhāgaṃ manuṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ vivasvataḥ  BndP yamau prāsūta ca punaryamaṃ ca yamunāṃ ca ha sā tu gatvā kurūndevī vaḍavā rūpadhāriṇī  BndP savituścāsya rūpasya nāsikābhyāṃ tu tau smṛtau prāsūta sā mahābhāga tvantarikṣe śvinau kila  BndP nāsatyaṃ caiva dasraṃ ca mārttaṇḍasyātmajāvubhau ṛṣaya ūcuḥkasmānmārttaṇḍa ityeṣa vivasvānudito budhaiḥ  BndP kimarthaṃ sāsurūpā vai nāsikābhyāmasūyata etadveditumicchāmo sarvaṃ no brūhi pṛcchatām  BndP sūta uvācacirotpannamatirbhinnamaṇḍaṃ tvaṣṭrā vidāritam garbhavadhaṃ bhrāntaḥ kaśyapo vidruto bhavet  BndP aṇḍe dvidhākṛte tvaṇḍaṃ dṛṣṭvā tvaṣṭedamabravīt naitannyūnaṃ bhavādaṇḍaṃ mārttaṇḍastvaṃ bhavānagha  BndP na khalvayaṃ mṛtoṃḍastha iti snehātpitābravīt tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā nāmānvarthamudāharan  BndP yanmārttaṇḍo bhavetyuktastvaṇḍātsoṃḍe dvidhākṛte tasmādvivasvānmārttaṇḍaḥ purāṇajñairvibhāvyate  BndP tataḥ prajāḥ pravakṣyāmi mārttaṇḍasya vivasvataḥ vijajñe saviturbhāryā saṃjñā putrāṃstu trīnpunaḥ  BndP manuṃ yamīṃ yamaṃ caiva chāyā sā tapatī tathā śanaiścaraṃ tathaivaite mārttaṇḍasyātmajāḥ smṛtāḥ  BndP vivasvānkaśyapājjajñe dākṣāyiṇyāṃ mahāyaśāḥ tasya saṃjñābhavadbhāryā tvāṣṭrī devī vivasvataḥ  BndP sureṇuriti vikhyātā punaḥ saṃjñeti viśrutā sā tu bhāryā bhagavato mārttaṇḍasyātitejasaḥ  BndP na khalvaye mṛto hyaṇḍe iti snehāttamabravīt ajānankaśyapaḥ snehāt mārttaṇḍa iti cocyate  BndP tejastvabhyadhikaṃ tasya nityameva vivasvataḥ yenāpi tāpayāmāsa trīlloṅkānkaśyapātmajaḥ  BndP trīṇyapatyāni saṃjñāyāṃ janayāmāsa vai raviḥ dvau sutau tu mahāvīryauṃ kanyaikā viditaiva ca  BndP manurvaivasvato jyeṣṭhaḥ śrāddhadevaḥ prajāpatiḥ tato yamo yamī caiva yamajau saṃbabhūvatuḥ  BndP asahyatejastadrūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃjñā vivasvataḥ asahantī svakāṃ chāyāṃ savarṇāṃ nirmame punaḥ  BndP mahābhāgā tu sā nārī tasyāśchāyāsamudgatā prāñjaliḥ prayatā bhūtvā punaḥ saṃjñāmabhāṣata  BndP vadasva kiṃ mayā kāryaṃ sā saṃjñā tāmathābravīt ahaṃ yāsyāpi bhadraṃ te svameva bhavanaṃ pituḥ  BndP tvayeha bhavane mahyaṃ vastavyaṃ nirviśaṅkayā imau ca bālakau mahyaṃ kanyā ca varavarṇinī  BndP bharttavyā gaccheti niyuktā ca punaḥ punaḥ agamadvaḍavā bhūtvācchādya rūpamaninditā  BndP uttarānsā kurūngatvā tṛṇānyatha cacāra sā dvitīyāyāṃ tu saṃjñāyāṃ saṃjñeyamiti cintya tām  BndP ādityo janayāmāsa putrāvādityavarcasau pūrvajasya manostulyau sādṛśyena tu tau prabhū  BndP śrutaśravā manustābhyāṃ sāvarṇirvai bhaviṣyati  BndP śrutakarmā tu vijñeyo graho vai yaḥ śanaiścaraḥ manurevābhavatso pi yathānyāyamarcayitvā vibhāvasum  BndP nirdagdhukāmaṃ roṣeṇa sāṃtvayāmāsa vai śanaiḥ tavātitejasā yuktamidaṃ rūpaṃ na śobhate  BndP asahantī tu tatsaṃjñā vane carati śādvale drakṣyate tāṃ bhavanadya paramāṃ dyutim  BndP pitṝṇāmādhipatyaṃ ca lokapālatvameva ca manuḥ prajāpatistveṣa sāvarṇiḥ sa mahāyaśāḥ  BndP bhāvyaḥ so nāgate tasminmanuḥ sāvarṇikentare merupṛṣṭhe tapo ghoramadyāpi carate prabhuḥ  BndP bhrātā śanaiścarastatragrahatvaṃ sa tu labdhavān tvaṣṭā tu tena rūpeṇa viṣṇoścakramakalpayat  BndP mahāmaho pratihataṃ dānavānprativāraṇam yavīyasī tayoryā tu yamunāca yaśasvinī  BndP abhavatsā saricchreṣṭhā yamunā lokapāvanī yastu jyeṣṭho mahātejāḥ sargo yasyeti sāṃpratam  BndP vistaraṃ tasya vakṣyāmi manorvaivasvatasya ha idaṃ tu janma devānāṃ śṛṇuyādvā paṭhecca vā  BndP vaivasvatasya paramadhārmikāḥ  BndP utkalaśca gayaścaiva vinataśca tathaiva ca utkalasyotkalaṃ rāṣṭraṃ vinatasyāpi paścimam  BndP dikpūrvā tasya rājarṣergayasya tu gayā purī praviṣṭetu manau tasminprajāḥ sṛṣṭvā śāpācchūdratvamāpannaścyavanasya mahātmanaḥ karūṣasya tu kārūṣāḥ kṣattriyā yuddhadurmadāḥ  BndP sahasraṃ kṣattriyagaṇo vikrāntaḥ saṃbabhūva ha nābhāgo diṣṭaputrastu vidvānāsīdbhalandanaḥ  BndP bhalandanasya putro bhūtprāṃśurnāma mahābalaḥ prāṃśoreko bhavatputraḥ prajāpatisamo nṛpaḥ  BndP saṃvartena divaṃ nītaḥ sasuhṛtsahabāndhavaḥ vivādo tra mahānāsītsaṃvarttasya bṛhaspateḥ  BndP ṛddhiṃ dṛṣṭvā tu yajñasya kruddhastasya bṛhaspatiḥ saṃvarttena tate yajñe cukopa sa bhṛśaṃ tadā  BndP lokānāṃ sahi nāśāya daivatairhi prasāditaḥ maruttaścakravarttī sa nariṣyantamavāsavān  BndP nariṣyantasya dāyādo rājā daṇḍadharo damaḥ tasya putrastu vijñāto rājāsīdrāṣṭravarddhanaḥ  BndP sudhṛtistasya putrastu naraḥ sudhṛtitaḥ punaḥ kevalasya putrastu bandhumānkevalātmajaḥ  BndP atha bandhumataḥ putrodharmātmā vegavānnṛpa budho vegavataḥ putrastṛṇabindurbudhātmajaḥ  BndP tretāyugamukhe rājā tṛtīye saṃbabhūva ha kanyā tu tasyeḍaviḍāmātā viśravaso hi sā  BndP putro yo sya viśālo bhūdrājā paramadhārmikaḥ dāśvānprakhyātavīryyaujā viśālā yena nirmitā  BndP viśālasya suto rājā hemacandro mahābalaḥ sucandra iti vikhyāto hemacandrādanantaraḥ  BndP sucandratanayo rājā dhūmrāśva iti viśrutaḥ dhūmrāśvatanayo vidvānsṛṃjayaḥ samapadyata  BndP sṛñjayasya sutaḥ śrīmānsahadevaḥ pratāpavān kṛśāśvaḥ sahadevasya putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ  BndP kṛśāśvasya mahātejā somadattaḥ pratāpavān somadattasya rājarṣeḥ suto bhūjjanamejayaḥ  BndP janamejayātmajaścaiva pramatirnāma viśrutaḥ tṛṇabinduprabhāveṇa sarve vaiśālakā nṛpāḥ  BndP dīrghāyuṣo mahātmāno vīryavantaḥ sudhārmikāḥ śaryātermithunaṃ tvāsīdānartto nāma viśrutaḥ  BndP putraḥ sukanyā kanyā ca bhāryā yā cyavanasya ca ānarttasya tu dāyādo revo nāma suvīryavān  BndP ānarttaviṣayo yasya purī cāpi kuśasthalī revasya raivataḥ putraḥ kakudmī nāma dhārmikaḥ  BndP jyeṣṭho bhrātṛśatasyāsīdrājyaṃ prāpya kuśasthalīm kanyayā saha śrutvā ca gāndharvaṃ brahmaṇoṃtike  BndP muharttaṃ devadevasya mārtyaṃ bahuyugaṃ vibho ājagāma yuvā caiva svāṃ purīṃ yādavairvṛtām  BndP kṛtāṃ dvāravatīṃ nāma bahudvārāṃ manoramām bhojavṛṣṇyandhakairguptāṃ vasudevapurogamaiḥ  BndP tāṃ kathāṃ revataḥ śrutvā yathātattvamarindamaḥ kanyāṃ tu baladevāya suvratāṃ nāma revatīm dattvā jagāma śikharaṃ merostapasi saṃsthitaḥ  BndP reme rāmaśca dharmātmā revatyā sahitaḥ kila tāṃ kathāmṛṣayaḥ śrutvā papracchuktadanantaram  BndP ṛṣaya ūcuḥkathaṃ bahuyuge kāle samatīte mahāmate na jarā revatīṃ prāptā raivataṃ vā kakudminam etacchuśrūṣamāṇānno gāndharvaṃ vada caiva hi  BndP sūta uvācana jarā kṣutpipāse vā na ca mṛtyubhayaṃ tataḥ na ca rogaḥ prabhavati brahmalokaṃ gatasya ha  BndP gāndharvaṃ prati yaccāpi pṛṣṭastu munisattamāḥ tato haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yāthātathyena suvratāḥ  BndP sapta svarāstrayo grāmā mūrchanāstvekaviṃśatiḥ tānāścaikonapañcāśadityetsvaramaṇḍalam  BndP ṣaḍjaṣabhau ca gāndhāro madhyamaḥ pañcamastathā dhaivataścāpi vijñeyastathā cāpi niṣādakaḥ  BndP sauvīrā madhyamā grāmā hariṇāśca tathaiva ca  BndP tasyāḥ BndP tenavānityapavaśapiśācātīvanahyapi sāvitramardhasāvitraṃ sarvatobhadrameva ca  BndP manoharamadhātryaṃ ca gandharvānupataśca yaḥ alaṃbuṣeseṣṭamatho viṣṇuvaiṇavarāvubhau  BndP sāgarāvijayaṃ caiva nāgādṛṣṭiviṣāgītānopasarpantimūrchanāḥ nānāsādhāramaścaivavaḍavātrividastathā  BndP  iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyamābhāge tṛtīya upoddhātapāde gāndharvamūrchanālakṣaṇavarṇanaṃ nāmaikaṣaṣṭitamo dhyāyaḥ   pūrvācāryamataṃ buddhvā pravakṣyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ vikhyātānvai alaṅkārāṃstanme nigadataḥ śruṇu  BndP alaṅkārāstu vaktavyāḥ svaiḥ svairvarṇaiḥ prahetavaḥ saṃsthā nayogaiśca
