nṛpaścāṣṭau bhaviṣyati samā nṛpaḥ bhavitā cāpi sujyeṣṭaḥ sapta varṣāṇi vai tataḥ  BndP vasumitrastato bhāvyo daśavarṣāṇi pārthivaḥ tato bhadraḥ same dve tu bhaviṣyati nṛpaśca vai  BndP bhaviṣyati samāstasmāttisra eva pulindakaḥ rājā ghoṣastataścāpi varṣāṇi bhavitā trayaḥ  BndP sapta vai vajra mitraṃstu samā rājā tataḥ punaḥ dvātriṃśadbhavitā vāpi samā bhāgavato nṛpaḥ  BndP bhaviṣyati sutastasya devabhūmiḥ samā daśa daśaite śuṅgarājāno bhokṣyantīmāṃ vasuṃdharām  BndP śataṃ pūrmaṃ daśa dve ca tebhyaḥ kaṇvaṃ gamiṣyati amātyo vasudevastu bālyādvyasaninaṃ nṛpam  BndP devabhūmiṃ tato hatvā śuṅgeṣu bhavitā nṛpaḥ bhaviṣyati samā rājā pañca kaṇvāyanastu saḥ  BndP bhūmimitraḥ sutastasya caturviṃśadbhaviṣyati bhavitā dvādaśa samāstasmānnārāyaṇo nṛpaḥ  BndP suśarmā tatsutaścāpi bhaviṣyati catuḥsamāḥ kaṇvāyanāstu catvāraścatvāriṃśacca pañca ca  BndP samā bhokṣyanti vṛthivīṃ punarandhrāngamiṣyati kaṇvāyanamathoddhṛtya suśarmāṇaṃ prasahya tam  BndP siṃdhuko hyandhrajātīyaḥ prāpsyatīmāṃ vasuṃdharām trayoviṃśatsamā rājā siṃdhuko bhavitā tvatha  BndP kṛṣṇo bhrātāsya varṣāṇi so smāddaśa bhaviṣyati śrīśāntakarṇirbhavitā tasya putrastu vai mahān  BndP pañcāśattu samāḥ ṣaṭ ca śāntakarṇir bhaviṣyati āpolavodvādaśa vai tasya putro bhaviṣyati  BndP caturviṃśattu varṣāṇi paṭumāṃśca bhaviṣyati bhavitāniṣṭakarmā tu varṣāṇāṃ pañcaviṃśatim  BndP tataḥ saṃvatsaraṃ pūrṇaṃ hālo rājā bhaviṣyati pañcapattallako nāma bhaviṣyati mahābalaḥ  BndP bhāvyaḥpurīṣabhīrustu samāḥ so pyekaviṃśatim śātakarṇirvarṣamekaṃ bhaviṣyati narādhipaḥ  BndP aṣṭaviṃśativarṣāṇi śivasvātirbhaviṣyati rājā ca gautamī putra ekaviṃśatsamā nṛpaḥ  BndP ekonaviṃśati rājā yajñaḥ śrīśātakarṇyatha ṣaḍeva bhavitā tsamādvijayastu samānṛpaḥ  BndP deḍaśrīśātakarṇī ca tasya putraḥ samāstrayaḥ pulomāriḥ samāḥ sapta tataścaiṣāṃ bhaviṣyati  BndP ityete vai nṛpāstriṃśadandhrā bhokṣyanti vai mahīm samāḥ śatāni catvāri pañcāśatṣaṭ tathaiva ca  BndP andhrāṇāṃ saṃsthitāḥ pañca teṣāṃ vaṃśyāśca ye punaḥ saptaiva tu bhaviṣyanti daśābhīrāstato nṛpāḥ  BndP sapta gardabhinaścāpi tato tha daśa vai śakāḥ yavanāṣṭau bhaviṣyanti tuṣārāstu caturdaśa  BndP trayodaśa guruṇḍāśca maunā hyekādaśaiva tu andhrā bhokṣyanti vasudhāṃ śate dve ca śatañca vai  BndP saptaṣaṣṭiṃ ca varṣāṇi daśābhīrāstato nṛpāḥ sapta gardabhinaścaiva bhokṣyantīmāṃ dvisaptatim  BndP śatāni trīṇyaśītiṃ ca bhokṣyanti vasudhāṃ śakāḥ āśītī dve ca varṣāṇi bhoktāro yavanā mahīm  BndP pañcavarṣaśatānīha tuṣārāṇāṃ mahī smṛtā śatānyarddhacaturthāni bhavitārastrayodaśa  BndP guruṇḍā vṛṣalaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhokṣyante mlecchajātayaḥ śatāni trīṇi bhokṣyante maunā ekādaśaiva tu  BndP teṣu cchinneṣu kālena tataḥ kilakilo nṛpaḥ tataḥ kilakilebhyaśca vindhyaśaktirbhaviṣyati  BndP samāḥ ṣaṇṇavatiṃ caiva pṛthivīṃ tu sameṣyati nṛpānvaidiśakāṃścātha bhaviṣyāṃstu nibodhata  BndP śeṣasya nāgarājasya putraḥ sura purañjayaḥ bhogī bhaviṣyate rājā nṛpo nāgakulodvahaḥ  BndP sadācandrastu candrāśurdvitīyo nakhavāṃstathā dhanadharmā tataścāpi caturtho vaṃśajaḥ smṛtaḥ  BndP bhūtinandastataścāpi vaidiśe tu bhaviṣyati tasya bhrātā yavīyāṃstu nāmnā nandiyaśāḥ kila  BndP tasyānvayo bhaviṣyanti rājānaste trayastu vai daihitraḥ śiśiko nāma pūrikāyāṃ nṛpo bhavat  BndP vindhyaśaktisutaścāpi pravīro nāma vīryavān bhokṣyate ca samāḥ ṣaṣṭiṃ purīṃ kāñcanakāṃ ca vai  BndP yakṣyate vājapeyaiśca samāptavaradakṣiṇaiḥ tasya putrāstu catvāro bhaviṣyanti narādhipāḥ  BndP vindhyakānāṃ kulānāṃ te nṛpā vaivāhikāstrayaḥ supratīko gabhīraśca samā bhokṣyati viṃśatim  BndP śaṅkamāno bhavadrājā mahiṣīṇāṃ mahīpatiḥ puṣpamitrā bhaviṣyanti ṣaṭ strimitrāstrayodaśa  BndP mekalāyāṃ nṛpāḥ sapta bhaviṣyanti ca saptatiḥ komalāyāṃ tu rājāno bhaviṣyanti mahābalāḥ  BndP meghā iti samākhyātā buddhimanto navaiva tu naiṣadhāḥ pārthivāḥ sarve bhaviṣyantyāmanukṣayāt  BndP nalavaṃśaprasūtāste vīryavanto mahābalāḥ magadhānāṃ mahāvīryo viśvasphāṇirbhaviṣyati  BndP utsādya pārthivānsarvānso nyānvarṇānkariṣyati kaivarttānmadrakāṃśceva pulindānbrāhmaṇāṃstathā  BndP sthāpayiṣyanti gajāno nānādeśeṣu te janān viśvasphāṇirmahāsattvo yuddhe viṣṇusamaprabhaḥ  BndP viśvasphāṇirnarapatiḥ klībākṛtirivocyate utsādayitvā kṣatraṃ tu kṣatramanyatkariṣyati  BndP nava nāgāstu bhokṣyati purīṃ caṃpāvatīṃ nṛpāḥ mathurāṃ ca purā ramyāṃ nāgā bhokṣyanti sapta vai  BndP anugaṅgāprayāgaṃ ca sāketaṃ magadhāṃstathā etāñjanapadānsarvānbhokṣyante saptavaṃśajāḥ  BndP naiṣa dhānya dukāṃścaiva śaiśītān kālatoyakān etāñjanapadānsarvānbhokṣyante maṇidhānyajān  BndP kośalāṃścāndhrapaiṇḍrāṃśca tāmraliptānsasāgarān caṃpāṃ caiva purīṃ ramyāṃ bhokṣyante devarakṣitāḥ  BndP kaliṅgā mahiṣāścaiva mahendranilayāśca ye etāñjanapadānsarvān pālayiṣyati vai guhaḥ  BndP strīrāṣṭrabhojakāṃścaiva bhokṣyate kanakāhvayaḥ tulyakālaṃ bhaviṣyanti sarve hyate mahīkṣitaḥ  BndP alpaprasādā hyanṛtā mahākrodhā hyadhārmikāḥ bhaviṣyantīha yavanā dharmataḥ kāmatorthataḥ  BndP naiva mūrddhābhiṣiktāste bhaviṣyanti narādhipāḥ yugadoṣadurācārā bhaviṣyanti nṛpāstu te  BndP bhaviṣyantīha payāye kālena vṛthivīkṣitaḥ vihīnāstu bhaviṣyanti dharmataḥ kāma torthataḥ  BndP tairvimiśrā janapadā mlecchācārāśca sarvaśaḥ viparyayeṇa vartante nāśāyiṣyanti vai prajāḥ  BndP lubdhā anṛtavācaśca bhavitārastadā nṛpāḥ teṣāṃ varttati paryāye bahustrīke yuge tadā  BndP lavāllavaṃ bhraśyamānā āyurūpabalaśrutaiḥ tathā gatāsu vai kāṣṭhaṃ prajāsu jagatīśvarāḥ  BndP rājānaḥ saṃpraṇaśyati kālenopahatāstadā kalkinā vyāhatāḥ sarve mlecchā yāsyanti saṃkṣayam  BndP adhārmikāśca ye tyarthaṃ pākhaṇḍāścaiva sarvaśaḥ pranaṣṭe nṛpaśabde ca saṃdhyāśiṣṭe kalau yuge  BndP kiñcicchiṣṭāḥ prajāstā vai dharme naṣṭe parigrahāḥ asādhanā hatasvāśca vyādhiśokanipīḍitāḥ  BndP anāvṛṣṭihatāścaiva parasparavadhena ca  BndP anādhārāḥ paritrastā vārtāmutsṛjya duḥkhitāḥ tyaktvā purāṇi grāmāṃśca bhaviṣyanti vanaukasaḥ  BndP evaṃrūpeṣu naṣṭeṣu prajāstyaktvā gṛhāṇi tu naṣṭe snehe durāpannā bhraṣṭasnehāḥ suhṛjjanaḥ  BndP varṇāśramaparibhraṣṭāḥ saṃkaraṃ ghoramāsthitāḥ saritparvatasevinyo bhaviṣyanti prajāstadā  BndP saritaḥ sāgarānūpānsevante parvatānatha aṅgānkaliṅgānvaṅgāṃśca kāśmīrānkāśikośalān  BndP ṛṣikāntāgiridroṇīḥ saṃśrayiṣyanti mānavāḥ kṛtsnaṃ himavataḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ kūlaṃ ca lavaṇāṃbhasaḥ  BndP araṇyamabhipatsyante āryā mlecchajanaiḥ saha mṛgairmīnairvihaṅgaiśca śvāpadaiścekṣubhistathā  BndP madhuśākaphalairmūlairvartayiṣyanti mānavāḥ cīraṃ parṇaṃ ca vividhaṃ valkalānyajināni ca  BndP svayaṃ kṛtvā pidhāsyanti yathā munijanastathā bījānnāni tathā nimneṣvī hantaḥ kāṣṭhaśaṅkubhiḥ  BndP ajaiḍakaṃ kharoṣṭraṃ ca pālayiṣyanti yatnataḥ nadīrvatsyanti toyārthe nūnamāśritya mānavāḥ  BndP pārthivā vyavahāreṇa vibādhante parasparam bahumanyāḥ prajāhīnāḥ śaucācāravivarjitāḥ  BndP evaṃ bhaviṣyanti narāstadādharma vyavasthitāḥ hīnāndīnāṃstathādharmānprajā samanuvartsyati  BndP āyustadā trayoviṃśanna kaścidativartate durbalā viṣayaglānā jarāyā saṃpariplutāḥ  BndP patramūlaphalāhārāścīrakṛṣṇājināṃbarāḥ vṛttyarthamabhilipsyantaścariṣyanti vasuṃdharām  BndP etatkālamanuprāptāḥ prajāḥ kaliyugāntake kṣīṇe kaliyuge tasmindivye varṣasahasrake  BndP niḥśeṣāstu bhaviṣyanti sārddhaṃ kaliyugena tu sa saṃdhyāṃśe tu niḥśeṣe kṛtaṃ vai pratipatsyate  BndP yadā yandraśca sūryaśca tathā tiṣyabṛhaspatī ekarāśau bhaviṣyanti tadā kṛtayugaṃ bhavet  BndP eṣa vaṃśakramaḥ kṛtsnaḥ kīrtito vo yathākramam atītā vartamānāśca tathaivānāgatāśca ye  BndP mahānandābhiṣekānta janma yāvatparīkṣitaḥ etadvarṣasahasraṃ tu jñeyaṃ pañcāśaduttaram  BndP pramāṇaṃ vai tathā vaktuṃ mahāpadmottaraṃ ca yat antaraṃ ca śatānyaṣṭau ṣaṭtriṃśacca samāḥ smṛtāḥ  BndP etatkālāntara bhāvyamandhrāntādyāḥ prakīrttitāḥ bhaviṣyaistatra saṃkhyātāḥ purāṇajñaiḥ śrutārṣibhiḥ  BndP saptarṣayastadā prāptāḥ pitrye pārīkṣite śatam saptaviṃśaiḥ śatairbhāvyā andhrāṇāṃ te nvayāḥ punaḥ  BndP saptaviṃśatiparyante kṛtsne nakṣatramaṇḍale saptarṣayastu tiṣṭhanti paryāyeṇa śataṃśatam  BndP saptarṣīṇāṃ yugaṃ tvetaddivyayā saṃkhyayā smṛtam māsā divyāḥ smṛtāḥ ṣaṭca divyābdāścaiva sapta hi  BndP tebhyaḥ pravartate kālo divyaḥ saptarṣibhistu taiḥ saptarṣīṇāṃ tu yau pūrvau dṛśyete uttarādiśi  BndP tayormadhye ca nakṣatraṃ dṛśyate yatsamaṃ divi tena saptarṣayo yuktā jñeyā vyomni śataṃ samāḥ  BndP nakṣatrāṇāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca bhogasyaitannidarśanam saptarṣayo hyathāyuktāḥ kāle parīkṣite śatam  BndP andhrāṃśe sacaturviṃśe bhaviṣyanti śataṃ samāḥ imāstadā tu prakṛtīrvyāpatsyante prajā bhṛśam  BndP anṛtopahatāḥ sarvā dharmataḥ kāmatorthataḥ śrautasmārtte praśithile dharme varṇāśrame tadā  BndP saṃkaraṃ durbalātmānaḥ pratiyāsyanti mohitāḥ saṃsaktāśca bhaviṣyanti śūdrāḥ sārddhaṃ dvijātibhiḥ  BndP brāhmaṇāḥ śūdrayaṣṭāraḥ śūdrā vai mantrayonayaḥ upasthāsyanti tānviprāṃstadā daurvṛttyalipsavaḥ  BndP lavāllavaṃ bhraśyamānāḥ prajāḥ sarvāḥ krameṇa tu kṣayameva gamiṣyanti kṣīṇaśeṣā yugakṣaye  BndP yasminkṛṣṇo divyaṃ yātasta sminneva tadā dine pratipannaḥ kaliyugastasya saṃkhyāṃ nibodhata  BndP sahasrāṇāṃ śatānīha trīṇi mānuṣasaṃkhyayā ṣaṣṭiṃ caiva sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ tūcyate kaliḥ  BndP divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu tatsaṃdhyāṃśe hi kīrtite niḥśeṣe ca tadā tasminkṛtaṃ vai pratipatsyate  BndP elaścekṣvākuvaṃśaśca saha bhedaiḥ prakīrtitau ikṣvākostu samṛtaṃ kṣattraṃ sumitrāntaṃ vivasvataḥ  BndP ailaṃ kṣattraṃ kṣemakāntaṃ soma vaṃśavido viduḥ ete vivasvataḥ putrāḥ kīrtitāḥ kīrttivarddhanāḥ  BndP atītā vartamānāśca tathaivānāgatāśca ye brāhmaṇāḥ kṣattriyā vaiśyaḥ śūdrāścaivātra ye smṛtāḥ  BndP yugeyuge mahātmānaḥ samatītāḥ sahasraśaḥ bahutvānnāmadheyānāṃ parisaṃkhyā kulekule  BndP punaruktibahutvācca na mayā parikīrttitā vaivasvataṃtare hyasminna nimivaṃśaḥ samāpyate  BndP etasyāṃ tu yugākhyāyāṃ yataḥ kṣattraṃ prapatsyate tathā hi kathayiṣyāmi gadato me nibodhata  BndP devāpiḥ pauravo rājā aikṣvākuścaiva yo maruḥ māhāyogabalopetau kalāpagrāmamāsthitau  BndP etau kṣattrapraṇetārau caturviṃśe caturyuge suvarcā nāma putrastu ikṣvākostu bhaviṣyati  BndP navaviṃśe yuge so tha vaṃśasyādirbhaviṣyati devāpeśca sapaulastu elādirbhavitā nṛpaḥ  BndP kṣatrapravarttakau hyetau bhaviṣyete caturyuge evaṃ sarvatra vijñeyaṃ saṃtānārthe tu latraṇam  BndP kṣīṇe kaliyuge tasminbhaviṣye ta kṛte yuge saptarṣibhistu taiḥ sārddhamādye tretāyuge punaḥ  BndP gotrāṇāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ ca bhaviṣyete pravarttakau dvāparāṃśena tiṣṭhanti kṣatriyā ṛṣibhiḥ saha  BndP bhaviṣye tu tataḥ sarge kāle kṛtayuge punaḥ bījārthaṃ te bhaviṣyanti brahmakṣatrasya vai punaḥ  BndP evameva tu sarveṣu tiṣṭhantīhāsureṣu vai saptarṣayo nṛpaiḥ sārddhaṃ saṃtānārthaṃ yugeyuge  BndP kṣatrasyaiva samucchedasaṃbandho vai dvijaiḥ smṛtaḥ manvantarāṇāṃ saptānāṃ saṃtānaśca śrutaśca te  BndP parasparādyugānāṃ ca brahmakṣatrasya codbhavaḥ yathā pravṛttisteṣāṃ vai pravṛttānāṃ tathā kṣayaḥ  BndP saptarṣayo vidusteṣāṃ dīrghāyuṣṭvādbhavābhavau etena kramayogena ailekṣvākvanvayā dvijāḥ  BndP utpadyamānāstretāyāṃ kṣīyamāṇāḥ kalau punaḥ anuyānti yugākhyāṃ tu yāvanmanvantarakṣayaḥ  BndP jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa kṣatre niravaśeṣite kṛteyaṃ saṃkulā sarvā kṣatriyairvasudhādhipaiḥ  BndP dvipaṃśakāraṇañcaiva kīrtayiṣye nibodhata ailasyekṣvākunandasya prakṛtiḥ parivarttate  BndP rājānaḥ śreṇibaddhāstu tathānye kṣatriyā nṛpāḥ elavaṃśasya ye khyātāstathaivekṣvākavo nṛpāḥ  BndP teṣāmekaśataṃ pūrṇaṃ kulānāmabhiṣekitam tāvadeva tu bhojānāṃ vistaro dviguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ  BndP bhajate tryaṃśakaṃ kṣattraṃ caturthātta dyathā diśam teṣvatītāḥ samānā ye bruvatastānnibodhata  BndP śataṃ vai prativindhyānāṃ śataṃ nāgāḥ sahaihayāḥ dhṛta rāṣṭraścaikaśatamaśītirjanamejayāḥ  BndP śataṃ ca brahmadattānāṃ śāriṇāṃ viriṇāṃ śatam tataḥ śataṃ tu paulānāṃ śvetakāśya kuśādayaḥ  BndP tato pare sahasraṃ vai ye tītāḥ śaśavindavaḥ ījire cāśvamedhaiste sarve niyutadakṣiṇaiḥ  BndP evaṃ rājarṣayo tītā śataśo tha sahasraśaḥ manorvaivasvatasyāsminvarttamāneṃtare tu ye  BndP teṣāṃ nibodhatotpannā loke saṃtatayaḥ smṛtāḥ na śakyevistarastāsāṃ saṃtatīnāṃ parasparam  BndP tatpūrvāparayogena vaktuṃ varṣaśatairapi aṣṭāviṃśadyugākhyāstu gatā vaivasvatentare  BndP etai rājarṣibhiḥ sārddhaṃ śaṣṭāyāstā nibodhata catvāriṃśattrayaścaiva bhaviṣyāḥ saha rājabhiḥ  BndP yugākhyānāva śiṣṭāstu tato vaivasvatakṣayaḥ etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarve samāsavyāsayogataḥ  BndP punaruktibahutvācca na śakya tu yugaiḥ saha ete yayātiputrāṇāṃ pañca vaṃśā viśāṃ hitāḥ  BndP kīrttitāśca vyatītā ye ye lokāndhārayantyuta labhate ca varānpañca durlabhā niha laukikān  BndP āyuḥ kīrttiṃ dhanaṃ putrānsvargaṃ cānantyamaśnute dhāraṇācchravaṇāccaiva pañcavaṃśasya dhīmataḥ  BndP ityeṣa vo mayā pādastṛtīyaḥ kathito dvijāḥ vistareṇānupūrvyā ca kiṃ bhūyo varṇayāmyaham  BndP iti śrībrahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte madhyamabhāge tṛtīya upoddhātapāde vaṃśānuvarṇanaṃ nāma catuḥsaptatitamo dhyāyaḥ  samāptaścāyaṃ tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ
